vther quham salit licianis stout quhilom fallowis king pandoure orontes eneas fallow dere ene hastelye north wynd ane hidduous sey schippit hi sterne behynd smat furth skippare clepit lewcaspis hede doun warppit schip thryis thare flude quhirlit round sowkand swelth sanke vnder sey dround huge deip saland dyd appere troanis armure tabillis vther gere flet wallis strang barge tho bare ilieoneus sche bare also forcy achates sche bare aba sche quhar antient alethes storme ouerset raif rebbis syde semes thay lekkit salt wattir stremes fast bullerand euery rift bore mene quhile mony rowt rore sey thus trublit tempest furth sent felt neptune wattir moueth schent deip furth yett schaldis thare gretly commouit sey stare plesand hede rasit hiest wall lukand behaldis se ouer eneas nauy shatterit fer sounder fludis ouer set troianis vnder flaggis rane heuin discend iunois dissait ire full well kend callit eurus zepherus eistand west wyndisby neptunus oracione tempest cesed said thus ye sa greitlye assurit hie kin ye wyndis quod durst leif begin baith erde aire moue manere eik se sa stout stormes stere fall chaistice bot behuffis first mei mocioun fludis thaym appese traist weile vnpunyst ye sall astert one sic ane wise gif ye falt efterwart withdraw hen kyng say ye na power aucthoryty sepis thre granit sceptour wand quhilk cut geuin bere hand hald craggis amang rochis hie thare dwelling place eurus quod bid eolus keip hald conding clois presoun wyndis thar ring thus said wyth wourde hastely swelland seyis swageit fra sky gadderit cluddis chaissit sone away brocht hame son agane bricht day dochter tymothie son tri enforsis troiane schippis anon rais lift scharp rokkis blynd god self hesing behind big scepture hauand granys thre oppynnys schald sandis temperis wele se ouer slidand lichtlie croppis wallis ye se ofta discripcion sedicion comme people amang commonus fallis striffe debate wod fuliche ire fleis stanys brandis fire thair greif furye ministeris wappynnys plente bot percace gif behald se sum man grete auctorite effers thay ceise still standand giffis eris wourdisthe frute eloquece slaik thair mynd swage samyn wyse fell seis rage p eneas affrik aryue thare wyth schote slew vii dartis beliue fader fludis neptune sic wyse behaldin see aboue vnder stabillit heuin mouit chare slakking renyeis prosper cours fare eneas feris strand wery forwrocht sped nerrest land coist libia arriuit hauyn place lang hals entre thair within ane ile inuironit athir part brek storme wallis euery art within wattir ane bosum gais bayth thare standis large craggis brais se hewis athir hand wounder hicht semes pingill heuin vnder ane braid sand souir fra wyndys blawis flowis schore depe euer stabill ony wawis ane wod aboue ourheildis braid bewis castis ane plesand sch dow ouer clewis rycht ouerforgane forrett bra vndir hingand rokkis alsua ane coif tharin resche wattir spryngand seatis stane neuir hewin mennis hand bot wrocht nature ane hous bene nymphes goddis fludis woddis grene perbrekit schyppis bot cabillis thare mycht ryde nane anker nedis make thame arreist bide nauy thiddir eneas brocht bot seuin schyppys gret desire thocht ground troyanis sped land thay desirit set softlye sand thare lichtis lymys salt wattir dyit strekit coist spred furthbekit dryit bot first achates slew fyre flynt kepit dry leuis tunder quhil thay brynt syne stikkis dry kyndill thare layd quhill flame bleis fyre vpbradis quhete fludis chauft wete instrumentis purge swith sete skant vittale cornes quernis stane thay grand syne beuke fyre ilkane mene quhyle eneas banke hie clummyn wyde quhare behaldand large sie gyf ony schyp tharon micht persauit quhilk late windis e dis iueth ane prince haue care people self bewauit ony troiane galay back barge antheus capis caitus stramaris large waiffand schewand fra thare top hicht na schip saw bot sone gat ane sicht thre hartis wauerand coistis side quham bak throw grauis wyde mekle herdis followit ane rout pasturit large vale thare stintis hynt bow hand swift fleand arrowis fast berand traist achates first ledaris thre quhilk thare hedis bare thare tyndis hie smartlie slew syne rin gald persewis grundin arrowis amang thik wod bewis stintis dartis bete quhil grind brocht seuin hartis gret schippis thare nowmer equale made syne heuin sped without abade thame distribute amang feris wine thare veschell grete small quhilk gaif acestes rial hoist departing cecilly coist thame birlis skynkis fast sic wordis comfortis thare drery chere ye ferisa constant orison eneas full consolation wyth nobyl vayeant prynce exhortes deir freyndis quod bywent perrellis ignorant ben ye haue susteni greter dangeris vnkend like hereof god sall make sone ane end rage silla huge swefte se ye haue eschapit passit eik haue ye euer routand caribdis rokkis fell craggis quhare monstruous cyclops dwell ye expert pluk vp hart aduersite pray dolorus drede expell away sum tyme hereon think may help perchance diuers casis sere parrellis sufferance vnto itaill ettill quhare destanye schap v ane rest quietharbrye predestinatis thare troye sall ryse agane stout prosper fortoun remane si plesand wordes carpand forth brocht sett mynd troublit mony greuous thocht fenyet confort chere outwart dolorus paine hid depe grauin hart feris pray ressauit raith thare meat addressis graith hynt hydis made boukis bare rent furth entrellis sum tailyeis schare syne brocht flikerand sum gobbetis lyre kest caldron vthir sum bet fyre thame refresch thus coist lenth sped thame fude recouir thare strenth grene gers sat doun fillit tham syne fat venison nobill ald wyne quhen huger thus meatis chasit away dischis drawin lang lang sermon thay bewalit thair feris losit flude betuix gude hope drede doute stude quhither thay war lewad tholit extreme dede al thay ansuerit set thay oft plene cal bot pryncipale petyfull eneas regrettis oft hard fortun case sterne orontes drownyt se amytus harme complenis allone cruell fate licus strang gyane stalwart cloanthus iowe beheld large coistis fer venus carpit iupyter gone day thar lang sermon quhan iupiter hie spere adoun blent saleryfe seyis erth tharby pepyl dwelling coistes fer sindry heich heuyns top baid houerand libie beheld graithly land within breist diuers curis thus musis thinkis vnto spak venus dolorus hir ene full brycht teris quod sche quhilk gouernis reulis steris baith goddis men enu oration iupiter thyne eterne impire oft affrayis thundir wylde fyre mycht myne enee sa gretly offend quhat mycht troianis trespas quhilk end ar brocht sufferit sa feil cors laid deid throw warld debarrit euery stede dreuine itale thow hecht sum tyme perfay thame schuld cum eftir mony ane day worthy romani troianis spryng princis power ouer sey land ring quhat wikkit counsel fader he turnyt thy thocht forsoyth troyis distructioun mocht tuke comfort herof thinkand baid hard wanwerd suld follow fortune glaid bot yit perchaunce persewis sare sundry danger cachit thare thare trauell quhat end grantis thou gret kyng sen anthenor mycht throw myd oistes thring grekis peirs soundis iliria souerlye pa strait regiouns alsua liburnanis ouer tymauy flude qhare nyne monthis rinnand thay war hill resoundes sa rudely doi rout like ane sey betis brayis thare netheles padwa ciete ane duelling place troianis biggit nemmyt pepill ful yore armes oft oy he set vp memore thy blud thi kinrent spring quham heum thow grantit ane place ring schame say throw feyd ane losit oure schippis ar betrasit ilk ane fer italie bene haldin eik reward ganand ar meik honour done bene godlik restoris thou thus sic wyse kinrik smyling sum deil faderof goddis men ilk sueit wisageiuppite confortes venus wyth log narration ken mesis tempestis makis heuins clere first kissit child syne said manere away sic dredeshowes hystory eneas emperour augustus time cytherea efferd thi lynnage vnchangeit remanis weir thou desyris ciete sal thow se lauyne promyst wallis hie eik sell thou raise aboue sterrit say manfull eneas deify sentence alterid thow traistis bot sall schaw sen sic tho htis thristis declare destanyis secrete full mony yeris tofore thay bene compleit eneas wyth hydduous barganyng itale thrawart pepill sall doun thring syne eftir statute lawis thay men beild townis wall cieteis quhen thre someris latin itale winteris ringin hale fra time retulianis bene subduit fecht yong child quhilk astaneus heicht surname clepit iulus sans fale ilion blude riall quhill troye ilion stude ring thre ty lang twelf monthis rowing ouer salbe king lauyne realme sate translatit alsua fortely wal cete lang alba thare sall thre hunder yeris giddir remane ring vnder pepill hettoriane quhill ilium nun dochter ane king consauit mar tua twinnis doith furth bryng glitterand volf skyn ouer array cled nuris talbart glad gay romulus sall pepill ressaue weild mare wallis rome sall beild eftir name call pepill romani folkis ful lang rul remams nothir termis space boundis senyeorye nane sett thame grant haue perpetuale empire end lest apersmar iuno gret vnrest cummeris erd se quod sall turne hir mind bettir wise foster romani lorde erdlye gere latine pepill kep baith pece determit likis goddis wy efter mony lusteris yeris ouers ddm tyme sall cum quhen auchises spring realme perthia bondagesall doun thring eik myte subdew regioun large vnder thare lordschip dant grece arge cesar novill troyane blud borne salbe quhilk sal empire dilate octiane se sterne vpspring sall fame iulus takyne name iulus thy neuo great kyng prince discend blude ofspring quhan eftir souir thine entent charge spulye orient amang nowmer goddis ressaue thou sall ane god men sall clepe call cruel tyme sone efter sall ceis weris stance sall rest peice antiant faith vailyeand knychthede chast religioun sall lawis leid dreidful portis sallbe schet faill ianus tempill takynnar battell hard irne bandis claspit fast cage wik kit bargane thare furius rage set apoun greisly armoure sete ane hundreth brassin chenyeis grete behynd bak hard bundin handis tua horryble tyrrant bludy mouth sal bra bcand said iupiter full euyn son mercury send doun heuyn cartage baith realme new ciete luge troianis sall reddy le dido destany mysknawand wald thame expell boundis hir land gret fardis windis flaw throw sky cuntre libie cum hye thare charge folk cartage thair feirs mudis hartis canassuage plesure god quhilk thame tauch first vthir quene hir selfhes caucht towart troians ane full freyndlie mynd vnto thame bousum kynd enee morowe thorow schaw met hys moder habit vnknaw bot reuthfull eneas mynd many thinges compas beliue halesum day wox lich dressit furth spy haue ane sicht new placis till ceirs knaw quhatkin coistis wind wes blaw quha thaym inhabit quhidder wilde bestes men semyt wildernes fand schupe feris schaw nauy derne amang thik wod schaw vnder neth hingand holkit rochis hie dekkit mony semely tre quhais schaddois dirk hid weile schippis flkane bot ane fallow furth gane traist achates atheris hand yfere braid steile heid schuke hunting sper amid wod mother met tuay semand ane made vissage array wappinnis like virginis spartha stowt wensche trace harpalita haistand hors hir fadder reskewe spediar hebroun swift flude persew venus efter gy maner thare ane actiue bow apoun hir schulder bare sche bene ane wilde huntreis wind waffing hir haris lowsit trace hir skirt kiltit till hir bare knee first vthir vnto thus speike sche howethe commonyng betwixe eneas hys mother say youngkeris saw ye walkand auenture ony sistiris dere cais arrowis cauchit hir syde cled spo tit en wh dyd knaw linkis hyde loud cry folow chace efter fomy bare thare solace thus said venus hir son agane answeris said treuly maid plane nane thy sisteris se bot thou virgine sall call thy visage semi na mortall creature voce soundis lyk humane nature ane goddis art thou soythly sycht quhiddir thou diane phebus sister brycht sum goddis thyr nymphyis kynd maistres woddis beis v happy kynd releif lang trauell quhat euer thow vnder quhat art heuin hie quhat coist warld finaly sal arriue thow teich v men land vnknaw driue wy wind storme sey cathit hiddirtyll mony fare sacrifice offerand thine alter sall de richt hand venus ansuerit dedeinye ressaue sic honour certis quhilk feris haue madinis tyre gise bere ane case arrowis wyse rede botynis thare schankis hie realme punis quhilk ye se pepill tire cite belt fra folk discend agenore ye bene marchis libie sans fale inhabit pepill vndantabill battell quhare dido quene reulis empyre hidder hirbreder fled realme tyre lang war iniuris doutis lang tald bot vmast mater sal hald ane husband quhilk sicheus hecht sayd sche richest ground phenice strangly louit sylly dido hir mater maner scho chance sche clene virginite weddit tyre cuntre heritage held pigmalioun brother wikkitnes cruell aboue al vther quhilk offence occasioun greif blynd couatyse gold throw mische altare slely ane knyfe wer reft sicheus lyfe mouit piete vnto sister sure conselit cruell dede lang vndercure fals man dissaitfull wordis fare wanhope trumpet wofull luffare bot hir husband bygrauit ymage hir apperis slepe pale visage meruellus wyfe lenth declare cruelly slane altare schew knyfe throw breist threst hid crime hir hous manifest syne grete haist exhortis hir fle leif hir natiue land tak se help hir outwart way vnder crd quhare auld hurdis hid lay siluer gold reuelit ane large wecht yrat como ult hecht hir departing followschip redy made togidder conuenis ony langare abade thay hatis cruell tyranni dedis yit feloun violence sare dredis schippis cace war reddy thare thay tuke chargit ful gold mare tressoure wrechit pigmalioun thus caryit ouer sey anone ane woman captane deide yone place ar thay cumyn thow may take hede quhare risis yone large wallis stout new cartage hie towris al meikle grund thay bocht first tyde thay mycht cumpas bullis hyde younder cheif castell standing bray thare langage lepit barsay deid name beris witnes yit bot quhat ye finalie wald wit quhat cuntre cumin passe wald quhare sche sperand eneas sichand sare voce drawand deip fra breist within said thou goddes gif suld begyn tell labor formest end story fet thou mycht attend maid end vesper eum sterne brycht suld clois heuin end dayis licht ancient troy gif euer ye name troy hard cuntre caryit throw diuers seys alsua fortoun coist libia dreuyn tempest reuthful eneas troiane goddis cursis nauy quham fra amyd enomies rent fame knawin aboue element seik itale natiue countre sere linnage cummis fra hiest iupyter schyppis twis ten phrigiane sey moder ane goddis teichand way toke fellowand destany quhilk grant slote wynd wallis stant seuin euill perbrekit saif remanis vnkend mysterfull deseirtis libie wander expellit ewrop asia venus na mare suffrit plene sa amyd dolour plantis thus spak sche quhat euer thou art traist wel tho fauorit goddis drauis halesumare quhilk sprete lyfe thy weilfare sen thow art cummyn cartage ciete hald thy way que entre present thy self schaw certane thy feres ar saif thy nauy cummin agane fayf brocht fre northwyndis al le parentis taucht spaying craft fals behald tuelf swannis randoune glaid fa quham newlie regioun iouis foul egill discending hicht sare affrait amyd skyis brycht lang range licht thay bene addrest spyis erth quhar thay sall rest thay returne thar weyngis southand iolely ther cours cirkill sky cryand singand eftir thar awin gyse schippis fallowschip samyn wyfe ar harbryit hauin iwys bent saill enteris port thys pa thy way euin furth samyn went thus sayd sche turnand incontinent hirnek schane like vnto rose may hir heuinly haris glitterand bricht gay kest hir forehede ane smell glorious sue hir habit fell doune coueryng hir feit hir passage ane verray god hir kyith fra kneweneas knawi mo moder alswith sic wourdis followis sche fle quhy art thou cruell thy sonne quod disceuand sa oft fals sembland quhy grantis thow micht ione hand hand rander wotis trew thus repreuis bot sche went adew ciete haldis furth way bot venus ane sop myst baith tway ane dirk cloud closit round na man suld thame se twch dout na wayis stop elli dere yit causis chare cumming spere hir self vp lyft paphum past swyith vesy hir resting place ioly blyith thare hir tempill cipirland quharin thare doi ane hundreth altaris stand hait burning full saba sence houri ane smelland swete wyth fresch garlad flouris eneas hys moderis commaundemet led mysty cloud cartage went mene time hastit furth thare way rode led thame quhill ascend ar thay hill far risand abane toun hicht quhare al cietie forgaue thame se thay mycht eneas wounderit gretnes cartage quhilk late fore bene ane small cotage fare portis alsua ferlyt fast brute pepill tharat past large stretis pathit bissy tyrianis laborand ardently ane part haistis beild wallis wycht sum rais grete castell hicht velt vp stanis volt hie sum grathis first thak rufe tre sum deluis fousy depe sum chesis officiaris lawes keip councellouris senatouris wise folkis younder vthir sum new heum holkis also ane end fast layis foundament theatry vtheris eik huge pillaris grete querillis gan hew bete till odorne place degre time cuming quhare grete triumph suld like beis feilda copariso flurist new gaddering thare werk many diuers hew soft somer bricht son hait schynyng quhen thare kynd thame list swarmis bryng kames incluse thare hony clene swete liquour stuffis thare cellis schene ressauis birdingis vthir thair rout fra thare hyff togiddir ane rout expellis bowbert best fenyt drone thare laubor besy feruent se hony smellis swete tyme seid quod enee full happy ye deid quhais large wallis risis thus hie quhill vesyit boundis ciete ane wounder thing couerit ane cloud enteris syne amyd thikest rout amang men thrang nane saw amyd ciete stode ane semele schaw maist plesand sobir schadow quhar punicianis first vpwrapit war eftir stormy blastis seis rage thay delfand fand takynnare cariage ane mekill hors heid wene iuno schaw fore goddis quene signifyit ciete excellent battell plentuous eik tymes vittale ilk place sidones dido begouth big ane proud tempill iuno drouryis sere giftis rich eik golden statew goddes entre rais hir stagis bra bra also cuplis fessynit brasin duris iarris marbill hyrst tempill sere nouelteis fyrst schawin till eneas mesit gretely fere first assurance comfort hope releif efter aduersite went diuers thingis se rowming large tempill schene abide cuming quene ciete grete prosperite mony werk n thare castis fle dew proporcioun wounderit ioy saw per ordoure al sege troy famus battellis vulgate throw warld king priame athir dis baldare thame baith fers achil styntis wepand sayd achates tyll quhilk place mi frendis quod quhat regioun erd may fundin quhare misfortoun fully proclame ala behald se younder king pryame lo worschyp halden memore thir lamentabill takinnis past oure mortall myndis aucht compassioun stere away drede take na langare fere quhat wenis thou na fame sall gude thus said fed hys mynd quhare stude plesand feny ymagerie murnand sair wepand tendirlie flude teriseneas lamentacion quhen remembris natyue countre haling ouer face lukit werk percace saw porturit quhare sic ane place grekis fled troianis followis chace wallis troy thay ficht younder part troianis takis flycht creist hede achilles chare persewand stranglie fer then saw quhare quhite tentis king resus euill kepe betraisit war apoun first sleipe quhare grete slauchter bludy diomede distroyit tent lede mylk quhite hors fers swift gude euir thay taistit ony troiane fude drunken flude exhantus yonuder lo beheld troylus wanting armoure fey barne eand recounter achilles vnganand hors hym harland behynd void carte hingand wyde opin hede doun warte suppos held reyneis fast faile neck haris erd traile spere ouerturnit dust write samyn tyme troianis madynnes quhite hare doun skalit sorowfull pa vnto tempil greuit pallas ask supple thaym ane wympill bare thay handis betand thair breistis way fremyt goddis held hir ene fixt fast apoun gound nar blenkis list thaym cast wallis troy saw quhat wyse achilles har lit hectoris body thrys dede corp syne gold saw sell law breist murnand gaif ane yell seand wod carte spulye knycht corp derest freynd sa dycht priame vnharmyt strek furth handis spy achilles sonnis body self alsua midlit persauit amang princis grece melle orient hostis knew one one vulcanus armour blak menon madinis cum fra amasone saw scone crukit scheildis schapin lyke mone led thare furius quene pairthassalye amyd thousand egerly fechtis sche quhar hir pap spere cut away gold thairon belt ane riche tischey ane wourthy weriour soithlie thay micht hir ken wensche stoutlye recounter durst men tempyl cummis quene dido quhare enee feris fand also qvhill manfull troiane eneas se thir nyce figurisquene dido hir tryane u mith church wonderand musit studeand ane stare bot one ane sicht quhar blenkit thare quene dido excellent bewte tempill cummis ane fare menye lusty youngkeris walking hir like goddes diane hir rout endlang flude ewrote bra vnder toppis hir hill cynthia ledand ring dancis quham followis ouer quhare ane thousand nymphis flokand thare hir schulder arrow cace bare sche quhare sche walkis laif hie may wele sene latona hir moder thys geuis reiosing secrete hartis blis sic ane dido sic ane hir blithlie bare amyd thame werkis weilfare prouiding realme tyme cum quhen sche temple dure cum syne enterid vnder hir myd volt tuke hir sete hie ane trone cumpanyis grete athir half standing armyt men dome law pronuncis sche thaym feis thare laubouristhe office prince equalye gart distribute gif dout fallis thare cut cauill plede sone partid bot suddanly persauis eneas quhare grete hast com rynnyng antheus sergest seis stalwart cloanthus diuers vtheris troiane menye quham black storme skarterit ane vthir coist dreuin land fallow awounders seand achates half astonyst stude affray fere ioy smytin bayth war thay langit sair schask handis bot thare hart vncouth care amouit iu sum part dessymill nathyng sene thai dirk cloud hid spy thay bad stude thare feris chancet eft quhat coist thare nauyne thay lef quhat thay desyrit full weill thay saw thare schippis per ordoure thay cum raw beseikand grace peace fast thame thocht tempill grete clamour socht fra thay war enterit temple tho licence grantit thaym speke also gretest oratoureilionius oration quene dido ilioneus plesand voce begouth sermon thus hie prince quham iupiter grant beild ane new ciete dant violence proude folk iust law wretchit troianis windis blaw threw strang stremis mony diuers se forbyd yone cruell fyre besekis suffer nat birn schypwis ane rage haue reuth apoun petuous aldlynage considder freindly mater standis come hidder drawin swerde handis spulye templis rich libia coist na sperich driue awa sic violence nane within myndis sa grete stoutnes vincus folk wy thare ane place quham grekis thay sa vnto name clepis hisperia ane nobill land richt potent batall fructu grund plentuos vittall kyng enocrius inhabit fyrst trow bot dayis lately fame eftir thare duke namid italie thedderwart cours laid quhen suddanlie flude boldynnyt stormy orione amangis blynd bankis cachit v anone bittir blastis contrarious alwayis throw wallis huge salt fame wilsum wayis throw perrellus rolkis v driue hidder coist ar v arryue quhat kind pepill dwellis quod bene sic theuis sufferit cuntre ar defendit herbry sand prouokit eik battall driuen land force storme slike thay v deny albeit scanth men ye set nocht mortall weris contempnis comptis belcuis yet wele haue thocht goddis sall remember traistis baith gude dedis iniquite v kingthe iustice wisdome fortitude temperace eneas wourthye eneas ane iustar man al warld nanc mare reuthfull wyssare wer mare valyeand dedis armes sere quham gif fatis alife conseruit haith tak heuinlie draw braith crewell goistis hid vnder erd thare na drede sall mak v afferd thow sall neuer repent sikkerly schaw v first frendschyp curtesy realme cicill al haue frendes cieties armit men plente troiane blude acestes kyng gif v war leuit flote land bryng wind storme schake grant erk leif hew wod tak tymmer bete airis vther misteris king micht fynd feris blithlie suld hald towart italy coist latin seik hy bot gif weilfare beleif clene gane maist souerane fader v troianis libiane se withhaldis gif thou gone ascaneus comfort remanis none soithly leist cecil se placis reddy fra quham hidder driuen sall seik king acestes thus sayd ilioneus thus ceis bot noyis rais amang troianis thay murmuritthe quenis gentil ansuer ye roians complenit amange fludis grene quhilk saw droun vthir thingis thou knawis conforme vnto thy moderis sawis skarslie thyr wordis spokin quhen cloude thaym swyth brokin vanyst tyte away amange aire vp stude enee clere licht schynyng faire like till ane god body face moder grantit hir son sic grace crisp haris war plesand vnto se fauour gudlye full fresche bewte like youngker tua lauchand ene al gratius behald ye seik behald present enee troianeeneas oracion quene delyuerit dangere storme wallis libiane se thou onlye quhilk reuch he piete vntellibill pyne troianis quhilk wes grekis leuingis remanis ouerset ciete gif thou mynd decretit eik weile likis thyne selfe thine eik vnto rewyne troy schent dede dur reddy patent mekill blede schedding priamus hiddir belife sal cum cruell pircus quhilk vaucys son assay haue done cum thys ye lattir day render grekis suffir bargane begyn may se daye vnwrokin sal neuer ane swerd belt agane schote left arme scheild mete bownyng furth quhen lo feit spous lappit honour god perpetually beystis blude fat ground neuer dry strowit garland flonris dyuers kind ilke kyng wod wraith halfe mynd schrewit rumouris sore amouit presens goddis quhilks louit altare iupiter father gif nought dredis quhen thou lattis thunder sle gif thi fyreslautht blind clouddis within fley myndes vane makis noyis dyn yone woman lait exile vacabound come boundis pryce bocht gound ane lytill vyllage byg quham manur gaif strand se quham lawis statutis gart mak marage gan lychtly saik hir regne tane enee lord thou secund paris ane accord vnwourthy sort skant half men bene aboue hede halffettis wele besene set like ane myter foly troyane hart hare anoyntit wele prunyet vnder reif mantemes hir suld ouers vnto thy tempillis dayly brynges offerandis vane hallowis thy name sic wourdis king hyarbas hame makand prayeris grippand alter hard anone almychty iupiter ene turnis towart riall wallis cartage luffaris quhilk fallis thay thare fame gude renowne foryet syne thus sayd mercurius let sic maner charge gan direct pa sone hastiubiter sendys mercury eneas exhorte hym depart fra earthage italye graith thy wyngis effect slide thy fedderom yone troyane prince quhilk cartage makis residence geuand na cure cieteis italie grantit fatall destany message swiftlye throw skyes say hym thus wordis sic wyse derest moder promyst v gyding sa faynt ane mane fuld sic causis delyuerit twyis furth grekis handis enemy bot suld haue bene wyis sage graif hie senyeoryis grete empire ha f itale dant quhilk brandisis battal dedis declare cleirly tell cumin tu trus hie genology subdew warldis monarchy sa grete thingis thoch na wourschip steris honour lyst labour efferis yyt fader aucht na wise inuy ascaneus bruke romys seniyeory spere quhat beildis dar duel amang ane pepill salbe inemyis fell linnage cum italy foryetys geuys na compt liuyne cuntre bid hym make sail effect thidder message thus direct said iupiter mercury st dressit obey grete faders behest first vntill fete fast buklit goldin wyngis quhare doi fle quhen list abone fluds hicht erd grete fard swyft flycht syne tuke wand quhare tel paill saulis cauchis hell vthir sunt thare gan schete ful hot deip soroufull griflie hellis pot quharewith makis folk slepe magre thare heid reiffis fra vthir sleip deid closis ene brekis stringis tua throw help tharof chasis wyndis aw trubly cloudis diuidis ane thraw tho furth fleis tyl last saw hie top sydes brade euin hard atlas ring crown heuin misty cloudis hede quhareon firren treis stand mony rout wyth wynd storme full oft schaik blaw schulderis beildit new fallin snaw furth chyn ilk hasard auld grete studis ischis styf ise schokillis cald doune sterne grisly berd hyngis first mercure heuenly schinand wingis gan areist hale farde fro then vnto sey fludis made discens lyke till ane foule endlang coist syde strandis fysche plenteous wyde fleis wattir strummand fludis law betuix heuin erch samyn wyse flaw mercurie clepit child cillineus di cending moder grantschir thus sandy coistis desertis liby eik wynges peirsyng wyngit solis feit cartage fyrst tred strete eneas found towris gan espy garrand bild new lugeingis besely belt ane swerd mettell brycht anone cartage proud wallis stone thow foundis quod biggismercuriis oration eneas desyryng obeye goddis co maud depart italy gret honur profyt hys posteryte deuyse ane ciete exercit ane wyiffis seruice thy awin materis realme foryetting allace hidder vnto bricht heuinly place gouernour godis sent quhilk rulis wyl erd heuin element bad throw skyis bare charge quhat beilds thou ly ic cartage quhat fine beleue takis hand waist thy time fremmit land gyf na law na honour moue list sa hie thinges promyst thy selfin thou wil occupy purches thin awin renowne ne glory yit hehald ascaneus vp waxin grete hope sede spryng quham till realme kinrik itale rome boundis bene destynate sans fale sic wyse thus carpys mercurius myddys sermond thus vanyst fer away wat neuir quhare furth mortal sycht schire p quhow eneas hym grathis depart co quham dido carpis wyth sare hart bot half mad doun stude al vp stert hys hare voce stak hys hals sare langis flewyse men oft time parturbet affectionis mid neuertheles gan place reson last depart sueit cuntre tothir part leif ful laith hym go large astonist sit hie ane charge disobey gret goddis beheist allace quhat suld vneis wy quhat wourdis suld assay amouris quene require pray quhat wyse tale mycht begin baith fra compasing breist wythin ful purpois euery part last thus stude dout resun hym semyt fynely best callis mynyscheus sergest strand cloanthus bad thay suld bye graith schippis nauin secretely gadder folkis towart coist togidder armour al thing necessare bryng thidder dissemmil gif askis quhy thay thus addressit thare gere suddanly self sayd mene quhile suld assay purches leif go pa away wat tyme speik therof maist habil quhen quene dido maist honorabit schuld beleif sa sone couth depart sa gret luf disseuer na art command thay al gladlye furth went besylie begoouth spede entent bot sone quene persauit al thys slycht quhay may begilethe furiousnes loue noted ane luffare day nucht thare departyng hand first sche aspyis dreding al soner thingis gise euery luffare al time stand fere ilk cursit fame spak ere bare amouris quene noyis gan roune schips ar grathad pa thay mak tha boune quharfor impacient myndeles hir rage sche wiskis wyld throw toun cartage sic wife quhen thir nunnys bachus ruschis relis ouer bankis brayis bus quhen euery third yere thare pagane wy thare goddis feist thay hallow loud cryis al nicht mont cytherone resoundis thare clamour quhare thay gone last yit thys hir frewill efter lang musing sche spak eneas tyl dissimilancethe quenes oration eneas desiring hym wyth syndry pyteful argumentis r may hyr wenyt thou vnfaithful wicht thou mycht haue hid fra sa fals ane slicht myne vnwitting ste le furth land nouthir grete luf promys rycht hand geuin vmquhile may withhald cruell deith didois cors cald gif thou depart forthir quhat wald thou wynter sesoun preis graith thy nauy addres pa throu voyd se myd tyme quhen stormes wyndis blow maist hie art thou sa cruel put cais also nane vncouth landis thou list go nouthir fremmyt place stedis wyl bot auld troy war yit vp standand stil aucht thou yit leif weilfare ioy sit perell seik throw sey troy quhat wyl thou fle frame allace allace al theyr teris trigland ouer face richt hand vmquhile thou gaif sen self elli left haif wretchit catiue treuth plichting eik spousage begynnyng beseik gif euir ony thanke deseruit toward ocht myne leif quod sche haue mercy lynnage reddy spil gif tyme remanis yit thou prayeris wil thys fremmit mynd pray away haif bene hatit mony ane day wyth al pepil affrik wich king rulis land mumyda ring myne awin tirrianis ar wraith womanhed went wourschyp baith fyrst fame laude eik renownye quhar rasyt sterne hye reddy de selfyn spil swete gest quham thou leyf wyll gest ha god quhen al thyng vane quhen spous nane vthir name remanys bot quharte suld dede langer delay sal abyde quhill thou went away quhil mi awin brothir pigmalioun bet doun wallis mi ciete anone sterne hyarbas kyng getulie leid away captiuite bot leist tofore thy way fleing ane child consauit thy spring gif ony young eneas small play within hall quhylk representit similitude thy face semyt thus wyse allace allace aluterlie dissauit dissolate thus sayd quene dido febil estate bot apoun iouis message ferinlye stude musing mouit ane e refrenit wil hidand hart hys thocht last thir wordis furth brocht gentill queneeneas gentyll humane ansuer quene schawing departs hys gud wyll comand god quhilk euery creatour shuld reason obey desyring hyr bew cotent tha kyng hyr kidnes ge tylnes aduersytye sall neuir deny gud dede desert mare wourthy thou wourdis toung may expreme sal neuir irk yit missene wourthy dido hald thy fresche memory sa lang self remember may quhill sprete lyfe thys body steres matir requiris ane litill heris purposit hide thistuisly vayage ye wene secretely away steil quhat nedis sa fene pretendit neuir na mene wyth make bande mariage yoik na frendschip cartage yit come enuir bot gif fatis may ony thyng amyd thy way traist rowkis blak thou sal dere thy treuth thou brak clepe oft rycht name dido dido wyth fyre infernale myne absence also sal follow fra cald dede reyf membrys thys saul euery stede goist sal present aggrise thou sal vnwourthy wicht apoun thys wyse punyst wele tharfor wald fame therof sal cum vnto ere vnder erth amang shaddois law thys spokin hir sermond ilk saw brak sche iwane ful dolorus hir thocht lycht sche fled al fast sche mocht turnis frawart hym wiskis hys sycht onsere materis leifand hym pensife wycht purposyng haue sayd mony thyngis damysellys fast thare forkit wayis mony mudy wicht ye infernale fury wrekis al wrang ye goddis eik quham amang dido standis reddy cum point de bessaue thir wordis quhilkis sall say quod sche withdraw fra hyne grete mychtis grete dangeris see bot land tell sum f r gretter perrellis remanis cum troiane pepill realme lauyue sall cum determit goddis diuyne thy mynd sic doutis away bot fothirmore vnto say quhen grund italy wrang wisly put dede cryme saikles sekirly thir setis ilk wycht war assignit iuge dome richt king mynes inquisitour iustice fatale vrne ballance deuise reulis equale discrecioun steris counsale iugement efferis sylly goistis callis secrete cage bayth thare lyfe crymes takand knawlage syne eftir thir sory full care thrid place haldis sall euermare giltles folk disdene wo fede thare handis wrochtthe third cyrkil selfis thare selfe dede irkit thare lyfe thay war thare sueit saulis made fra body twyn quhat penurite hard distres fere wald thay suffer warld bot fatis goddis decrete gane standis thay returne may neuir ther landis wofull pule watter thame vnlufly withaldis thame thay may ga stix flude belappis thame nyne tymes cloisthe cyrkyll schawis immoderat loue perisched may neuir away hiddils held thay roddis derne ane myrtre wod thame loukit yarne thare paneful masing thare heuy thoch eftir thare dede also foryet thay nocht thare phedra spous thesius poirus eik wyfe cephalus ilk stede trist eriphilce hir cruel sonnis woundis schewis sche euadne beheld laodomia pasiphe fallouschip tha ceneus first ane wenche ine ane man hir auld schape eftir dede changeit amang vtheris knaw full clere schewin thou swerd slaw bereft thy selfe life brocht daw allace causer thy dede sterne schynes aboue hede goddis aboue swere faith laute gif ony treuth may befund depe vndererd quod magre prince mote thy coistis depart constrenit commandementis goddis vnfenite quhais grete mychtis hidder driue pa throw dirk schaddois beliue gousty placis welfche sauorit moist hare quhare profound nycht perpetualie doith repere compellit disseuer mynde ymagine mycht neuer departing abscence wy thou suldelst caucht sa grete difeis thys stynt thy pais abide thou gentill wicht withdraw sa sone sycht quham fleis thou latter day wourdis schap speik may wish sic wourdis eneas full wo sett mei sprete quene dido quhilk inflammit ful wrath ire acwart luke glowand hate fyre made wepe sched ouer teris wak fremmitly fra wart spak hir ene affixt apoun ground held sche mouing na mare hir curage face bre sche bene ane statewe marbyl stane ane ferme rolk mont morpesiane bot finalie ful swift sche wiskit away agreuit fled derne woddis gray quhare sicheus hir first spous ful sure corispondis hir desire cure rendring luf amouris equiualent neuertheles fast eftir hir furth sprent enee pexplexit hir sory cace weping gan hir follow ane wele large space regrettand mind piete distres mouit hir fle p warde wourthy weremen enee beheld deiphebus spak spede fra then tuke gate vntill grantitthev cirkil contens valyeand nobil captans warre fate sone thay warren cummin plane lattir wardis quharein doi remane vailyeand folkis feildis cheuelrie tha secrete steddis hantand recounterit partanopeus complening thare e saw glaucus medontus thersilotus anthenoris thre sonnis polibetus vnto goddes cere consecrate ideus saw auld estate baith reuland yit cart wapynnis weldand vnto eneas left syde grete routis agamen ne al sone thay stalwart troiane saw bricht armour amyd schaddois law gretelie efferde war smyte felloun drede sum gaif bak tak flycht gude spede quhilum thay vnto thare schippis socht sum rasit ane cry wake voce thay mocht bot al nocht thare clamour ful skant soundis brak gaspyng ane gant syne diephebus quhilum armip oent kyng priamus son body tor rent thare beheld ane cruell til ane woundir grene vale ful sence saulis inclusit quhilkis war wend myddill erd thare bodyis ascend gan rekin beheld ententfully alhale nowmer genology thare fatis thare fortouns euery gre nobil actis ther posterite thare condicouns thare strenth hardymen sone persauis quhare thay went forgane hym cummand throw gressy swarde derrest son enee hasty farde baith hys handis ioyful furth straucht beleuit thou cum tyme calculit comptit quhen suld consait dissauit god throw fele landis brad large mony seyis ouer caryit thy barge eftir feile dangeres wyth storme oft schaik sauit dere son allake hie bene vthir bodyis eftir ischape yone riuer flude lethee sikkir watter curis traist qnharby obliuius becum thay al tyte foryetting pane past langsum syte forsoith purpois furthwith declare schaw thy face standand thare saulis al nowmer thy presence quhilkis ar cum stok discence mare glaidly tharby thou may reioyce haue found italy fader quod eneaspithagorus van opinion transformacion saulis wretchit wychtis sa desyre luf drery lichtis sall schaw forsoith caus quod dirrest son sall wyse hald thochtful mynd na doutsum way tharewyth anchises bayth hys ene tway gan lyften vp towart heuin behald euery thyng per ordour thus tald p sere punytion saulis syndrye thay passe syne flude lethee fra begynnyngphilosophicall sayingis god hye prouidece al thyng le mare fyry regioun erth plane flowand boundis se lichtnyt monys lamp lemis hye heuinnys sterne brycht sonny ball ane sprete thare within sustenis euery part hie wysdome deuyne diffoundit mouys thys warldis hale ingyne power mydlit ouer mekill body clepet vniuersale fra thai infusioun thir elementis sere baith kynd man beist cumys leuing foulis fleing fischis monsteris doith repare vnder slekit se marbel hew ane hate fyry power warme dew heuinly begynnyng original bene thare sedis quhilkis saules cal sa fer thir noysum bodyis cauld taryis thaym thare fra doi withhald withdrawis souerane heuinly kynd thare erdly lymmys yit thare irksum mynd throw thare mortal membris euer dede like dullith thare curage thare spretis godlike fra quhilk cummys al mankynd thay dredis desiris murnys ioys aye dirk mansioun prefoun blynd thir wile bodyis yfetterit blynd saulis thare cleyne nature may attend sa fer al eftir lattir end quhen saul disseuerit fra body natheles yit ar fullely harme cryme wrachit saulis seperate auld infectioun cum body late thus alu erly nedeful thyng mony vicis lang tyme enduryng c ntrakkit corpis away purgit sere wounderful wyfe ay thay suffer panis torment thare inueterate vicis ald went punytioun satisfactioun make sum stentit bene wisnand wyndis ake sum cryme committit clengit vnder watter depe hidduous se fyre gilt vthir sum purifyit clengit al sum ilkane v ganand purgatory mon suffir fra thyne ar send hy vnto large feildisthe ix cirkyll blessed pepyll elisee thare bene v nane bot ane menye quhilkis cummis inhabit remanis ony purgyn thir ioyful planis bere mon duel quhil lang day perfyte cours tyme done away spot fylth hardynnyt sprete fand sum tyme body sueit quhil purifyit fynd na thyng remane ane clene heuinly mynd subtel pure flamb celestial thir vthir saulis quhilk bene purgyt al efter thay haue within thir planis cirkil rollit ouer ane thousand yere god callis thaym vnto flude lethe felloun ferd nowmer ye e effect thay myndles becum baith plesoure panis al sum alienare blude sall gener sic ane quhilk fal name aboue sterne vp bring quhais stok neuois spring vnder thare feit lordschip sal behald al landis sterit reulit thay wald al fer son circuland se couth ouer al citieis italy wide quhare quhen younkeris troy arr uit wa schore vnder gresy bank thare nauy thay anker fast hank eneas vtheris chistanis glorius fresche lusty springald ascaneus vnder branschis ane semelie tre gan lenyng doun rest thare bodyis fre thare dinnare thame al addres grene herbis soukis soft grees floure skonnys war set vthir meissis sic reddy syne brade trunscheouris thay fill charge wilde scrabbis vthir frutis large betid iupiter fault fude constrenyt thay war vthir metis consumyt done paringis thare bred moup vp sone thare handis breik chaftis gnaw citistis coffingis raw ne spare thay last laik mete thare fatale foure nukit trenuscheouris til eite och quod ascaneus befall behald eit tabillis vp saide bot halfe dele bourd thame thocht thay hard ane fatall hym goddis confortis fallow geuis thankis goddis destany ye traist penates said enee alhale natiue goddis wele ye duellinge place quhare sall leynd remane cuntre heynd certis new remember fader anchises sic secrete takynnyis fatis wise schew rehersit sayand thus son quhen sic hunger thou stad sal thou art caryit til ane strange coist meissis consumit ar loist thou art constrenyt thy burdis gnaw fret thou irkit may beleif get ane sober dwellyng stede perpetually remember place nere fast found first cietie thy hand dicht fowseis wally hie standand hunger taryit v sa lang sal makend ful wele knaw lynnage ciete also cummyn eris ye set cours ouer sethe kyn askys troyanis causis ther cu myne land thir mony yeris schaw quhat caus quhat necessite schippis ouer sa teil haw siremes se bene hidder coist italy caryit dryue quhiddir nauy errit thare cours fer gane yit force storme cachit hiddirtyll oft wyl happyn frawart tyde marineris fludis depe wyde gyf ye syc wyse within reuer wourdisilioneus ansuer kyn thys wyse ansuere made mayst ryall prynce cummin hye parage god fawnus nowther scis rage force dyrk tempest v dryue vnto realme therat made arryue yit laid sterne cours neuer repent sche folk troy ressauit therof think ennoy al eneas destaneis swere traisty fayth rychthand sa vailyeant vnset defence hys lang vse experience armes quhilkis batal hantit ful mony pepil victorious vndantit desirit v freyndschip allly ionit thare senyeory lithlie thy freynd proffir quhil oure fre wil vnrequirit offir wourdis requeist tretye taikynnis oure handis borne vp hie oft fatis ladyis wrocht brosit al herand sic wourdis ilioneus ful stil visage haldis latynus sicht vnmouit erd prent ene rolling eris richt attent brusit purpour mouis na thing priamus sceptoure fer steris king ye hartlie welcum traistis sa lang leuis king latyne countre rich maist plentuous fertil ground ye fal want realme sound yit nane vthir welch welefare na ioye quhilk ye war wount bruke haue troy bot leist ye caus prince enee gif sa gretelie desiris v confiderit till alliance gif langis langare discrepance within palice entir vthir clepit companyeoun brother duel langare cum hidder haist ne faar freyndis face ane gaist maist part conuene band sall twich kingis hand agane ye sal curnand went bere prince charge commandement haue ane douchter quham responsis schaw furth faderis oratry law mony fereful taikynnys heuyn diuers wayis schewin fyry leuin suffer sche wedlok geuin vntil ane man countre al spay men declaris thare suld cum remane italy fra strange coistis son law ane dochty man beheld troyane nauy stand raw eneas blyith glade sche saw ioyus bodward vnto brocht besely hast mocht inforsis thare herbry strencht beild assurit land feild thare schippis left desolate waist extasy sche studeiuno yi troians prosperite ore commo ed yth hyrself desparat folkis quhensch fynd helpe goddis schese hys helpe deuyl hell mad almaist suddane dolour smytyn wounder sm rt schaik hir hede harmes hir hert hir breist thir wourdis wrappis hy och kynd pepill haitfull vnwourthy wylis fatis troyane bene myndis destanyis euer agane mycht thay bene slane troy feildis mycht thay haue swelt vnder thar scheildis ar thay vincust ouercummin ilkane quhat may thare presonaris agane tane troy infyrit yit thame brynt na syc labour fornocht tynt haue thay found eschape away threw myd fyre myd oistis way traist last force mychtis lyis dolf irkit yone catyue wychtis insaciat haitrent rest pece sa bald afore neuer wald ceis quhen thay ware chasit thare natyfe land flurt strome fra hand hand persew thay flemyt wauyngeouris throw al seyis self ilk tyde houri agane troyanis consumy strenth al heuinnys se quhat proffitit certis soukand sand yit scilla swelthis ay routand quhat awalit purches help forsoith attour alquhare gyf may heuinly goddis inclyne purpoisiuno leuis god sekis help deuyl sall seik forthir sine tham fer doun acheron fell sall moue depest pit hell put cais may optene latyne land thaim expell clene bot fatis immouebyl destany lauinia remanis spous enee yit leist thar may fall stop delay sa grete materis ane yere tway lefull yit athir kyng retinew batall doun sete myrk dungeoun hell sche prouoik callis ane yell ane sory furius sisteris thre alecto quhilk causis myscheif euermare desyris hyr kynd full grene emprentit hyr mynd dedly batellis dolorus strif dissate harme discordis sere freyndlich hellis monstour tartariane hatit wyth hyr vthyr sisteris ilkane pluto eik fader hellis se reputtis bisming belch hatefull se sa mony grisly formes sere sche doi hyr self translate sic fere bene hyr cruell schappis vysage sa foule laithlie hyr personage hyr pilis stede hare feil snakis springis ouer hyr body alquhare quhilk fury quentiunoi acion alect distruction troyans kynd sa perrellus iuno tyistis myscheif sayand thus vyrgine douchter myrk nicht thys ane seruice thy propir werk rycht thys laboure quhylk thyne det honouris fame ouerset na yit subdewit sic ane place yone troianis standis vode grace lat neuyr enee sa proudly optene spousage latinus douchhter schene na way lat neuer feris weild ane fute brade italiane ground feild thou brethir ane assent mony yeris aganis vthir enarme mortal weris thou may ouerturne haitret striffe hale houssald man aganis wyffe thow mai skurgeing andstraikis lugeing rais thou freyndis may mak quene amata al witles gart sche go cruel monstoure allecto ane infect fel venom gorgonyane socht first lat chime hie laurentyne kingis cheif ciete priuely begouth wach loure spous quene amatais bour quhilk al inflammyt ire wyffly thochtis new toune troyanis al fllocht bissy cure turnus mariage skaldyng hir breist mynd al ane rage wikkit goddes towart hir al fast ane hir slymy serpent haris cast depe hir bosum let inslip slicht amyd hir hart pipis precordialis licht ilk monstouris instigacioun wod wraith sche suld pertroubil al toun eddir slyding ouer slekit bodyis soft thyr ladyis amang thare wedis oft went thrawin nane wist quhar glidis furius quene dissauyng athyr sydis hyr mynd gan blaw kendyl syne ane felloun greif ouer curage serpentyne grisly serpent sum tyme semyt hyr hals ane lynkit goldin chenye sum tyme hyr cursche lap ane wai become seluage bordour hyr quai sum tyme hyr hedelace knyt hyr hare ful slyd sche slyppys hyr membris ouer alquhare sone fyrst infectioun ane lityl slymy benoun inyet quently sche sche begouth hyr wittis assale depe amid hyr banis skale multiply rage byrnand furie yit hyr breist cruellie sprete felt flamb freneticall quharfore mare sobyrlie furth eftir commoun custome vsage auld matrouns thare auld dotage huge complant hyr douchter regret troyane wedlok contrare hyr consate thus said sche weping ful pyteously fader kyng latyne quhy wyl thou quhy quhat sall child lauinia may banyst men geif lede away nouthir thou thy tender get pyete yyt compassyoun thy self hyr moder quham sa sone full desolate yone fals sey reuer wyl leif sturt god wate cary made mata quene dissuadis kyng atyne eue y ochter eneas ouer depe fludis haw al sone euer first north wynd doi blaw itnot euin sic ane fenyet gird quham paris furth phrige troyane hird socht vtheris went yelland vnder lynd quhyl al skyis thare skrik fordynnys sum war cled pilchis foune skynnis thare handis rasit apoun hie lange stourys wound sweit wine tre amyd thaym al quene amata gais soeuer ye latyne wyffis herkis gif ony fauouris frendschip yit remanis deuote breistis amang thir planis vnhappy moder amata gif ony thocht remordis mind alsua effectuous piete maternale lous hede dirk nycht alecto hir thrawin visage away furius membris lade part array hir schape transformyt ane trai hir forhede skorit runkillis mony rai ane vaile ouer sprede hir lyart hair ane branche oliue thare knittis yare iunois tempil l tos acion king turnus exhortyng battell contra ye tr anys semyt scho nun trattes clepit calibe visage stout yonge knycht present hir self thir wourdis hicht turnus thou suffir vndocht thy lang trauell laubour nocht thy scheptour croun deliuerit young banist new cumin troiane menye king latyne spousage lauine thy dowry bocht thy blude pyne denyis grant elli ocht succede realme besoucht ane alienar borne ane vncouth land pa thy way set gane stand thir perrillis thank gane yeild sen thou art mokit go doune bett feild oistis ethruria syne defend pece rest folk latyne almychty saturnus douchter aluterlie thou nicht thus doith quietly bad schaw planlie thir thingis haue done tharefore assembil cuntre addres thy fensabill men thare array enarmed glaidlie moue hald way towart portis hauynnys seye set apoun yone troiane menye drife thare chiftanys land hone thare payntyt caruellis birne done grete pouer heuinlie goddis diuyne commandit decrete determine lat king latynus awin harmes haue experience turnus armes bot grant wyfe childe lauyne kepe promys conuyne young man mokand prophetes herand sic speche answeristurnus answere moucht expres standis thou wenys weris messingere gone myne eris full lang ane strange nauy arriuit tybris streme fast fenye na caus till affray wene lest purpoos leif way riall iuno quene realmes list querrell foryet thole sall bot auld dame thy vile vnweildy age ouer set hasart bare fante dotage quhilk vode treuth verite sic curis vane occupyis dissauis prophete fals drede geuis thy mynd tharon thou na hede trete battall betuix kingis thyne occupatioun standis vthir thingis quhilk suld haue cure alanerlie bot goddis tempillis ymagis spie thole men peace carp reherce quham partenis battell exerce sic wourdis alecto haite fyre brynt hir fury rage felloun ire young man spekand suddanly trymbling hynt al membris hys body ene stude abasit hys hede hellys monstoure ful wrath fede hissit quhislyt sa feil eddir soundis hir figure sa grisly grete haboundis wyth glourand ene byrnand flambis blak turnus awondering styntis drawis abak purposit mekyl mare say stede haris sche rasit vp serpentis tuay hir scourge sound scho made wyth rageand mouth syne sayd felloun bere behaldis vyle vnweyldy age ouerset wyth hasaed hare fanat dotage quhen eild vode al treuth verite fals dede dissauis sa quod sche trete battel betuix kyngis behald gif consyder thir sygnis lo present ane systeris thre infernale furyis ferful hellis se se bere handis powere dede battels mortall sayand thus ilk feirs young knycht ane hait fyrebrand kest scho birnand bricht hir breist furius lemand schide dedely smoik fyxit depe hyde huge drede dissoluit slepe ouer al body bristyng furth crepe warme swete throw euery lith vane al enragit gan efter harnes frane armour al witles bed sekis armour ouer al lugeing law grete curage irne wappinnis wade crewell wylde al wit muade wikkit wodnes battal desire quharon birnis hait felloun ire lyke quhen ingil stikkis dry blesand found laid sydis pot playing liquour sparkis heit buling within feruent bullir violent wattir making reky froith vpsprent swellis vp skun bellis bedene veschel may broith contene bot furth poplis fyre thare quhip vp fleis blak stew al mekil turnus thus stad gretest chiftanis bad king latyne declare peace brokin wald moue graith thare armour fast commandis defend itale thare awin cuntrye thare inemies expel dryue yit yneuch baith lete thame wit baith recounter latynis troianis quhen said sic wise ganis goddis callit thare helpyng besely rutilianis ouer al thing ather vthir fast exhort pray best wyse werefare puruay sum maist semely farrand personage tyistis feild proue grene curage sum youth hede theis gude sum mouit throw riall blude progenitouris nobil kyngis sum war eik indueit proues knawin eik landis dedis wrocht maist knichtly handis ascanius huntand ane tame hart hurt quhilk first mouing thare strifs sturt qvuhil turnus wise partis rutilianis rasys hardy hartis hir infernall wyngis furth cary alecto towart troianis mare tary ane new flicht ane place spyit sche quharfor tyme coist se young semely ascaneus solace dyd hunt wyld dere following chase thare suddanly hellys wenche infest ane haisty fury houndys kest thare neis thyrlis ane sowir sent scho filly sothe fyrst occatio warbetuix troians rutilians besely thay went efter fute ane tame hart quhilk thyng first caus werefare fechtyng first steris wyld fosteris fell moue debait make batall hart body bayth grete square large hede ndis birnist fare quham chider ane thirreus thame amang reft moderis palp nurist lang thireus thare fader hie maister gyde stedis folkis bowis hirdis wyde storour kinge kepe yime large plane trust geuen full dantit full tame thare command becum beist command silma thare sister diligence arrayit flouris sweit sence oft plet scho garlandis tyndis hie dere also full oft tyme kame wald sche fele syis wesche till ane fontane clere full wele sufferit hir handis tame dere accustumyt quhen liest eit awin maisteris burd seik mete querall woddis wald raik ilk day euin tide turne hame strecht way till lugeing wele bekend fute hait selfe war nicht neuer lait hart errant fer ressett ascaneus wod hundis vmbesett percaise hait sonny gleme held doun summand clere ryuer streme cule hete vnder ane gresy bra ascaneus child self alsua birnyng desire notabill renowun nokkit bow byuent reddy boun wenand wyld lete sone ane arrow glide goddes wes reddy fast besyde thus hand addres wauering flane flaw fast ane sprang fra string throw wambe en rellis stynt scharp schaft duschit dynt dere dedelie woundit lame vnto kynd resset gan fleing hame enteris stall anone blude besprent mony grank gron like ane man besocht help supple plenyng house fillis silma eldest sister ane schout hir handis clapping fast hir schulderis cryis efter help gan togidder cal landwart folkis doureforstaris thay tho assemblit fray hy flokkis furth rycht fast vnwarnistly ilk furie pestilentiale houre ful priuely derne wod dyd loure cast thame flely hyr fereful rage furth vpstertis baith man wife page ane burdoun ane lang stif tre poynt scharpit brynt ane lityl ane knotty club knorry hede quhat ilk man fand first reddy stede sekand ane swerd rinnand fra pleuch thate greif made thing wappyn gud yneuch thirreus maister storour ane rout karllis assemblit al quhare percase besy wedge stude schidand ane foure akyn squarit tre mony pant felloun hanchis quaikis al oft ax reboundis straikis cruel goddis feirful alecto til ennoy hir tyme espyes tho spelys vp ful sone scho war wod apoun ane heith stabyl quhare beistis stude richt bustuously apoun rufe hie hirdis ensenye loude vptrumpis sche ane bowand horne hir awin wil ane feyndliche hellis voce scho schoutis schill quhais sound trymblit forest derne woddis resoundid est west blaw hard then mylis mony ane depe loch triuia ar diane dyn hard eik elli quhare full far sulphureus quhite ryuer callit nar laik fontane velyne baith fro cuntre syne wemen moderis effrayit case thare young child fast thare breiflis brase spedely haist besy fare lauborars vndantit thare hynt wappinnis assemblit euery syde towart sound quhare trump tyde dedlye voce blew ferefull syng treiane power also furth thring hale routis ascaneus reskew battellis war adionit new manere landwart folkis bargane hard blokkis ruschand ouer ane blunt styngis brissillit tre sharp scherand wappinnis made melle ground blaknyt ferefull wox alsua drawing swerdis sclentyng fra bricht mettell vthir armour fere quharon son blenkis betis clere elitteris schane vnder bemes brycht castis ane new twynkling ane lemand lycht stoure sa bustuous begouth rise grewe like fey changeit first hewe quhite lipperis wyndis blast syne pece pece schote felloun sound smate rycht hals bone lopperit blude stoppit aynd anone closit life tendir sprete fell doun dede loist swete mony hird men amangis quham ane elder galesus allane offerit self amyd fra fyrst slauchter made apoun wise turn u pepill battell cryis bargane manere yede plane feild euery battall stede hellis goddes iosing hir hir promys quhilk scho hecht fulfil al sone grete melle ryuer al laik asia fer nere likewyse fer mane mycht ken rout bene ane oist armyt men bot southand swannys suld wene ane sope fleand thay bene quhilk chasit affrayit iolely socht crowpyng coist syde fast p yit comptis poet chyftanys sum aganys troyanis fall werefare cum lo clausus eik douchty gude discendit ancientclausus dyuers pepil italye cummi ware sabynis blude ane mekil rout leadis furth grete men wourthy sic ane oist stere fra quham clan pepil claudiane cummyn ouer al boundis italiane ef ir rome geuin made fre sabinis thare propir ciete togiddir gan assembil ane huge route fra ciete amaterne flokkis ancient sabinis hait querites enety al fensabil men mytista quhil hecht tribule quhare growis oliue treis grete plente al thay duellis moentyne rosye feildis besyde laik velyne scharp craggy rochis hie quhilk harsknes ar clepit tetricye hingand hewis mony sloukand bra thidder held ciete casperia thay inhabitis ferales toun flude hymella vp doun al thay drinkys tyber riuere sauarus rynnys fresche clere wynnys nursia sa cald ortyne nauy grete bald latyne pepil also al thay quhare vnhappy flude allya flowis throw boundis bedyis thare land al thik thay gadder flokkys fra hand hand vnto amphitrion vthir goddis euery one ciete ane hallowit fchaw pallas son thidder also draw togidder principallis younkeris sobir senatouris pure officiaris samyn kest ensence ane stew besyde altare blude hed skalit new beand lew warme thare fulfast reik bot yit al swyth thay persauit eik grete bargis slidand thus raw throw derne woddis fast thidder draw stilly bendand vp thare airis ilk wicht thay wourth affrayit suddane sycht euery man thay left burdis hye fute gan sterting maniorie quhen hardy pallas forebyd defend thare sacrifice brek quhil war end hynt ane wappin ane menye thaym recounter anone furth haldis yit wele fer ane hil ane know thaym callis standying men quhat caus mouit youpallas oracione troias apoun sic way thir strang wentis vnknawin assay quhidder etil ye quhat kinrent ye schaw quhens ye come quhilk countre quhidder ye bring vnto oure boundis boidworde peaceeneas answere cummys fere eneas tho fader wourschip maid ansuere fra pulpit schip hand straucht furth mycht se takin pece ane branche oliue tre freynd quod thou seis pepil troy latyne folkis enemyis man boy quhilk flemyt realme newly agane thay ilk latynis socht wyth proude bergane vnto king euander al seik require succour supple bare message declare plane chosin men discend king dardane bene hidder cummyn beseking freyndschip knyt vp band armes fallouschip pallas astonist sa hie ane name dardanus abasit worth schame cum furth quod quhat euer thou berne bald say fader quhat thou wald enter lugeing rest quhare thou sal ressauit welcum gest furth anone hynt hym hand ane wele lang quhile rycht arme embrasand syne furth togidder rakit thay raw flude thay leif enteris schaw eneas tho freyndly commonyng spake curteslye thus sayand kyng thou maist curteseneas oration euander king desyryng helpe prince best nede euer byget grekis sede quham fortonn wald suld cummin lawlie besekin requere wald also suld furth reik wippit bendis branche oliue tre takin thy supple nede forsoith caucht maner fere drede thocht thou ane capitane grekis yborne also archade cuntre blude conionit athrides tway meane agamenone menelay bot myne aum vertew haly akillis goddis diuyne myrakillis forbearis al ane kinrede thy fame diuulgate euery stede fermly adioynit vnto fatis eik tharto inducis wilfully obey thare commaund schir dardanus king first land belt cietie troy ilion cheif fader grekis grantis lawlie stede ilk pepil vnder dawnus king rutulianis gouerning quhilk ledis aganis thy cuntre cruel batel persewis gif thay micht expel v land thay wene tharby may thaym gane stand bot thay sal vnder tyme first speik began ene mouth al body richt gan behald espying wyth sycht syne schortly madeofferynge hym hys help thyngis ansuere thus agane thou glaidly maist forcy troyane ressaue tendir freynd fere full blyithly knaw wele may voce wordis speche lei thy fader gretest anchises ful perfitly draw mynd vissage wourthy knycht maist kynd ful wele remember lang tyme gone pryame son kyng leamedone wesy systeris land hesyona socht ciete hecht salamonya samyn rais vayage made throw cald frosty boundis archade grene youth tyme pylis ying fyrst cled chyn berd begouth spryng ioyit se tha troyane dukis ilkone son kyng leamedone say ilk young pryamus behald maruell gloryus bot thy fader anchises quhare went hier fer al remanent mind brynt youthede throw desyre speik commun lordly syre acquentit adionit hand bene auld confederatis perfay quharfor morne al sone brycht day begynnis lycht landis skye succoure supple blithly sal yone fra hyne one army send gudis moblis amend mene time sen freyndis dere vnto sacrifyce ye cummin quhilk yerely vsyng anniuersere bene vnlefull defer tary tharfore v alhallow hie feist glaid sembland blythly mayst leist accustome then instant tablys freyndly burdis hant quhen thys said mesis cowpis ilkane quhilk war away tak bad bring agane self troyane men fute hate sonkis gersy scheraldis doun set thare principale capitane syne enee besyde self deis resauis benk ybeildit grene holyne wyth lokkerit lyoun skyn ouer spred syne young men walit besy thare eik preistis hercules altare rostit bullis flesche set bakin brede baskettis temys hye wynis birlis grete plente eneas samyn troyane menye dyd perpetuall oxin fillatis eit purgit entrellis clepit clengeng mete p euander telly eneas bade verray caus quhy sacrifice made stancheit hungeris rage appetite men begouth assuage said kyng euander na supersticiouns vane mysknawledge goddis anciane hye feist grete solempnite banket mesis ye se institut tyll v altare excellent maieste standyng bot dere freynd nobyl gest troyane preseruit fra cruell perrellus pane hantis seruyce apoun manere proper det obseruance ilk yere fyrst behald yone schorand henchis brow quhare yone craggy rochis hingis huge wechty brayis bene doun cast holkit fowis mont syde left waist quhare craggy quhynnys doun declyne drawin hyll ane huge rewyne yone ane cauerne caue auld dayis wyth gousty entre fer furth wayis nane quhare wyle fleure euer lew warme spred retent slauchter blude newlie schede tyrantis yet men dede affixit stude mony dolorus hedis visage blaiknyt blude berun bla laithlie odoure filth still inspirit send v help ful lang desirit becuunnyn mychtful goddis presence dantaris monstouris defence maist redoutit hercules come hand auenture vnto ilk land new slauchter strang melle gerioun quhilk hedis thre proude spulye arriuing triumphal conqueroure maid thidder driue cal bullus oxin huge grete eik ky pasture ete endlang yone wale large wyde tuk thare lugeing riuer syde bot vndantit furius mynde theif schrewit cacus al way myscheif thrawart engyne sle consait manere wikkitnes dissa micht ne durst tak hand ne vnassayit leif land foure semelie oxin body grete square al mony tendir quyes excedand fare al thay cattal away draif thay tred fuld na way persaif vnto caue ay bak wartis talis turne thare fute steppis thaym harlis tralis thus spreith vnto ane quhine stane closit gyn sic way wrocht quhay thare tred lyft goif na taikynnis suld conuoy thame coif mene quhyle al beistis war repaterit wele eftir thaire nychtis lare hercules depart hen behuffit morow airly first thay remouit catal gan rowting cry rare woddis rang thare sound ouer alquhare wyth thare noyis dynnyt hyllis knowis quhilk caue ane quyok lowis wyth loud voce squeland gousty hald al cacus traist reuylit scho tald bot tho greif wourthy hercules alcius neuo douchty alcydes oft syis clepit commonly within skyn begouth birn fry brym furie bittir gal wappynnis armour hynt wythal wechty burdoun knorry e hillis heicht held ane rase first time ony erd pepyl persauit cacus efferd within hede trublyt ene tuay swift wynd fled gar away caue sped cry sprete drede adionit wyngis foot fra self sesit tharein ane stane huge wecht clois gyn lete fal sic haist doun thrang chenyeis brak quharewith fessynnyt hang forgit war faderis engyne grete irne slottis schet entre syne bot lo haist hercules come hand furious mynd carying ouer land passage entre seking besely ene thare rolling hie gnassing teith birnand full ire auentinis hill thryis swyre sesis ouer thryis assayis brek rent craggy stone entre bot thocht neuer wycht thryis irkit doun hillis hicht rest vale gone thare stude ane pynnakyll quhyn flynt stone apoun bak side cauerne cald rais one end rycht hie hald wilde foulis reif ane ganand stede rent rycht hand dyd assemble stere wattry cloudis makis thunderis bere forthir eik sayd vntyl enee yone twa toun stedis thou behaldis quod wyth barmkin doun bet euery wal forefaderis thay beue memoryall thys ciete beildit auld fader ianus younder ciete foundit saturnus ianiculum thys hecht myne awin leif brother saturna clepit vthir amangis thame sic carpyng talke towart euandrus pure lugeyng thay stalke cattel eik beheld thay raik raw stede thare pasturand thay saw quhare rome chief markyt placis bayth squeil low thay ilk plentuous gatis quhilk symtyme hecht caryme fare large quhare hous war counsal eneas conteine wardly ryches follow vertew quhilk ledis hys honour rich thy selfe compone schaw dede goddis stede wourthy succede thame equale ressauit sic herbrye amang smale gere enteris bousumlye sayand mychty grete enee within narrow chymmes ledis made sitting doun apoun ane bed stuffit leuis ouer spred rouch skyn ane bustous wylde bere affrik bred mony ane yere p vntill eneas venus armour requiris fra vulcanus quhilk grantis hir desiris nycht appro hir wingis gray ouer spred erde put allicht away quhen venus moder til enee efferde caus seand felloun rerd dredful boist assemblay attanis aganis hir son pepil laurentanis wlcanus hir husband gudeman within goldin chalmer scho began thus speik hyr wourdis fyre diuyne luf towartis inspire quhod sche quhil kingis grece arge bet doun troianis wallis wide large destinat war baith tour towne wal inemyis flawmes doun fall na help vnto thay wrachitvenus oration tyll vulcanus desyring armour hir son eneas folkis socht na armour askit thy craft besocht derest spous exerce bad thy craft werk vane wald occupy albeit chyldren pryame kyng bedettit mekyll thyng vntollerabyll labour enee bewalit oft wepand ful sare quod sche quhilk iouis power stad remanis wythin bonndis rutulianis quharfore tyme thy ilk spous wyffe thy blissit godhede derrest lyffe cummys lauly beseik requere wappinnys harnes armoure syc gere dere son moder prayis sen nereus dochter thetes mycht quod sche induce tyl enarme hir son achill eik tythonus spous hir awin aurora hir teres brak tyl enarme hir child menon blak behald quhat pepyl lo assemblit bene quhat wallit townis yettis closit tene gryndis thare wappynnis aganis myne bryng v distruction rewyne thus said goodis hir mylk quhyte armes full tendirly belappis warmys quhyl musis hait fyre sle luf bekynd anone ressauit naturell hete merch glide persand bane maid soft euery syde nane vthir wyse sum tyme se schynand brokin thunderis lichtnyng fle wyth subtel fyry stremes throw ane rift peirsand wattry cloudis lift venus spous confydyng hir beutie full glaid persauis claucht sche fader vulcanus god aboue lokkit eternale chene loue answerit saidvulcanus louing ansuer wyfe venus quharfor myne awin hart dere safer thou glosis mattere quhy aris thou planelie thy desire quhidder becummyn thy lord syre ferme confidence thou suld haue goddes quhat nedis bot schaw thy mynd expres gif siclike curis desire bene thy mynd samyn tyme mene subuercioun troyis ring v bene bot lesum thing troianis til haue enarmyt thy request nouthir fader almychty leist ne yit fatis contrary gane stand bot troyis ciete mycht haue langar stand king priamus ring pouer mycht haif remanit fullely vthir ten yere gif thou thy grathis fecht thare thy mynd set hecht manere thing solist diligence may wrocht craft science yit may forgit irne stele moltin mettell graue burnist wele sa fer fyre wynd hie engyne art may compas deuyne tharfor desist thy strenth haue drede pray ocht thou nede sic causis thare nedis na requeist reddy fulfilll thy beheist thir wourdis said hate fire hir enbrasing desire lappit spousis breist armes plesand naturall slepe bete harmes eis wery membrys tak sine slummerit bot ane swak quhen fyrst silence quyet nycht myddell cours cyrkyl run rycht prouokyng folk fyrst slepe awaik lyke pure wyffe quhilk euin raik hyr ingyll risis bet hir fyre sche nanecompar son vthir rent hyre bot wyth hyr rok spynnyng thryffe therwyth sustene hir empty lyffe hir day werk encres sche may se thartyll ane part nycht ekis sche candyl lycht hir handis tway eik hir pure damesellis sche may naithly exercis wirk lyne snoif spyndyll lang thredes twyne quharby sche micht sustene hir powerte kepe chaist hir spousis b honeste therwyth eik fostir hir childir lyte michty god fyre tyme al tyte slawar bot samyn manere furth bed steris hint gere smedy craft forge hym spedis thare standis ane ill wyth reky stanys gledis vpstreking hic betuix coist sicille liparen god eolus wyndy yle vnder quhilk big iland se ane coif thare hirnes fele thar like tyl e hna holl mont ciclopes furnes worne bront makis rumbling quha dyd thunder bustuous dyntis studyes ser ane huge dyn noyis straik make irne lumpis cauis blak bysse quhissill hate fire doith fuf blaw bleisse birnand schyre quhilk forgis bene vulcanus duelling call eftir vulcane cuntre namyt mychty god fyre doun heuin foresaid ile descendig euin quhare til large gousty caue hidduous cielopes forgit furth draue bronte storopes nakit piragmon glowand irne wel poyne anone fyre slaucht yit formyt perfytlie quhylk fader goddis oft throw skye euery art doun erde doi cast thay thare handis wirkand fast ane parte polist burnist wele dycht thare vthir party parfitit richt thre rawis wel thay frosm hale schoure thre wattre cloude eik stoure thre blesis birnand fyris bricht thre blastis south wyndis bricht syne thare werk manere gun pouder thay mydlyt thay mixt fereful souder ane grislie sound grete drede goddis ire quham followis ay fel flambis fyre ane vthir sorte ful beselie marte rynnyng quhelis forgeis cart quhare men battel doi stere mouis cieteisthe armour wysdom raise mortal thay dicht polist egirlie alsua horribil tergate bustuous egida quhilk greuit pallas grisly scheild serpent skalis poudderis goldin feild togidder lynkyn lowpit edderis tuay breist goddis graif thay gorgonis hede monstour grete wounder wyth ene wauland nek bane hak sounder away wyth ye ethne ceclopes quod vlcanusvlcanus commaundis seruandis make gudly armour eneas sic werkis ceis saw imprentis thocht vnto ane forcy man ar wrocht harneis armour nedis quod strenth exerce pythus schaw let se quhay nymlyest cum turn thare handis al maisteris poynt craft standis put away haist al manere delay na mare said wounder frakly thay vnto thare labour thame al addres assignand euery man part expres irne metal throw conduttis flowis moltyn gold relike stele hate glowis furth gousty furnes found ran maist craftely forgin thay began ane huge grete semely tergane ane scheild quhilk onlie micht resisting feild agane dynt latyn wappinnis euery place seuen ply thay well cal sum ressaue glowand hate sum wynd wyth blawand bellyis bet fire behynd sum trouch apoun sperkland gledis bissand watteris trinklis ouerspredis huge coue al mont wythin straik studyis gan resound din amang thame self thay grisly smethis grete mekle force forge peyne bete thare armes hesing vp doun nowmer dew proportioun wyth grypand turkes oft also glouand thay turnit fro euander telland eneas thynges sere vulcanus armour skye appere qvhill faderis lemnos vulcanus wythin boundis wyndy eolus werk gere haistis euery syde blysful licht airly morow tyde myrthful sangis birdis bay swallo singis rufe hir lay walkynnyt kyng euander maid ryse wythin sobyr chyme quhare lyis vpstert auld cled cote apoun fete hys mete schois hote war buklit wyse tuskany syne ouer schulderis doun myddil hyngis buklit crafty swerde archade left arme richt syde laid ywomplit spottis pantheris skyn hys twa keparis furth hym ryn hie palyce bustuous houndis two haldis thare lordis pais quhare euer go furth held secrete priuy way towart stede quhare eneas lay hys troyane gest remembryng rycht help promys grantit yester nycht one wise morowfull arely eneas haistis vp mycht ly kyng onlie bot son pallas achates eneas accumpanyit thay ioned handis sone thay wer met syne amyd chawmer doun thame set quhare fynaly thay fell commonyng secrete materis autentyk thing king begouthking eua deris oration eneas schawynge hym way begin warre said first enee maist souerane ledar troyane cumpany quhay beand life neuer grant sal troy distroyit cassyn doun wal yit troiane power put vnder haue bot sobir pussance wounder help battell make supple vnto hie excellent maieste half fortun wist sa happelie thou schawis helpe supple maist douchty campioun ene desirit destany fatis ye wele arryuit mony gatis foundit auld stanys hyne inhabit stude ciete agillyne quhare wourthy pepil commandement stout begyning sa douchty may nyte na thing forsoith woman quhat soeuer sche frathyne fordwart sal moder wanting na mare moder plane alanerlie bot creusa hir name thus sic ane birth na moder vnto thy kinred sal fully bene obseruit thy stede thus said wepand tharwith alsua gyltin swerd hynt schulderis fra quham wounder craftely land erete lycaon forgeit wrocht mete ane birnist principally fresche afcaneus ying uf al vtheris commonyng schewand wisdome consate fore sicht agit men eik curage wicht gaif thame fele chargis commandementis bere fader twichand ententis bot wynd thay skatterit war raw nocht amang cloudis law furth ischit thay fowsyis wentis silence dirk nycht amang tentis perillus palliouns thame inemye thay entrit ar caucht grete harme thareby bot netheles ony skaith thay hynt dede monydronkinnes meit war thare douchty dynt apoun gers ouerset wyth slepe wyne fordwart fallin doun al drynkin swyne bodyis rutulianis thare thay persaue coist alquhare cartis stand lymouris bendit strek men ligging hame thare nek amangis quhelis thetis al samy lay thare armoure wyne metis baith men cartis mydlit al ouer ane ane bai voce thus nisus spak agane eurialus matir thus standis stout forcy handis thys passage quhilk way mon wend thy part sal kepe defend nane vnset cum v bak spy fer gude tent thareto thou tak sall mak vode passage way conuoy throw ane large strete away rehersand thus anone held clois noyis mycht thare hard voce tharewith eik drawin swerd preis gan assale pompus rhannetes quhilk lay percase slepand soft sound proud tapettis spred apoun ground ane kyng ane spay man soith say turnus kyng maist trest anguriane bot wyth diuinacioun augury traik deith ne couth put thre seruandis fast hym lay full reklesly kelit al thoch thay amang thare speris ligyng war fere quellit ane remus squyere tartar syne liging apoun strete hynt anone amang hors fete swerd nek hingand syde twane hakkit samyn tyde thare lordis hede mene said rhamnete smytis quhil al bed wox wete lyke ane dede stok corpis wantand hede lay bullerand al besprent sprangis rede al erth grew warme wyth teppit blude attour slekit eik quhare stude twa forcy men lamus lamirus al likly young child serranus al fore nycht ryet play spendit list lay wyth membris stekit plesand vysage brycht ouerset god bachus mekyll micht ful happy wele fortunat sport gam samyn wyse gif remanent nycht spent quhil licht day tyl self tane tent like empty lion lang vnfed nychtis tyde quhen al folk slepe bed trubland fald ful sily schepe wod rage hunger depe constranyt sic wise fare ryuis harlis thare tendir beistis awful fere presence dar nowthir blate stere rummesis bludy mouth brayis eurille none vthir wayis na le slauchter made plane ire inflammyt hys wod brane ane multitude commouns birth law quhilk reasoun thare name ar vnknaw vmbeset put confusioun fadus syne hesebus dang doun arabis also vnwarnistly ret u eik lay walkand hard thaym behaldand al thare sterage deray bot stout eurialus affray behynd ane wyne boit ane pipe hid quham eurialus cace betid kippit swerdis poent al blaid hid coist vp hiltis glaid dede duschis doun bayth stiffe cald vp purpure sprete lyffe yald blude wyne mext gan furth schaw last drank yeiskis dede thraw sic slicht ful brym thus enforcis make huge slauchter vnweildy corpsis et yng wichtlie nixt stude hym thare mesapus feris al ly last fyris quhiddir ar ye boun ye fchaw v plane tothir twa maid nane ansuere agane bot woddis hyis flicht assurit gretelie dirknes nycht horsmen prikkis fast furth sprentis wele beknawin pethis turnis wentis sla lo said turne hiddir blaid swerdis ye retulianis al flicht feris slane silly innocent creature sa ying mycht yit durst hand tak sic ane thing heuynnys hie sternis swere v behaldis thare bemes se eurill nisus hedis speris hie fixit thay rasit haldand wall huge clamoure followand ane forcy stout eneadanis tyme ciete remanis bront force thare army tyde endlang wallis set left syde richt hand closit riuere thay held forefront quhare thare danger kepand brade fowsyis towris hie thay stand ful dolorusly thay se twa hedis stekand speris ane miserabill sicht allace vnto thare feris thare fatis war ouer wele bekend baith twa blaiknyt dedely blud droppand tharfra mene quhile throw drery ciete wyngyt messingere fame swiftlie fle slippand come thy modir eurilly suddanly wrachit wich vnsilly
