wyth wepyng wyfely womenting ryiffand hyr haris wallis thryng wod enragit wyth spedy pace dyd occupy thareon formest place takand nane hede yit na manere schame sa amang men ryn roup rame na manere fere perrill seis sche mynd dartis cast fast fle wall hir sonnis hede behaldis sche woful wyl rede hyr pietuous woful complantis sare heuinnys sche fyllit eurill lamentably sche cryis sall sethe moderis lamentabyll oracio hyr oni deth demanit sic wyse thou lattir quiet myne age micht thou sa cruel rage leif alase thus myne allane maist tender hart quhare art thou gane na licence grant tyme ne space thy wretchit moder allace allace thou thy selfe vnto sic perrillis set wyth mycht sa mekil laser get tak leif euer ay thy last regrait quenching wordis say ythane allace till ane vncouth land wepand wounder fast hynt hir vp betuix thare handis square sine hamewart hir lugeing thay hir bare bot trumpettis rely blastis aboundis wyth terribyl brag brasin bludy soundis skry clamoure followis oist within quhil heuinnisthe rutilious inuadis bemyt dyn wolsteaners assemblit ane sop fyll fowsyis wallis stop samyn haistand ane pauis tre heissit togiddir aboue thare hedis hie sa surely knyt manere enbuschment semyt ane clois volt quhare thay went ane vthir sort preissit haue entre clym wallis ledderis large hie quhare army troyanis side thynnest skatterit wallis wyde bricht arrayit cumpany men war diuidit sloppit thay micht ken weremen sa thyk sic ane place bot troyanis oft sic like case lang vsage war lerned kend thay thar toune wallis fuld defend kynd wappynnis dartis thame slinggis dang thame doun wappinnys poyntit stingis doun weltering eik huge wecht grete stanis ony way gif thare nanys micht force disseuir punye quhilk thame assailyeit thekis pauis hie wele thay kn w thare fais al manere tene vnder volt targis mycht sustene sa lang thay samyn vnserit ware bot thay mycht thare ordoure hald na mare troianis euer thay wald ceis thare thekest rout maist preis ane huge wecht hepe mekil stanys ruschis weltis dounthe troianis defendis thame attanis diuers rutulianis lay thare vnder laf skalit brede brok sounder couertouris ordinance thare scheildis fra then hardy rutulianis feildis preissit na mare hiddillis fecht bot thame enforsis thare mycht ganyeis arrowis dartis sling thare famen wallis ding ane vthir side felloun fere mezentius grym apoun ane spere heich grete slauchter troyanis ire calliope ye musis inspire til endite call schaw quhat slauchter octisioun fe l corpis thare brytnit doun turnus wappinnis dartis fell quham euery man kelit send hel help neidfull place nere yet quham assailye ouercum doun bet hale pissance italianis vter power vmbeset anys contrare tothir syde kynd discensis troianis prouide threw stanis doun shotys thare euery part opin fynister grundin dartis lete fleturnus byrnis tour slayis mony pepyl doun thik fald turnus prince baith derf bald ane birnand bleis lete foreteres glide festnit fire hard towris side quhilk windis blast thare stak vpblesis burdis thak spredis wyde amang gestis grete birnand low consumed al throw hete within thay schulderit feil affray bot nocht preis wyn away na lasir dangere eschape thay ran abak thame hape till withdraw towart tothir side quhare fire yit ouerglide hurlit togiddir ane hepe tho thare swe htis thay rele lepe birnand towris doun rollis ane rusche quhil al heuynnys dynlit dusch doun welteris men half dede brokin banis huge hepe thame fallowit ani thare awin wappinnis stikkand sum stikkit throw coist speilis tre lay gaspand thame skarsly tway ane helenor lycus gat away quham formest ilk helenore flurist youth get lore betuix meonyus king priuate latiuia bound wensche wounder sle quhilk troy send hinder yere vnkend armour forbodin deliuer drawin swerd hand quhite targate vnsemely euil farand helenor seand selfe dout amyd thousandis enarmyt turnus rout behald graithlie apoun athir hand arrayit oistis latine pepil stand like wilde ragent beist quham huntaris stout vmbeset thik range al seand na mene scho mycht euade apoun wappinnis rynnys ane brade slippis hir self grete force hir beris apoun poyntis hunting speris nane vthir wise ilk young helenore thus vnbeset behind eik amyde fais ruschis redy de quhare thekest preis thare ettlis quhilkis abade alsone himslane spark glede wald sey remane bot licus spediar fer fute throw oistis armed men fle wallis wan vp hicht enforcis clym mycht grip sum hys feris handis quham turnus lansand lichtly ouer landis wyth spere hand persewis spyll quhen ouirtane wil thus chyde catyue witles knape quhat wenit thou handis tyl eschape tharwith drew hym doun quhil dide hing wall ane grete part bryng lyke egyl iouis squyer straucht wythin bowand clukis vptaucht ane young cignet quhyte swan hare tharewith resursyng vp hie ane reuennous bludy wolf throw slycht hyntis goule furth fald nicht lityll tendir kyd young lam wyth feel bletingis socht gate hir dam rutulianis ioy rasit ane schout fast iuuadis ciete wyth hepis erd fowsyis thay sill sum vthir presit schidis mony ane fill fyre blesis rufe sling bot illioneus time dyd doun ding wyth ane grete quhin roche craggy stone one lucecius brak nek bone approche towartis yet hate flame fyre tharin set ligere ane troyane wall also doun bet ane rutuliane hecht emathio ane phrigiane eik asilas flerne stout fruschit chorineus without quhilk akin spylis dykis sic wy schame ye prolong liuis said thir vincust cowart wychtis behald se dar spousage batal craif quhat wyld dotage sa made hedis raif quhat vnthryfty god sic foly yon bewaiffit italy ar ye slaw remen atrides fenyeare fare speche vlixes bot bene naturu derf doure cummin kynd bene men ane stoure young child fyrst tyme borne thay vnto nixt rynnand flude webare hardin thare bodyis mak thaym bald schil frostis wattir cald childer ying exercis beselie hunting houndis horne schout crye wylde dere throw woddis chace mate dant ryn horsis late thare gam sport thay hant raw wyth thare bowis schute dartis thraw yong springaldis may al laubour endure content litil mete assure youth thay accustumed skant erde pleuch harrowis dant batal bettis cieteis doun euery age wyth irne graith ar boun passand plewis gadwandis broddis oxin speris handis yit slaw febil vnweildy age may waik oure sprete mynnys curage strenth altare ocht pare stele helmes thrist hedis hare best likis v al tymes rug reif driue away spreith theron leif yone payntit habitis doi purpour schyne hartis likis best deuyne ydilnes rest aboue al thyng tak lust go karrellyng cotys traling sleuis ouer handis foly hattis trappouris brasin bandis verray phrigiane wyiffis dasit wichtis call men troy vnrycht ye vnwourthy se hie stile clame dyndyma top go walk hame quhare quhissil renderis soundis sere tympanys tawbernis ye war wount bois schawmes torned buschbome tre grewin beretentia montane hie vnto moder ida dedicate callis eftir dante debate yeild men leif al armyng rendir swerdis al wappinnis resyng ascaneus ying birnand propir tene sa grete outrage wourdis micht sustene herand sa hie pompus pryde sic dispite blawin apoun syde hys bow hors senonnus bendit tharin ane takill set souir tre tasand vp armes fer twyn thus vnto iouy lauly begyn make first peticioun prayere omnipotent hieascaneus oratio iupiter iupiter assist hardy commantement self vnto thy temple sall present solempnit giftis maist gudly may get eik thyne altaris sall set ane young bullok cullour quhite snaw wyth goldin schakeris forehede arrayit raw beist sall full tyde trig wicht hede equale tyll moder hicht reddy horne fuyn put schraip skattir soft sand wyth fut fader heuyn acceppit prayere part quhar lift maist clere towart left hand maid ane thundering samyn soundit dedely bowis string quhirrand smertly furth flaw takyll tyte qwite throw hede remulus smyte groundin steile throw templis glaid hald thy wayis haist ascaneus said thy self loif knak scornefully proude wourdis al standis sic bode worde twis takin troianis sendis hansell rutulianis thus fer spekis ascaneus mare bot troianis rasit ane skry rerde clamour blythnes man boy sterne thare curage sprang ioy ascaneus extolling aboue skyes thay mak riot sic wyse doun regioun heuin tho bricht curland harit appollo apoun ane cloud sittand quhare wald oistis italianis behald eik new troyis ciete chere glaide til iulius thy victorapollois exhortacio ascaneus thus said eik contynew new vailyeand dedis thou young child way ledis vp sterne heuynnys hye thou verray goddis ofspring quod al engendir goddis sede veray ressoun nede batellis quhilkis werde ar destynate aganis asseratus hous moue debate sal appesit quiet brocht thys litil toun troy wrocht may wythhald sic boundis lyte sayand thus hie heuin al tyte discendis mouand halesum chyld ascaneus socht richt thare figure changeit tyme wald likenes ane butes hare ald purseuant fore squyare troiane anchyses fader enee traisty kepare hys chalmer dure enee commyttit cure tyl attend apoun ascaneus ying lyke thys antient butes al thyng furth steppis phebus bayth voce hew wyth lokkis quhite armour na thing new rously ane felloun sound clatteryng sic wourdis spak iulus yyng vthirwyse hate ascaneus wyth ardent mynd bargane desirus eneas verrye douthty son may suffice nedis na mare sen thou vnhurt thy schot stede strang numanus thou doung dede fyrst louyng eik hie renowne souerane appollo grantis nane disdene sall haue soithly perigall archery leif chylde syc batell ceis na mare tyme draw preis wyse carpis brycht appollo myddis sermond tho wanist fer away wat neuer quhare furth mortall sycht schyre nobyllis troyanis capitanis trew thir taikynnis god appollo knew hard arrowis clatterand case tharfore thay haue withdraw furth place ascaneus brycht phebus mychty targe wald na langare thole hym go large thocht fecht desyre ioy name tyl hys innis thay conuoy syne bargane thame sped agane oppin perrell dangeris pane thare persouns liuis thare toun offerand defence maid thayme boun p pandarus bitias brethir twane kest vp yettis thare bitias slane endlang wallis kirnellis euery stand brute clamour rais fra hand hand thare bustuous bowis kyndely thay bend scharp querrellis castyng dartis furth send quhilkis thay lyames quhayngis lang threw thyk ganyeis flanes flew takyllis schaftis feildis war strowit large planis ouerheildis bois helmes scheildis werely schot maid rap rap reboundand ilk stot scharp awfull incressis bargane al violent euer yet doun rane furth west doi smyte apoun wald october quhen twa sterne cald clepit bene kiddis first vpspryngis al thik hale schour hoppis dingis furdis schald brayis thare quhen trublit bene heuynnis wyth stormy tempestis northin blastis quhil cloudis skatteristhe hystory pandarus bitias al lift ouercastis pandarus bitias twa brethir germane alcanor engendrit troyane quhen hibera wilde forstaris knaw bred vpbrocht iouis haly schaw big young men thay war grete wicht equale semyt thame hicht fir treis thare landis hillis thare eik sa egir thare willis thay porte quhilk eneas charge commandit steikit large warpit opin brede wall baldly dyd chay fais clepe call entir gyf thay durst thame assay sa grete confidence thare fors thay thay wythin stude yet tyde quhilk oppin richt left syde thay touris bene bayth grete square enarmed wyth thare wappynnis brycht bare hie tymbrettis thare helmes schane lyke behald bustuous aikis twane beside bene riuere achises grow flowand fludis bankis pow vpstrekand thare byg croppis vnsued branschis waiffand thare al swyith rutulianis se yet opin thay ruschit entre quercens formest equitolie ane lusty knycht armes richt semely wyth tmarus feirs myndit asiale bald emmon wyth curage marciall bot thay wyth al thare complicis ficht war doung abak constrenit tak flicht troyane routis striue quha abade loist porte thare lyue tho brymmer grew thare feirs mudis wythin troyanis flok samyn ryn towart place maid felloun debate bald thay wox plane gate ischand wythout portis land thay durst recounter thare fais hand hand ane messyngere turnus come tyde wounder feirsly vthir syde toun assailyeis thare tyll hym schew quhat hait slauchter hys fais made new sic ane porte al wide opin set first purpois left yet wyth felloun ire mouit furth sprent tho towart troyanis proude brethir two first slane big antiphates case met formest preis sone bustuos nobyl serpedone purthes get ane thebane wensche apoun smate doun cast ane dart fleand schaft italiane hart glidand throw schire duschit sone stomok peirsit coist done cauerne wound ane flude furth bruschit blaknit dedely blude depe grundin steil hede sicht ful hate warme festnyt lichtis syne meropes erymantus apydnus slew wyth hys hand al thre eftir wyth ane sterne mude ful tene slew bitias al glourand ene bot nouthir dart swerd knyffe na sic wappin mycht hym haif reft lyffe bot ane hidduos bissand fyre spere clepit phalirita quhylk wyth vehement force thus turnus threw thunderis dynt hym flew quham nouthir scheild twa bull hydis thik yit doubil mailyit traist haubrik al gylt wyth gold mycht resyst stynt bustuous body doun duschyt wyth dynt quhyl al erd granyt wyth rattyl hydduous scheyld aboue hym made ane brattyl lyke hye pyllare marbyl stone standand apoun coist eubortone vmquhile besyde bay ryche ciete wyth grislie swelth doun duschit se quhilk auld masly stone ane bing fludis sic wise doun ding fal drew doun ciete quhare stude ruschit ane fer way flude seyis mixt ouer ane al ouerhede blak slike sand vp poplit stede quhilk fereful sound ilandis twa trymblit inaryme eik prothita quhil inaryme iupiteres command ful hard bed typheus giand thys tyme mar god armypotent ekit latynis force hardiment felloun ire prikkand thare myndis self list turnis wyndis makis troianis tak flycht gude spede one thaym kest sie fere schamful drede latyne pepil flokkis euery syde quhen thay beheld porte opnit wyde seand thay ane roume fecht wyl god stryffe thare curage steris thar tyl p turnus big pandarus smote doun lyke ane wodlioun past wythin toun pandarus seand brotheris corp erde quhat wyse thys fortoun wyth thaym ferbe chance batel yede al wrang ful force lie brade schuldaris strang thristis leuis yet closit queme entre furth schet without porte ane grete sort teris hard bargane amyd mortal weris hys inemyis sum inclusit ressauand al thrang entre ane fule witles ane thing persauit turnus rutuliane king violentlie thring yet quham vnwar within ciete schet like rageand wilde tygyr vnstabil amang febil beistis miserabil sone turnus inclosit sene ane glowand new licht bristis ene armour ringis clatteris horribilly creistis trymblit hede hy sanguine bludy scheild al stracht kest schynand fyry bemes like fireslaucht sodenlie affrayit eneadanis face vnfreyndlie persauit big banis hidduous pandarus furth schew wounder feruent furoure grew brotheris slauchter reuenge wil thus austerlie spekis turnus vntil quene amataisthe bargane betuix turnus padarus chief ciete suld begeue doury sayd yit myddis ardea ciete bald thy faderis burgh turnus doi hald thou seis thy fais strenth wallis wyde yeild thy thou may eschape na syde turnus agane curage blyth glaid abasit ful baldlie hym said freynd begyn gif thou hardyment mache allone apoun bent hand hand gif thy wyl thou sal schaw priame thou fund achil tothir two ane huge spere hale tre bark knottis al togiddir lete fle al force bot dynt dere bot woundit sper wikkit iuno auld saturnus get choppit schaft fixit yet ha quod turnus sa sal thou astert wappin faith depart sic wyse eschape bitand brand quhilk grete force thus rollis hand aw swerd wound sal wirk sa faynt ne sa sone sal irk word standand tip tai heuand swerd heith hand rais doun dynt duschit steile blade kene amyd forehede hard betuix ene berdles chekis chaftis round sounder schorne ane grislie wound sa felloun sound clap made grete clasche huge wecht fell ane rasche erd dynlit al ciete schuke large feild gousty body tuke fer brede remembrit caucht mynd rent lokkis vp opynnyt yettis wyde feris without porte tyde mycht haue enterit cummin cyete last day batel lattir finale end romani phrigiane folkis pepil troianis bot sic ardent hic furoure martiall slaucther desire vnsaciable draif follow thaym hym ganestandis first kelit phalleris handis ane vthir giges hecht alsua quhamlche hochis bayth smate twa syne speris rent hynt vp raw flearis bakkis fast dyd thraw wounder se hym quhare went iuno ekit strenth hardiment syne ane hale vnto corpis dede company ekit stede phegeas donn brittynnys feild spetit throw body scheild alchandrus syne proude halyus nemonas syne kene pritanyus quhilkis mysknew turnus within wal bargane thare feris cal apoun ground anone al dede laid bergane ful expert syne inuade wyth shynand swerd hard dykis syde ane lyntheus quhilk samyn tyde resistis mycht fell efferis eftir help cryis apoun feris bot wyth ane straik smat nek twa bayth helme hede flaw fer body fra eftir thir ane amytus slew bane bene wylde beistis ynew nane vthir mare happy expert graith till inoynt ane casting dart vennom garnes steile hedis turnus handis ilk tyme doun dede eolus son hate clitias heynd creteus also mus freynd creteus poet mus familiar hys mynd breist al tymes bare sangis geistis musit harping apoun stryngis playit mony ane spring lay rymes apoun best awise euermare manere gyse sing blasoun diseriue men stedis knichthede striue p troyanys set ou turnes dyntis rude quhil fleis lap flude last mnesteus strang serestus troiane capitanis herand thus thare pepil slane war doun conuene thare feris fleand pale wan haue thay sene thare cheif inemye closit thare wallis mnesteus thaym clepis thus callis quhare ettill ye fra hynemnesteus callys agane hys troyanis fleyng quhiddir wald ye fle quhat vthir wallis seik ye ciete quhare haue ye outhir strenth forteres cietezanis behaldis expres nane bot ane man standand aganis closit within dykis wallis stanis vnreuengit grete occisioun huge slauchter sal mak within toun sa feil vailyeand young capitanis kend vnresistit thus doun hell sal send maist vnwourthy cowartis ful sleuth vnsilly cuntre haue ye na reuth piete ancient goddis kind think na lak schame mynd sa grete outrage strang enee obsence thus catifely fle troyanis sic wourdis said curage grew fermlie al abaide thare famen flokkand ane rout turnus ane litil thocht stark stout begouth frawart bargane draw sattil towartis riuer syde law aye pece pece part toun closit riuer rynnand doun troianis seand mare apertly assailyeit mony schout cry thikkit fast inuiroun quhen awful wylde lyoun wyth thare inuasibil wappinnis scharp square ane multitude men belappit war ful feirs thrawin vult start seand scharp poyntis reculis bak wart bot gif bak fle away nouthir greif curage suffer may thocht wald al mekil mycht aganis mony men wappinnis bricht preis fordward may cum na spede nane vthir turnus sic ane nede steppis abak huly pay ful stil mynd skaldand greif egir wil son word wisdome eternale betuix thir twa lufe perpetuale quhilk haly gaist fra baith procedys faderis nature mynyst substance generis hys son blis ne son kynd ybore ane parte therof bot al geuis hys son al ilk thing genis remanis singil substance indefferentlie thus ganis thre ane ilkane thay thre samyn thing ane maieste thocht thir thre persouns seueral thre granys like saull man ane wate hauand prince marrubianis ancient pepil bene quhilk anthemolus ilk wene defoulit faderis bed incestuoslie forlyne awin stepmoder ye also stout gemmel brether twa chylder sonnis vnto dawcia tymber mene thy brothir laryd amyd feild rutulian abide ye war sa like forme similitude na mycht discerne betuix quhare ye stude quhilk maner errour sic misknawing fader moder oft plesand thing seand thare childer sonny fatis strang hid preualy thik woddis amang bot fra auld elesus lay de yeildis vp breith wawland e fatall sisteris set hand anone gan young elesus dyspone euandrus wappinnis ilk stound destynate yone harnes cote armour spulye brycht quhilk werelie schynis yone knycht sall hing apoun ane aik fast bray god asking hard pray quhil elesus vnauisitlye cled scheild imaonis freynd fallow dere brist stude nakit armour gere quharia pallas dedly schaft resauit bot lasus wilfull syde haue sauit ane grete part oist list suffir sic fere boist slauchter made pallas deray companyeouns suld caucht mare affray ruschit lle first tene slew aba grete bargane sustene thikest rout preis thare maist tary wald ceis lusus sparpellit inuadis doun beting war barnage archadis doun beting eik war ethrurianis ye also feil bodyis troianis war put greikis vterance oistis semblit spere lance chiftanis ionedthe ionig feild hale poweris hendmest wardis swarmed yferes thik stale merrit wox rout one mycht ony turne hand weild wappin schute ane dart full douchteli pallas ta part enforcis greif fais tyde lausus resistis vthir syde thare age war fer indifferent maist semelie stature quhare thay went thay war excellent bewtie thay tway bot stude fortoun wele away wald nouthir suffir realme resort netheles mete samyn schort feild preif thare hardyment gouernour heuin omipotent lyst na way thole bilif eftar athir thame thare dedly fatis wy ane fer grete aduersare remanis anone doi follow vnder anys p quhow fei turnus young pallas quham folkis makis grete dolour mane dvring feruour bargane sa haly nymphe clepit inturna brothir turnus dyd monis exhorte succour lausus folkis support quhilk turnus spedy chare myd routis went sloppand thare beheld feris debatyng wyth pallas lo tyme desystturnus desiris techt pallas let pa al sic bargane quod ceis hye wyl set pallas enterly onelie none vthir wycht victory pertenis sic ane knycht glaidlie wald fader stude hereby interprise derne espie thus said feris command vodit feild al plane left land young pallas seand rutulianis withdraw feild sa swyith roume planis proude bidding prince kyng ameruellit ful gretely thing ferlie turnus behald ouer al bustuous body wald rollyng ene al corp hye thrawin luke fer begouth espye syne mouing fordwart sic wourdis hye ansuere turnus speichpallas answer thus carpis owthir thou quod ay belouit sall riche kinglie spulye triumphale quhilk sal rent mine aduersare sal renownit euermare ane excellent end maist glorius way thy boist mannance made v fader quham thou desiris besyde reputis elike quhow euer chance betyde say thus amyd plane furth flertis blude congelit archadane hertis turnus doun lepis twa quhelit chare bownis fast towartis aduersare like ane lioun hillis hicht amyd vail scharply gottin ane sicht sum proud bull horn plane addressand reddy mak bargane cummis bradand beist fast ane ling sic like wise turnus cunnyng quhen pallas saw cum nere mycht areik ane casting spere formest bownis tane flycht wod lioun ruschit fycht quhom arekis nerrest hand wythout reskew downe mawis brand bitand blade inuyroun amyd routis reddis large roume enrageit inflammyt thus yre throw oistis turnus proud syre quhilk new slauchter made socht ay prentand mynd e gudly pallas sa stout ying grete gentrice euander kyng chere feist hyme made ane strangere perodour al thing quhat manere ressauit tretit thankfully syne band freyndschip ally aithis sworne interchangit handis remembring tho promyses commandis amouit hete euer stynt foure young men quyk handis hynt borne war ciete hecht fulmon mony syne takin anone bred vpbrocht besyde flude vsens quham ettilles send then pallas like walkis obsequies strow funeral fire birnand treis gise blude prisoneris eftir auld rite mortall weris syne hynt eneas ane perrellus lance hand addressis fer furth land ane magus subtell sle iowkit vnder spere schaft schakand flew furth hede eneas samyn stede kneis grippit humelie pietuous voce syne thus begout cry thy dere faderis goist beseik gude beleif quhilk thou eik ascaneus vprising estate silly saul myne sa faynt mate thou sauf myne awne son fader dere haue house riche full mobillis sere quharin bedeluin lyis ane grete talent charge fyne siluer veschell quent forgeit pounsit wounder craftely ane huge wecht fynest gold tharby vncunyete yit ne neuir put werk sa thou saif thy pissance sa stark troianis glorie thare victorye sall na thing change dymynew tharby ane pure saule thus hingand ballance may sic diuisioun mak discrepance thus said silly magus vane quham enease ea answere answeris thus agane thy mony talentis fyne siluer gold quhilkis thou rehersand tald keip vnto thy small childer airis late thame bruke wele consent tharis interchange ransonyng perfay batal turnus done away laitlie hawbrek fyne ground doun hede declyne thocht humly besocht schupe say mekil al nocht hys pallat dust bedowyne stude body bathit hate blude enee oue weltis sayand thir wourdis wyth wyth troublit breist mynd inimicall ly thou thareeneas wordis wenit wicht thou ferefull vntyl euery wicht thy best belouit moder sall haue erd custome delf graif na thy bone honour syc cure thame lay faderis sepulture bot silence like egioun king gyandis quhilk thay ane hundreth armes handis fifty mouthis quham fyre schyne battall gigantyne incontrare iouis thunder fyre slaucht al mony drawin swerdis faucht clatterand bargane sa mony scheildis samyn wyse enrag ing throw feildis went eneas victor ouer hand fra tyme anys bedyit birnist brand wet hate rutuliane blude also ilk furie wod draif nypheus amyd breist bane suffir sustene thame sic feruoure felloun tene bot ruschit furth ane grete spere forganis thame sicht appere quham ligere carpis apoun hie thou seis diomedis stedis said yit achilles chare persauis draw thocht athir vniquest feild knaw yit troiane planis behaldis thou end thy age bargane sall maid thir landis ground sic wourdis vane vn semelie sound furth warpis wyde ligere fulichelie bot troiane baroun vnabasitlie na wourdis pres render agane bot fa let fle ane dart flame hit lutagus quhilk fra felt dynt schaft hinging scheild stynt bad driue hors char al fordwert streicht addrest feicht strekit furth left fute chare bot sone eneas spere reddy beneth schynand scheild law grundyn hede ilk thraw left flank lisk perfit tyte quhill clare ouer chariot sinyte ground weltis dede thrawis quhom wise soure wordis sawis pieteous eneas begouth schyde lutagus sayd forsoith tyde na slaw cours thy hors weldy thy carte rendrit thy inemye yit nane vane wrinchis gaistis quent thy chare constrenit bakwart went magre thyne wythdraw fais grippis lo thy fre wyll thou skippis ouer quhelis thy carte god wa leiffand renyeis hors al desolate beand said hors renyeis hynt tothir fey bruthir euer stynt lap fra cart lurkand pieteously vp heuand bare handis thus dyd cry troyane prynce lawly beseik thyneawne vertuisa humbyl supplication thewis meik thy parentis maist renowne syc ane child engendrit thou spare sylly wofull saul leyst haue reuth admyt request wyth wourdis fele thus gan requere enee last wyse made ansuere syc sawis war langayr thy mynde sterff behuffis le thou war vnkynd leif thy brother desolate hym allane na fallow samyn gate tharewych hirnys goist rypit wyth swerd amyd coist tyl hys hart stonndis pryk deith weltis ouer haldis vp breith thys dardane prynce vyctour thys sa mony douchty corpis brocht bere amyd planis ryddand large gate doi ane routand ryuererede spate hys dyntis wox hys fais agast ferefull drumly thunderis blast quhyl fynalie ascaneus young page remanent troyane barnage quhilkis war sayd besegeit vane thare strenth lesit taken plane p iuno rycht quently causis turnus ane fenyete figure persewand enee ilk stound awin fre volounte ioue callis spaceiupiter grantis yit restis wil lenth hys lyffeiuno turnus tyme quhilk grant quod bot gif sa beis vnder thy requeist mare hie pardoun lurkis wald thou ceist gif thou wenys al victorye batall wourdis fatal destany grounschis thou gif concede say quhat force thocht thou dede woldest repreif ratyfy agane turnus lyffe ane lang tyme suld remane bot approchis innocent knycht ane fereful end sal dede dycht sawis ar voyde verite wald god rather suld dissauit war bot fals drede thou list thou mycht dede thy fatal promyssis thy statutis strange bettir purpois translate change fra sche thir wourdis sayd ilk tide doun heuin sche lete hir selfin yde driuand ane tempestuous wynd al eik behynd within ane cloude myst circulit clene sche throw bownit furth thys quene towart troyane oistis planys tentis socht laurentanis goddes furth ane bois cloude liknes enee schape ane schroude ane vode figure strenth curage bald quhilk wounderus monstoure behald troyane wappinnis armour grathis sche scheild helme tymbret set hye semblant like eneas godly hede thareto eikis sche euery stede quent fenyeit wourdis faynt counterfete voce mynd ony vthir consate fenyeis eik hir counterfete pasis sic lik thay say diuers placis wrachis walkis goistis ar dede slepy dremes fra stede stede fleand sweuyn makis illusiouns quhen mennys mynd oft driuylling gronys forefront feild rycht haltanlie curagious vnder scheild musturis thys ymage wyth dartis kene aggreuit turnus child prouocand bargane ire turnus tho al hate fire figure inuade thare grete dispite ane quhirland dart let fle bot ilk schaddow sum dele addred turnit gaif bak fled turnus wenyng enee tane flycht awounderit selcouth sycht wythin hys mynd ane vane comfort caucht cryis loude quhiddir fleis thou enee leif neuer schame thus desolate waist thy new alliance promist haist lauinia spousinge chalmer hand al ilk regioun land quhilk thou safer soucht ouer se richt hand sal sauyn gif quod sic wourdis schoutand persew ay glymmerand brand schuke schew na thyng persauand myrth blis away quyte wynd bewaffit cais thare stude ane meikle schip tyde hir wail ioned til ane sthore rolkis syde wyth plankis wyth briggis laid land entre reddy graithit wele thay fand quhilk schip osynus king wy come laitely ciete clusis thiddir went wrayth schado enee semyt abasit fast fle hid hir derne vnder hichis therin na slaware turnus haistis hym ryn delay spedis schip ran ouer brig inwyth burd skip skars enterit fore castell quhen saturnus douchter saw hir tyme befell sone cabyl sonder smitis sche fra schore draif schip throw se bot turnus absent thus samyn houre eneas serchis throw amyd stoure renk quham euer met lay dede full mony ane man kelit stede tharewyth lycht fenyeit goist fra tyme schyp chargit fra coist na langer sekis hirnes hyr hyde bot flew vp samyn tyde desoluit ane dyrk cloud mene sessoun force wyndis loud turuus fer furth amid depe se dryue dyd behald tho belyue ignorant quhat wyse thys chance wrocht hys lyffe sauyng nothing roucht wyth handis ioned vp towartis heuyn sic wourdis furth brade wyth drery steuin almychty faderturnus oracion iupiter heuinnys hye thou reput sic wyse confusit schame myne offence wyl suffir sic torment penance quhidder driue quhens cummyn quhat maner eschewing fleing haue mummyn quhat estate sall returne agane sall neuir se wallis laurentane euir est tentis sall se quhat may yone douchty man defalt falland fey ground quhat sal allace woful stound quhilk land thocht ane thousand tymes steruit may swelly depe haue seruit bot ye wyndis rather haif mercy rolkis craggis swak schip end bot thare feildis laurentyne vnkend haldis body myna brym stoure stound mezentius like strenthy sanglerea comparison bore quham houndis quest mony quhryne rore doun driuing hychtis made descend quhilk mony wynter fore defend vesulus cauld montane hie ouerheildit wyth mony fir tre bustous swyne fed wele bredis amang buskis rank risp redis beside laik laurent mony yeris quhen betrappit fra hys feris amyd hunting ralis nettys standis bay vp birsis settis graissand tuskis wyth austerne fyrie ene spaldis hard harsk awful tene nane al hunt mene thare present aggreue strenth hardyment dar approcheing wythin bit ere bot stand nd fer dreich wyth dart spere assouerit reak beist assayis felloun schoutis bustuous cryis brayis nane vthir wyse stude tuskane rout stalwart knicht mezentius thocht thay iust caus wraith fede thare nane thaym durst hym put dede curage drawin swerd hand hymtyl assayle mach apoun land bot wyth takillis casting dartis fer thay warp hym durst nane cum nere wyth huge clamour infestis tyde vnabasit euery syde behaldis girnand ful propir tene scheild choppit schaftis bedene furth ancient boundis chorit tho cumming ane greik quhilk clepit arto fugitiue lusty hete left spousale treuth plicht vncomplete quham mezencius saw amyd rout greuand sore werioure sterue stout saw plesand plume set hicht trymbrel eik purpoure bricht quhilk treuth plicht luf bare syng like ane hungry lyoun rummissing constrenit hys empty rageand maw beistis dennys circuland al raw gif cais espies ane swyft ra young hart springand tyndis twa ioyfull bradis theron dispituusly wyth gapeand goule vprysis hy lokkeris lyand nek rouch al beistis bowellis thrymlis trouch hurkilland thareon quhare remanit stude gredy gammes bedyis rede blude samyn wyse mezentius rycht baldly mydwart hys fais rout ruschyt hye doun smytis fey atroun amyd oist ded thraw yaldand vp goist smate wyth hys helys ground matalent brokin schaftis wyth hys blude bysprent thys ilk mezentius eik dedenyete tosla orodes quhilk flocht knaw quhylk frawart went repute na wyse hys entent sic steand wound hys bake vnwarnist quhen na defence micht make bot ran met hys rais athir man assemblit face face orodes prettik mare al bot tothir dedis armes mare stout erth ouerthrawin fere possand hym wyth stalwart spere apoun set fute thus sayd feris beis baith blyith glaid lo ane grete partye lei lyis erde douchty orodes feris samyn rasit vp ane cry wyth ioyus sound sygne victory blew prise triumphale deith bot orodes yeldand vp breith vnto mezentius carpis thus hye vnreuengit thou sall neuir victor wele wate sone sal wrokin na al thy proude wourdis thou spokin thou sal endure syc ioy bot siclyke chancis sembland ennoy abidis thocht thou neuir sa bald samyn feild sall thy dede corp withhald quham mezentius smyland sayd tene thou sal de first quhat euer foresene prouidit almychty ioue quod quham fader goddis king men clepe sayand thus schaft ilk thraw furth wound body draw orodes hard reist doi oppres cald irny slepe deithis stres vp breith yeld anone ful richt wyth ene closit euirlesting nycht cedicus al trinschit alchatous sacratoure ground laid hydaspus rapo ane archade partheneyus slane or wounder big blude bane mesapus kelit stout clonyus erithathes lithaonius formest lyggand erd ouer raucht hedstrang hors ane fal caucht lathaonius eik ane futeman lichtit fute slew melle aganis went ane man arge hate lytyus bodyn wyth spere targe way valerus gud nedis inexpart douchty cldaris dedis recounterit put dede salius ane troyane samyn stede atronius slew nealtis expert schute steand arrow casting dart quhilk inuadis ane man war slew lyus wyth schot beand far p eneas young lausus sla quhilk f ed hys fader hurt bargane thus aufull mar equale brand sorow rasit apoun athir hand huge slauchter made sere wonndis wyde thay kele bete doun euery side samin feild thay fall fere baith victouris thay vincust nowthir partie wistmonye slane partyis nowthir saif self quhare away fle goddes iouyis heuinly hald compassioun reuth behald wraith ire athir fichtis sic distres rang amang mortall wichtis venus towart troyane side uke tent aganis quham full matalent saturnus dauchter iuno full bald towart partye aduersare behaldis paile furoure thisiphone walkis wod wroith amydwart melle bot principale mez engreuit ane grete spere quharewith feil mischeuit went brangland throw feild allone al bustuous hidduous orion quhen fu e wod throw mekylse scherand streme schuldderis hie aboue wallis flude apperis like ane anciant aik tre mony yeris grew apoun sum mountane oppis hycht semand hie euery mannis sicht quhilk thocht rutis sprede ground sydis crop vpstracht amyd cloudis hydis siclike mezentius musturis feild wyth huge armour baith spere helme scheild aganis quham eneas fast hyis fra tyme amyd rout hym espyis tothir vnabasit al reddy thare cummyng douchty aduersare abydis stoutly fermyt force massalie vpstude wyth bustuous cors mesurand hys e al large spayis mycht thraw ane casting spere thus sayis rycht hand fleand dart mot quhilk cais verray god assistyng schot beseik awow promittis eik sing trophe triumphale meith louyt son lausus cleith spulye al harnes rent quod younder rubaris body fals enee thus sayd fra hand ilk tyde casting dart fast birrand lattis glyde fleand stlentis eneas scheild syne staudand fer roume yonde feild smat wourthy achores ilk thraw betuix bowellis ribbis law anthores ane grete hercules feris come arge lusty yeris inherdand euander arthade duellyng residence made palentyne ciete italiane vnhappely liggis thus doun slane ane wound dynt within fycht addre ssit towart ane vthir mycht deand beheld heuynnys large behald swete cuntre arge reuthful eneas kest spere quhilk throw mezentius armour dyd schere throucht gird arge platit thryis wyth stele throw co chit lynnyng euery dele thrynfald playis bullis hydis law doun flank dynt abydis bot bereft nowthir lyffe ne mycht eneas quhilk expert ficht ioyfull quhen mezentius blud saw furth hynt hys swerd hang law feruently towart hys fa pa quhilk dynt sum dele astonist quhen lawsus saw auenture wepit wale sare hys fader dere wo begone become thys lusty man salt teris fast ouer hys chekis ran forsoith sal ouer slip stede thy hard myschance lausus fatale dede thy mayst douchty actis bellical fresche youngkere maist ding memorial sal rehers gif ony fayth may geuin sa grete dedis antiquite mezentius menyeit drew abak harland leg quharin schaft stak quhare went beris ouer feild hys inemyis lance fast fixit scheild betuix thaym ruschis young lawsus amyd thare wappinnis sterne curageus self set sustene fycht vnder eneas richt hand rasit hycht reddy smyte ane dedely wound insteppis baldlie ilk stound bytand brand vpheuit keppit resist stent grete ene feris followis ane felloun schout quhil mezentius feild wan defend couerit sonny scheild thay cast dartis thikfald thare lord heild wyth schaf schot flanys grete plente perturband thare feirs aduersare enee al enragit souir targe erekkit thare vnder hym haldis cloisly dekkit lyke sum tyme cloudisa comparison bristis attanis schoure furthyettand hoppand halestanys al plowman thare hynes hy fleis croftis feildis eik trauelloure yound vnder wald lur kand withdrawys sum souir hald owthir vnder wattir brayis bankis dern sum craggis clift depe cauerne lang schoure lestis plane may quhen son schynes agane exerce hys iournay werk al fast siclike ene wyth schot dartis cast ouer held vnbeset ilk syde quhill preis batall styntis tyde al thare force sustenit deray repreuand lawsus thus begouth say mannysand wyth brand blude rede quhiddir haistis thou sa fast apoun thy dede quhow dar thou vndertak ficht syc interpryse quhilk aboue thy micht thou art wise thy tendir hart quod reuthfull mynd dissauis bot al young lausus al hale wald wyse ceis eneas assale heiar rais wraith felloun ire ilk manfull troyane lordly syre eik fatale sisteris tho dede wymplit vp lausus lettir threde eneas stokkis stiff brand throw youngkere hard vp tyl hand swerd made mannysyng boist throw gyrd gentyl body coist tergate peirsand hys armoure lycht eik coit goldin thredis bricht quhilk moder span conclude bosum al fillit hait blude sone eftir spret lyffe furth went doun goistis law sad entent left body dede hyne dyd pa bot quhen anchises son feirs eneas beheld vult contenance deing swete vissage sua dede thrawyng becummyn wan pale dyuers wyse sychit profoundlye owthir twis thryis draif abak hys hand reuch hynt sa mynd eftir dynt ymage hys faderly piete emprentit wise said doughty yinglyng wourthy menit wourthy bewallit complenit quhat sal reuthful compacient enee sa grete louabil dedis render quhat may yelde sufficient sic naturale inborne hardyment thyne armour quharof sum tyme thou reiosit leif ay eniosit vnto thy parentis handis sepultre beleif entirit quod gyf sic manere tryumphe coist may thame plesure elli thy goist bot thou vncilly chyld sa wyll rede counfort wyth thy lamentabyl dede thou ouer machit art thus lyis slane gretest eneas handis twane syne feris repreif chyde thay sa lang delayit besyde makand na haist bere corp away self betuix handis tway dede body vp lyftis fra ground rede blude new grene wound besparkit yallow lokkis brycht ayre kemmyt addressit rycht p fra mezentius knew young lausus decei reuenge lyfe loist pr mene sessoun fader feris doun flude syde tyberis stanchit woundis water weschand swete blude body helme stele besyde hang wele ne apoun ane grane branche ane grene tre vthir wechty harnes gude nede lay gers besyde hym mede crafty chosen verlottis ful sore woundit dout stude lenand wery nek bonis ouer ane bowand tre wyth sary grones hys wele kemmyt berde hingand doun ful straucht vpon breist vntil girdil raucht fele tymes lausus menys prayand ful oft micht saufelie se mony messengeris vnto send wythdraw hym feild defend abyde na langare bargane schaw hym quhat sorow fader tane bot lausus dede feild hys woful feris caryit apoun ane scheild wepand sa grete ane man brocht ground disco fest wyth sa grislie ane wound mezentius mynd consait ilk tyde suspekand harmes quhilkis war tho betyde fer considerit caus thare murnyng canois hare dust slyng mekil pouder fylland hasart hede baith handis samyn stede towart heuin vpheuis ane fary goddis sterne fast wary syne lenand sonnis corp thus cryis dere chyld tender get heir lyis sa grete appetitemtzetius lamentis sonnis dede delyte vnto wrechit lyfe sa ful ofsyte sufferit entir ony stede vnder fay handis thy dede lyfe salsit sa thy fader quhilk begat onely son dere suld saif leiffand eftir throw thay sa grisly woundis se allace vnto wrechit catyue thyng myne exile last bannassyng becummyn hard vnsufferabil stound deith panys lamentabil depe ingrauyn myne hart vnsound smytyn wyth mortal wound self man caus thy dede wyth trespas chyld euery stede filit glore honour thy name thy hie renowne bespottand wyth schame inuy haitrent myne awne pepil thare hale assent expellit sceptre ryng addettit misdoing vnto cuntre haue sufferit pane aucht wourthy haue bene flane hane yeld wikkit saul myne maner torment pyne till amend offence feid ha leif allace thou art dede yit want men cumpany nouthir licht lyffe clerenes skye bot sone sall thame leif part therfra sayand thus samyn mynd full thra rasit vp apoun woundit determyt reuenge de thocht violence sare smert maid vnfery yit stalwart hert curage vndekyit gude innede bad ga fethe rhebus riall stede quhilk wourschip comfort hale support fais till assale hors euery grete iourney hame fra feild victor eschapitt quham mezentius ony mare abayde seand sted droupand sad thus sayd rhebus twa le fit lang yfere gif mortall wichtis erde ony tyme may reput lang quod outhir day beis thou reuengit lausus dolorus deith wreik schame sall v victor bringin hame yone bludy spulye eneas hede gif na strenth force stede suffar ony way sal feild samyn de baith two thou moist forcy stede louit fole wise beleif thou may tho e ony vtheris commandment leist dedenete gif war schent tyl obey ony maister lord troiane say thus ful cowartlie anone stede bekend held schoulder plat eis vpon bak doun sat baith handis fillit dartis kene helme hede birnist bricht schene bone quhilk tymbret buklit lyke til ane lokkerit mane mony fa sic array swift cours furth steris stede draif melle depe hart boldynnys felloun sthame mixt dolour anger defame feruent lufe son yong age caching furius rage tharto also persuadis ficht hors wele knawin hardiment mycht sic po nt throwout routis al mychty voce thryis eneas call eneas hard cry wele knew glaid thareof towart persew prayand sayis fader goddis hie eik mychty appollo grant thou wald begyn bargane land mell meit hand hand thus carpis sterne lause tary furth steppis mete aduersary bot mezentius se cummand cryit anone bad stand thou maist cruell aduersare said quhat wenis thou affray boist sen thou son bereft day quhilk onlie manere way quharby thou mycht ouercum destroy sen haif tynt warldly ioy nowthir abhor dede sterue fecht rek ocht ony goddis mycht desyst ceis boist mannace cummin de ilk place bot fyrst bryng thir rewardis quod wyth word fa ane dart lete fle eftir ane vthir cast syne ane vthir fixit fast hym prekand ane cumpas large bot al thir dintis sufferit goldin targe thryise left half fast weir woud eneas rade quhare stude thyk wyth handis swakkand dartis kene thryis troiane prince ouer al grene tyl stalwart stelit scheild stekand lyke ane hare wod dartis bare last ennoyit thys deray irksum trasing iowking delay commerit wox sa mony dartis vane thus oft draw furth cast agane machit time fale wyth hys fa men bargane inequale quhilk ay ane auantage flocht full mony thyngis reuolwit thocht syne man ruschit tene forehede betuix horsys ene kest spere al force mycht vpstendit stalwart stede one hicht helis flang vp doun swakkis knycht sone wyth ane felloun fare founderis fordwart flatlingis spald ouerquhelmyt man hys feyld vnfald latynis eik pepil troianis heuynnis dynlyt ane schout atanis eneas gird aboue ane braide hynt furt swerd forther thus saide quhare mezentius sa sterne quhare stout feirs curage berne quham mezentius ilk prince tyrrhene fra mycht alifting vp ene se heuynnys lycht draw breith richt mynd agane recouerit haith thus answerismezentius last anseuer afor decht thou dispitefull fo quharto chydis thou reprochand mannassis dede slanchter thinke na velany sic wise come feild stand aw swelt vnder scheild beleif na freyndschip thy handis nane sic trety sauthning commandis son lausus band vp perfay bot ane thing beseik pray gif ony plesure may grantit beild till aduersaris lyis vincust feild knaw suffir body haue ane spulture erd graue knaw standand stede folkis bitter haitrent grete feid defend thare furour requere grant corp besyde sonny fere sum tumbe entirit sayand thus knawand must de ene persauit birnist brand throu gorgeit went eneas hand within armour schortlie strokis wappinnis thay thare nouthir spere bud geis staf polax swerd mace takin cheuelry fecht mindis suld haue iust intencioun ground batal groundit apoun richt thou list make discencioun seik occasioun contencioun bot ripe querelthe iust cause war suld cosiderit al wyse pryce discus plane wranges redres suld vndertane na conquest reif stayt pensioun speke mortall vertewis hardyment rathir diuyne myne entent warldly strenth febill import nt goddis sicht insufficient psalmist sais god content mannis stalwart lymmys strenth cors bot thame traisting ther fors askand mercy dredand iugement strang fortitude quhilk hardyment clepe aboue quhilk vertew souerane ac ording princis heich magnanymyte ane boet setfort tud ful hardenes towar ne betuix vice twane quhame fule hardines clepit tane vndertakis al perrillis auyse tothir namyt schamefull cowardise voyde curage dolf ony stane first hardy mesure tyme resoun geuis na cure dout castis bot thinkis sure nocht may suffir hete indure tothir proues sa pure euer standis fere felloun dred neuir dar vndertak ane douchty dede bot doi curage manhede samyn smure first soundis towart vertew sum dele hardy couth auisit hardyment tothir na feile may curage cowartnes agre fortitude compt euery gre aristotil ethikis doi expres wald contene ouer lang proces quhareof vthir cheuelry carp wyl gyf cristis knichtis lyst v aucht promyst font man bide baldlydiuyne cheuelrye neuir fle nouthir abasit tepit yit blont cowardes eschew first dont paul witnessis nane sall wyn croun bothe quhilk duelie makis redy boun stand wichtely fecht forefrount quhay sal wyn croun mede say euerlastand blys fyre eternale nedelinges moist thay drede crist gospell sayis wi quha bydis contrar gif thou aganis god art thou wageour vnto lucifere god saue v sic ane assaltis couatice estate aganis quham ful perrellus debate fais familiare bene full quent knaw leif thy flesche maister thy cors leif warld ay remane resist freyndis slicht al thy force ancient enemy werst ane ane thousand wilis mony ane trane kendillis oft flesche birnand hete causit wrechit plesance sem ful swete nocht fals warld makis fane thy fa aduersare principale promyssioun wald expel land ane schore think haly marthyris went think pane hel endles glore think lord rude rent think thou fle fra thou art schent think al thou sufferis vntil pane nocht think precius price thy saul bocht aye vnto wourd thy mynd bent fele bene thy fais fers ful slicht bot thou stal wart campioun knycht feild grace foresaid armour bricht thay mayd de bait thame lithlie ilk ficht fre thine actioun sa wicht nane may peirs thou resist stande becum thou towart crawdoun recriand consent cry cok thy dede dicht think fa waik impotent may vincus nane bot thame list ouercum sall neuer ouerset thy consent eith ane strang melle syne yeild thy fa ony quhy towartlye tak bak fele na sall nane obtene hie victorie le thay sustene bargane douchtely sa quha perseueris end ane conquerour ane campioun euir kend palme tiumphe honour glorie maist vnsilly kind fortoun haue bene happy boecius techis v haue bene welth hartis blys decayit wo richt quha vertuus fallis tharefro verray reasoun mallewrus hat yit grace fre volunte may recouer merit agane also say grace quhen thou art grace thou may eik grace grace ay bot quhen thou fallis syn therfra allace merite thou gettis neuer yit quhen thou deulie disponis tharfore doand thare may done gudnes eternal lord alsone restoris merite grace erlis glore hale thym erite thou tofore fall say thy werkis meritabil restorit ar agane baith grete small grace thareto quhilk sa profitabyl thou thareby eik merite art habyll bot ilk gre grace thou gettis thou sa sone quhil forthirmore war tharefore fal bot standis stabyll lyke quha offendit lord lang tofore trew seruandis bene syne agane becummys ane accord maister althocht hys lord wald mene ald seruyce yit netheles wene sal sone tender war tharwith kepe fra snare tyne labour thank betwene exemple takis prince enee fatal cuntre behest sa feil dangeris sustenit land se sic strife stoure oft spere reist quhil realme conquest bayth west ei sen al ane temperale ring preis v wyn kinrike ay lesting addres v fast till attene feist may callit sayis sanct augustyne delicate ouer esy christin knicht refusis thole trauell sturt orpyne debait wenys obtene ficht wyn feild neuir preif thy mycht war nyce thing thy king christ batell quhat sufferit catine wicht lyis thou eis thy prince bargane fell eschames sleuth cowardise seand thir gentilis thir paganis auld ensew vertew eschew euery vice sa schorte spulye mar gise dvring quhile furth sey spring fresche aurora brycht dawing enee albeit basty thochtfull curis constrenit twiching sepulturis folkis new slane berying prouide ane tyme maist accordyng thus exhortis enee feris syne chiftanis lowkit war quhilkis glaidsum werren thys ioyus fare douchty men quod wourthy weris gretest partyeneas co fortis folkys exhortyng batellagane werkis efferis bene endit sa tyme cumming fere drede ar passit ony thing thir bene spulye first werelie wede reft proude king handis dede lo mezentius vincust lyis doun bet wallis laurent yet way made kyng latyne wend tharefore addres myndys attend armes werefare euery ane prouidyng consatis bargane ye reddy na delay may floppin stonis ane vthir day bot awin sleuth lak gud forsicht gyf ye vnwarnist beis callit sicht al sone first god omnipotent sum signis takinnis lyst consent ensenyeis baneris vp hynt al yonkeris met swerdis dynt thare tentis conuoyit array se ye al reddy delay mene quhile let v erd haue corpsis fallowis vnbegraue quhilk onlie honour haldin daynte acheron lawest helles se pa sayd thay saulis vailyeand quhilk habundance chare blude besprent conquest v realme apoun sic wyse honour thare funeral seruice wourschip fynale last rewardis bot first al corpsis thay lardis vnto euandrus dolorus ciete young pallas body send mon quham wantand na vertew prowes woful day v bereft expres ane woful slauchtereneas lametis deth fred palas caucht allace thus sayd wepand salt teris ouer face syne tuke vayage towart ilk stede quhare pallas lifles corp liggand dede quham ancient acetes thare kepe flottrit berde teris bewepe quhilk atetes tofore squyare king euander ciete parrha cum archadye tyme send cumpany dere foster child cure bot happy auenture corp alhale multitude seruitouris commouns troianis stude dolourus phrigiane wemen thare gise hare doun schaik pieteous spraichis cryis bot fra enterit eneas bald within portis large hald ane huge clamour thay rasit womenting beting thare breistis quhill lift reyng loude thare wofull bewaling haboundis palice dynnys resoundis prince fra behald snaw quhite visage pallas bald hede vphald self sustene eik gapand dedely wound sene maid speris hede rutuliane amyd sneith fare slekit breist bane teris brist hys ene thus plenit douchty childa lamentable moue palace dede maist wourthy menit fortoun inuyit sa far eft ouer wele cummyne thus art thou bereft sa thou suld se ouer reyng said yit ane victor prosperite vnto thy faderis ciete haue retoure sic promys hecht lattir houre thy fader euandrus quhen departing last embrasit send conqueis ane large empire dredand eik lordelie sire v monist war auyse becaus men quham ware bald sterne said hand wyth bustuous folk wele stryfe durst stand certis leuand hope vane thy prosper returnyng hame agane perchance doi mak prayer offerandis chargeing altaris oft awin handis bot lifles child quhilk aw na thing vnto goddis heuinly ryng womentene menand tenderly vane honour accompanyis fey vnhappya p tyfull exclamamation pallas kynge archadian thy sonnis dede corpis cruelly slane thou sall behald allace panis strang ouer hamecome thou desyrit lang sall ouer tryumphe lang abaid se thy awin sona consol cion bere tre laid ha quhat promys gret faith bot euander beis wraith thou sall se thy son drife abak wyth schameful woundis caucht bak thou fader war alyue day suld neuer haue lak na pray desert deit ane schamefull deith wyth honour yald breith bot netheles quhat harme full wayis large supporte ha quhat beild supple tint ausonia ryng grete dele loist ascaneus ying p pallas corpis tyl euander sent wyth al honour accordyng hys tyrement qvhen bewaled manere woful corp bad lift bere hym send ane thousand men hye walit euery rout cumpany conuoy hym falloschip last honour funerall wourschip present lamenting fader confort murnyng thocht smal solace regrate quhilk sa huge bot estate according wele sic thyngis suld quhen wichtis mycht rew se sum eneas feris besely flokis plet thaym preissisa lang narracion contenyng honour pallas funeral entyrment smal wikkeris beild vp ane bere sowpill wandis brounys sere bound wyth syouns twistis sle smal rammel stobbis akin tre thir beddis beildit funerall littetis sic tumbis dede corp efferis wyth grene burgeouns braschis fare wele thay gan ouerheild stintis euery dele amyd quhilkis blumes apoun ane bing strowit ful hie thay laid pallas ying ligging tharon semely se fresche flouris schynand bewty newlie pullit vp stalkis smal tendir fyngeris damysell soft violet doi freschely schyne purpoure floure hate acinctyne quham al thocht erd moder wyth sap nurissis comfortis hir lap yit schyne cullour figure glaid al went bewty defaid eneas syne twa robbis furth gart fald riche purpoure styf burde golde ful dolorusly eneas cled young pallas body fynale last honour lokkis haris selfe houre quhilkis war brynt assis cald tothir habit fold aboue al rewardis mony ane conquest batel laurentane hale hepis send bad thay suld tak gude kepe attend lede pray perordoure pompusly feil horsis gaif thame wappinnis eik vtheris precius gere reft famen prisoneris also quham tak sendis handis bound behind thare bak quhilkis obsequyis intyrement infernale goistis suld sent thare bludis schede gise funeral famb strinklit sacrifyce bad capitanis dukis al signe trophe pomp triumphal grete pykis bare trene syplyne square cled wyth armour thare aduersaris wryte hing thareon baith al sum name thare inemys ouercum furth led silly achates ouerset age sorow mycht ceis bludy yth awin breist feistis nalis face renus breistis oft doun fallis speldit erde wyth mony goule ane ful pietuous rerd furth war led riche cartis nanys sprent wyth blude rutulianis eftir come aethon werely stede dispuleyit harnessing wede wepand went woman mycht haue sene grete teris flodderit face ene ane bare helme ane vthir bare spere remanis hys harnes gere sic riche girdil coit armour turnus victor byreft floure furth haldis syne drey cumpany troianis tyrrene dukis thaym wofull archades signe dolour weris scheildis reuersit doun turnit thare speris eftir perordour thay bene fu th passit euery cumpany eneas tho gan stentyn abaide wyth ane pietuous regret thus sayd horribill batellis thire samyn weris til vtheris funeral womentyng teris callis v then may follow thyne entirement behald se dew ay pallas belouit best farewele euer intil eternal rest na mare sayd bot went towart new troy enterit therin wyth teris ennoy p eneas vnto latynis gaif u lf dayis respit dede corpsis graif war cummin fra kyng latynis ciete embassiatouris wyth branche olyue tre besekand fauouris beneuolence wald suffir caryit thence thay corpis dede quhilk feildis broun lay strowit thare swerd bet doun thame restore agane gentrice suffir thame begrauin assuring thame thare mycht led na vincust folkis lifles micht stere prayit spare thare peopil sic mischance quhilom clepit freyndis acquentance quhen eneas heynd curtas gude thare peticioun sa ressonabyl vnderstude man fulfillit bounte thare hale desire ful gladlie grantit thir eik vnto thaym thus sayd latine folkiseneas ansuer lattynis quhat mysfortoun vnglaid inuoluit sa vnhappy ye chace v away freyndis dere desire ye peace bot thaym bene loist martial fate slane oist forsoith til al leuand wald glaidly grant samyn say neuir hidder cummin war perfay stede fatis hecht ay resting place promouit herbry ne na werefare pepill lede bot king confederance vp geif rathir settin al beleif turnus vassalege hie prowes thocht equale ganand war ge thys turnus brekar pece auenture de preis gif pretendis batale ane brand end troianis land expel semyt hym vnder scheild wapinnis recounter feild nane bot ane v war left leuand quhois lyffe god list withhald ouer rycht hand haldis al lifeles banis corp wrechit cietezanis birne bery eftir awin gyse sayis eneas troiane war wyse speich wounderit war thay kepit thare silence wist say bot ather towart turnus mare behald fallow ane stare eldest man amang thaym fynalie clepit drances ful grete inuy young turnus alway infest auld malice cryme manifest begouth tospeik ansuere thus agane huge grete thy famedrances oracion thou duke troyane bot fer greter may espye thy dedis armes thy cheuelrye wyth quhat louyng equale may compare goddis heuin aboue quhidder sall fyrst extoll wounder thy grete gentri sa iust equyte grete force labour bellicall glaidly forsoith hamewart bare sall vntyl oure natiue boundis ciete thir sa grete sygnis humanite gif ony chance fynd way sall fully euer may conione wyth kyng latyne hy turnus quhare list go seyk ally furthir eik wele lykis v help rayis fatall massy wall bere apoun schulderis war ioye thir stone grete thys new werk troy thus sayd drances remanent thare cryis wyth hale voce consent twelf dayis trewistrewis taken ii dayes thay band stanche debate kepe pece weris sequestrate throw woddis thir holtyes troyanis latynis samyn quhare thaym list wanderis dangere hie eschis soundis thare dyntys rude scharp stelit ax doun weltit ar mony granand strax firris rekand sterne hye mekill sillis warren tre wyth wedgeis propppis bene diuide strang gu ceder al schid ne ceis furth al murnyng fillis sche euander king pallice ciete quhilk late fore schewin pallas latyum land sa victorius sayis sche lo brocht bere archades ruschit portis fere euery wicht handis hynt al tite thaym adionis thare folkis sare wepand quham matronus behald sic wyse dulfully went kyngis palice dolorus toun euery strete way wyth pyetuous skrykis glouling fillit thay na force euander mycht refrene bot amyddis thaym wyth grete disdane ruschis plenyeand woful manere fel grufe aboue dede pallas bere wepand waland hert wald brek embrasit hym na wourd mycht speke skars last wyth grete murmour soundis lyke swift wattir stremys clere sum tyme routand men fer may quhare stoppit wyth thir stanys round riuerys brute brokyn sound bry ellyis ouer thyr demmyt lynnys bankis endlang al fludis dymmys bot eftir thare mudis mesit thare wauerand wourdis stanchit sic bere reuerence first blissand goddis mycht king thus carpis trone hicht latyne pepil forsoith wald alga bene laitinis os fer bettir wele wate full lang auisit twiching commoun wele materis sic ane poynt apoun wise counsele assembil auyse quhat fais aduersaris ar boun besiege wallis toun cietezanis moue ledis hand ane inportune quhilk vnganand aganis folkis goddis clan discend bene inuincibil wele defend bargane may thame irk tyre thocht thay vincust war bayth man syre may thay resist ne withdraw melle gif ony hope confidence cheuelry etholianis quhilkis naplis diomede remanis thare men armes thidder send sic traist away defend lat euery man awne self haue hope bot febill sic traist ye grope eik eue clere ye may se grete perrell proplexite vther materis lyis standis sic thingis bene brade amang handis wyll accus argew na wicht alhale force strenth mycht ficht exercit wate sene floure pissance realme sterue stoure wyll breuely end schort wourdis mak vnto kend doutsum purpois mynd remanis attendence gif harknes attanis haue besyde tyber tuskane flu e ane auld feild vnproffitabill rude far strekand west boundis quhare remanis cecil pepil quhilkis clepit ar sitanis folk armitane rutuly ground sawis full vnthriftely scharp plewis steil stokkis sere thare hard hillis hirstis till ere thir wild bolti hat also faynt pastoure doi thir beistis go cuntre band hillis hie sa full rochis pynnakillis se lat geif amyte concord troyanis eneas thare lord syne offer thame equale trety condigne peri call thame thys ryng samyn lat tham duell gif thay haue sic desire italy lat thame beild thare ciete wallis square bot gif thay list elli quhare othir coislis pepil wend thare duelling place ay apprehend possibil boundis thay may depart then wend away twys ten schippis lat v beil agane strang tymmer treis italiane gif thay ald complete may land ther lyis redy strand thare schippis noumer maner lat thame commaund sall furnis irne graith werkmen wrichtis schippis langis richtis forther eik likis quod er wourdis thys prince enee conferme freyndschip pece ane hundreth gay ambassatouris le gretest large douchty king thou askis counsele said mater quhilk semes nouthir dirk doutsum full clere mysteris auisis bene pepil hale grantis thay wate quhat fortoun schawis quhat estate matteris standis bot thay ar arth schaw quhisperand amangis thame thay stand sic aw bot caus gif thame liberte speik way boist thare breith may breik mene quhais vnhappy werde fraward theuis dede erde sa mony chief chiftanis dukis lyis forsoith sall say furth myne auise thocht braik boist wappinnis doith awate manace de dedis may se expres ciete halely plungit distres quhilkis made assay troyanis strenth stall sa sone away hauand assurance withdraw fle armes doi boist heuynn y hie thou al thare best riall king thir giftis eikis ane thing vnto thir presendis wise wourdis sere troyanys thou bid say bere eikys ane gift lat neuir demyt bustuousnes ony man dant bot thy dochter thou fader gude vnto yone gentill prince whurthy blude geuin thy son law wy wourthy sic ane wedlokis knyt vp pece mare disseuerance eternall band alliaunce gif sa grete dreddour drede haue within myndis breistis quod turnus dar sic thing lat v welefare ryng beseik tharfore hale intent requier wald grant consent king fre volunte mycht vse proper dewite wele public land desire na wise thareto gane stand turnus hede causere verely thir myscheuois grete italy quhare sa feil syis plane perrellis thir silly wretchit cietezanis warpis thou nane hope welefare haue pece halile require giddir lauinia schene may quhilk pand plege dar say pece kepit violate forsoith quhilk thy consate thou fenys thy euyll willare commoun wele sa mot cum refuse gude brother bot lo formest vthir humelie beseiking require haue mercy lord thyne awne freyndis dere lat thy stout mynde go thy way lak ane mare strang rebute driue bak dede corp bet doun ynew haue sene large feidis boundis betwene left desolate waist induelleris bot gif thy fame gret renoune thou steris gif thy breist sa hie curage mycht thou consauit think wicht gif sic wise hald riall suld thy drowry riche gift dotal thou betis hert sa dere vndertak thing end addres thy body baldly spare recounter agane thy aduersare intent turnus al lyfe may weild kingis douchter wyfe dolf curage lede doun strowit feildis dede cumpanyis vnberyit bewalit bot thou feild sa fele assayit gif ony strenth thou hardiment marcial prowes stering thine entent thy cuntre aganis richt behald thy sa prouokand ficht younder al reddy make party gude delay mare manfully go tude p turnus dran speche commonit sare rycht subtelly allegeis contrare feirs mind urnus bald syre sic sawis kindillytturnus oration agany drances hait fyre sichand richt sore depe breist anone thir wourdis pronouncis ane pietuos grone drancis forsoit quod euer thou bene large mekil speche weil sene quhen batel desiris werk hand counsel sittand first thou vpstand bot wourdis suld court fyllyt set thou grete tharm ful euill wyllit haltand wourdis fleand quhen thou assouerit art al dangere sa lang strenthy wallis gude inemies debarrit doi exclude quhil fowsyis forteres kinnis ouer bludy spate ge tharefore trump vp blaw furth thine eloquence thou wont make thy defence bot thou may drances mine auyse reproche fere cowardise quhen thy richt hand batal stede sa mony hepis troianis laid dede quhen thou takinnit sa vnwourthely signe tropheal fild haue ful cith til assale se quhat may sprety force melle al full wele knawin v cik fa bene fer then seik bot plant wallis toun aganys thame go make v redy boun quhy duellis thou taryis thus al day quhiddir gif thy marciall dedis thay war ay thy wyndy clatterand toung sal thy cowart fete euir wount fle sais thou repulsit driffe away maist vnwourthy wicht quha say iustely reprocheing sic lak rebutit doung abak quhen thou beheld mycht tyber flude boldyn ryn spate troyanis blude al femel euander king brocht vnto ground alhale ofspryng archades confoundit ouerset mony armes doun bet grysly bytais pandarus hys brothyr thay ar expert gyf fled ane vthir eik thay thousand saulys ane day vyctor hel send confutacio dra ce argumentys hine away quhen inclusit dystres amyd ynemyis wally forteres thou sayis na hope welfare w le wicht pronunce betid traistis thay haue al fele dede corp haue gyf thys tempestuous traik batal baith halfis al ou equale quhy failye sa schamfully mycht fyrst entre ficht quhy quakis thus oure membris vp doun bludy blast trumpis soun time felesyis eik varyant chance instabyl lyfe hing ballance reducyt ful mony vnlykly thyng better fyne thare begynnyng fortoun interchangeabill blenkis quent full mony ane dissauit schent syne efter ane thraw thus wele wate restorit thame agane thare ferme estate put cais set etholianis diomede pepill arpanys list tocum help supple yit bald mesapus wele happy columpnyus alsua quham ful wele ye knaw na thyng behynd na repu e name eldaris prowes thys saul lyffe quhilk sa wele luf doith promys auowis behuffe thay say allone challancis enee beseik grete god challance na bid mendynge camyllys stoutnes hir ansueris thou virgine glory italie quhat thankis yeild rander may quhat may refer thy renowne bot sen thowart thyng reddy boune surmonting al curage souerane thys tune sic laubor pane grant part sa athir syde betuix v twa bargane deuyde herk sal schaw myne auise quod yone detestabil myscheous enee rumoure surelye made kend al spyis schawis thidder send ane certane hors men licht armyt nanis send forray planis self ascendis hie band hill wentis strate passage scharp wil schape ciete cum preuilye tharfor ane prat ik deuyse wyl ly wate quyet enbuschment athir p hede secrete went stake younder woddis syde full dern sal men armes hyde set thou apoun horssit tuskane rout wyth pynsellis semblit sammyn ane schout stalwart mesapus sal go latyne barnage brethyr two capitanis come fra tyburtyne ciete wyth al thare ordinance hale menye tak thou cure thaym reule stere alhale riall army thus sayd sic wordis schorte mesapus fecht exhort feris syne euery capitane syne towartis aduersaris gane thare lay ane vale ane crukit glen ganand sticht enbusche armit men quham wounder narrow apoun athir syde bewis thik hamperith doi hyde skuggis derne ful obscure perfay quhar throw thare strekit ane rod ane strate way ane narrow peth baith gang entre full scharp schrewit passage wounder sle aboue quhilk apoun thy hill hicht quhare men mycht spy ane wel fare sycht thare debate thame anys thare fay welt doun wechty stanis thidder young turnus held discend al passage wel bekend place tuke ful priue vnknaw liggis wate vnder derne wod schaw p opis doun fra diane send kinne camilla dyscend mene sessoun latoneis douchter diane wythin hir sete heuynnis souerane swyft opys ane nimphe ane hir feris ane haly virgyne hie sort mony yeris hir callis richt dolorus vnglaide sichand sare hir sic wourdis sayid virgine dere lo camylla gais cruel batel agane mortal fay al vane hir sic weris wappynnys armour hir beris declare certyfyis quod sche aboue al vthir ful dere sche na lufe southly commyn new yit lait dianis breist vp grew wyth ane hasty sueitnes mouit sprete bot auld kindnes lang tyme vnfor lete quhen hir fader kynred mechabus kyng throw inuy expellit ancient ryng priue run cruelte pepil fled ciete wyth hym bare young infant dere hys fallow exile playfere eftir hir moderis name hait casmilla camylla clepit ane lettie tane awa bosum hir bare socht vnto wilsum holtis hare cruel fayis thare wappinnis kene vmbeset al partis tene armyt men wageouris wolstanys nere almoist lappit attanis thare na passage quhare away fle lo amyd went quhare ettillit amasenus riuere fresche flude aboue brayis bullerit war wod clouddis brist sic spate rane riuer flowis ouer large plane dressand hym swym bank syde luf young bab moist nede abide dere birding dreading quhare wylde forestis inhabitare fader professis seruand tendir youngling bund vnto tre fleand fais throw sayes lo knyt schaft laulie beseikis scho ressaue hir lady testify god wate thyne alhale vnto dedicate quhilk thou seis standis dangere commyttit windis aire thus sayd anone ane swak gardy vp bendit fer abak threw spere al force mycht stremes soundit schaftis flycht ouer feirs riuer forther bra fey vnsilly bab young camylla flaw knyt vnto quhirlland schaft tre bot mechabus quhen se grete preis fais sa nere na langar duelt bot swam throw riuere cummyn hys purpois blyith glaid spere anone sa buklith wyth maid presand vnto thrynfald diane furth grissy swarde vp tane na rurale biggingys yit na strang ciete wald hym ressaue within thyr wally hie thay wald herbry haue tane fers mynd couth subdew nane manere hirdis pasturage wylde montanis wounit al age quhare hys douchter amang bu rouk derne adis mony sloggy k wyth milk nurist beistis wilde wyth pappys fosterit hys chyld sauage stude hir sulder buklit ane propir bow ane litil arrow cace hir goldin garland hede lace stede eik hir syde garmound pall ouer hir suldderis hir nek doun grisly tygris skyn rent hing self tyme yit sche bot tendir youngling thir dartis takillis swyft let glide oft hir hede ilk tyde wald warp stringis stout staffe slyng quhare wyth fele sy ground dede wald sche ding cran trace quhite swan sche desirit mony man moderis fele throw townis tuskane desirit hir thare gude dochter vane sche onlye ful ferme hir entent dyane goddes chaistite flude content list hant euer woddis dartis schutting loue virginite remanand incorrupt ane clene made wald forsoith tyme sche abade haistit sic cheuelry molest troyianis stout army bot ane feris suld sche oft al tyme dere haue done anone nymphe opis sche said wyth wikkit fatis sen bestad yone made thou slide doun heuin hy latyne feildis thou wesy espy quharein woful batal melle ane vnhappy chance betaucht sche tak thir dartis sone case ilk reuenge able arrow thou rase quha euer wound doi hurt violate hir haly body vnto dedicate quhithir troiane italiane elike anone slane blude myne offence dere self thare eftir ruthful corp hy amyd ane bois cloude sal cary away vnspulyeit hir armour array hir bigraue reducit hir cuntre sepulture ful glorious said sche opis lichtlie heuynnys glade throw skyis southand fast doun glade persand body ouer tuskane dukis hors men routis alhale arrayit batall euery warde stale ouer al planis brayis ampand stedis ful galyeard thare bardis werely wedis apoun thare strate born brydillis brankand fast trypand thare hede cast large ground worth grisly vnto se stele wappinnis scharp spere hedis hie fyre al birnand schane feildis bricht armoure hie helmes braid scheildis aganis thaym anone also apperis bald mesapus vaileyeand weris agil latyne pepyl wyth hym ane duke catellus wyth brothir cora eik weing wolstan pepil feild ou wensche camylla vnder scheild furth thay stroke thare lang speris wele far drew thare armes wyth schaftis chargeit fer tasit vp dartis takil fleand flanis counter first tocum nanis ful ardent woix auful se men birnand ioue melle furoure grew stedis st rand stray thay approcheing sammyn array wythin ane arrow schot athir syde syne made e litil stope stil bide rasit vp ane schout bad thaym wyth ane cry quhil brute clamour fordynnyt sky thare feirs stedis bargane athir half thay mak ane werelike fere ther withal attanis euery sydis dartis fleand takillis glidis doi schoure snaw flicht dirkynnyt heuynnys skyis licht thirrenus tho ane tuskane rout aconteus ane rutuliane ful stout togidder semblit thare speris ran preif first fal samyn man man thay met melle ane felloun rak quhill schaftis al schudderis ane crak gidder duschis stout stedis attanis atheris counter fruschit vthers banys aconteus like thunderis blast smate sadil fer way cast lik ane stone warpyt ingyne al fruschit doun decline wyth sic rebound rewyne wounder sare lyfe sperplit al suddanly latynis tuke ane fray gaif bak bedene fled away tharescheildis ouer thare sulderis kest behynd toun spurris al feirs wynd troianis persewing chace fast inuadis thaym prince asillace quhen thay approchein portis nere latyne pepil returnis al fere thare wele danit hors nekkis quhelit syne gaif ane cry one thaym ane schout tothyr party tane flicht leit ga bridil fled al thare mycht lyke flowand se fludis roude ruschis land war woud skellyis coistis bay vp swakkis fast samyn wallis gray iawpis coweris fare sandis ouer bay farde swift gois ebband fast abak hys bullerand iawis ouerswak hym soukis drawys mony stane leiffis strandis schald schaldis plane tuskane folk latynys sic wyse vnto ciete wallis chasit twyis twyis thare self fle gaif bak scheildis defence behynd thaym swak bot thare eftirthe together thrid assay thay mak oistis samyn ioned crak euery man chosin hys fere forsoith granys men micht thaym eruyng doun bettin bene armour wappinnis dede corp bedene stedis thrawand ground weltis mydlit men quhilk yeild goist sweltis bedouin lay ful depe thare awin blude stoure entrestis furius wod orsilothus ane troiane al fors drelsis hys lance ane remulus hors hym mete stude ane maner fere hede remanit vnder hors ere stede enragit cruel dynt lawsus apoun hicht al fers flynt impacient wound remulus doun weltis ground catillus ane brether tyberine yollas doun bet thare eftyr syne grete armynius wounder big cors bot f r bigger curage fors quhots hede schulderis nakit war bare croun bot lokkerand yallow hare thocht nakit vode gere na wound wappin mycht hym anys effere forganis speris bustuously blomyt catillus stalwart schaft tre throw girdis baith braid schulderis banis wyth dynt stude schakand al atanys transfixit persit euery part doublis renewis mannis smart blaknyt dedlie ding vincust aunus al fare fleiching auful made camylla ilk tyde wyth cais arrowis caichit hir syde amyd slauchter melle apoun hir fone proudly pransis like ane wynsche amazone hant bargane assay hir de ay furth hald samyn feildis sone wyth crukit scheildis schapin lyke mone thou sterne made camyllaa commendacione camillais stoutnes battall quhat sal say quham first quham last thou strake erde day faill corp batal stede thou layd ground ouerthrew put dede formest ewmynius one son clyseus quhais brode breist bone ane lang stalwart spere fyr tre throw smyttin tyte peirsit sone sche cauis ouer furth bokkis stremis blude teith eik schortly conclude bludy erde bate sweltis apoun wound oft writhit tumlis weltis nixt scho eikis vthir two loris ane pagasius also quhom tane say loris fordwart stoupan iwis hynt hors rene gan founder tothir present kepe vnder furth straucht febil arme stynt fal ground togidder ruschit ane al hir sine son hyppotes amastous hate dede scho adionit pres lenand
