ane hunter fer raw armur cognissence vnknaw rade ane coursour apulye throw feild brade schulderis wele cled ou rthelld ane young bullis hyde newly hynt hed couerit saif hym fra dynt ane wolfis hidduous gapand iowis wyth chaftis brade quhite teith bustuous browis mak debate held til hand ane rurale club culmes stede brand quhare went amyd routis hye aboue thaym al hale hede men mycht se camylla myschefe vnset scho bare hym throw ground doun bet norna grete curage forsoith mycht al hys rout tofore tane flicht bot forthir eik thys forsaid camylla wyth mynd vnfreyndly thir wourdis sa thou thirrene fallow quhat wenyt thou woddis chasand wylde dere quod sche day cummyn proude wordis hate ane womannis wappin sal resist debate theeles na litil renowne then thou sal turs away faderis goistis blithly schaw camyllais glaue thou art ouerthraw incontinent madin eftir thys slew orsilothus ane hate butis twa byggest men body banys al oist fallouschyp troyanis bot ilk butis standand hir throw nek sche pers bore betuix hawbrek helme hye hys hals quhare sche dyd nakyt espye ouer hys left schulder hang ane scheild bot orsilothus fled hyr feyld gan triuphe mony ane turnyng went cirkillis wide sche draue hym bent mony ane cours iouk quhare euer fled sche followis last sche ouertak man throw armour harne pa hir braid pollax rasit hie al hir fors mycht syne strikis sche besocht hir grace grete request sche doublit hir dyntis prest wyth fell woundis hede torte rent harnes bait ouer al vissage went awnus son quhilk also awnus hate cais betid approche debate towart made al sone hir saw abasit huffis stil drede aw mont opennyus duelt amang liguriane pepil cuntre forsoith lakest weriour bot forty man richt stalwart stoure lang fatis sufferit hym ficht exerce prattikis ieoperdy slicht awnus fra wele persauit na wai fle eschew melle mycht eschape quene stud hym agane begouth assay hir ane trane ane sle dissait thus first sayd quhat honour till ane stout wensche maid tyl assure traift ane strang hors leif thy swift stede traist thyne awyn fors nane auantage quhen thou list fle licht plane hand hand addres v debate fute allone thare sal thou se thare sal thou knaw anone quhom thys wyndy glore vast avantis honour pane louing grantis thus sayd bot sche al hate fyre aggreuit sore inflammit felloun ire alicht hir mait hors betauch desire anone fute vpstraucht equale armour bodin wounder licht drawin swerde hand schameful brycht vnabasit abaid hym feild abulyeit onlie bot wyth ane qubite scheild young man wenyng sle dissait begilit hir consate bridill turnit mare delay flicht sprent furth brak away feil sydis let hors sydis feil scharp irne spurris prik apoun hell quod made thou fals liguriane ouer wantoun thy proude mynd al vane bariant man perfay quod sche thou assayit thy cuntre craftis sle dissaitfull wicht forsoith say thy slicht wilis sal bere away hailskarth hyne turs hame fra v vnto thy faderis hous fals awnus thus sayd wensche vnto vthir syre furth sche sprent spark glede fyre spedy fute wiftly rinnis sche past hors renk furth fle feld wyth grete disdene claucht anone coursere rane syne set apoun baldlie quhare sche stude hir reuengit hir fais blude al lichtlie happy gois halk se hicht ane rokit pennakil hie swift wyngis persewis wounder sare silly dow hiech vp quham fynale chepis last lonkit punsis sari fast thristand callouns throw hir entrallis quhil al blude aboundly furth ralis wyth hir beik deplumand al sydis licht downis vp skyis glidis p tharchone grete chiftane tuskane oist fle folkis turne agane boist fader goddis men wyth diligent ene al hir dedis vnderstand sene setuate heuinlie hous hie inducis commuis melle tarch one tuskanis principal lord syre braithful stoundis rasit brym fyre amyd ful mischeuus ficht grete slauchter routis takand flycht horsbak tarchone baldly draw wilful pepil support saw thewardis al euery nacioun wyth admoniciouns sere exhortacioun diuers wourdis tyistis fecht schame clepand calland ilk man name quhil thay dreuin war abak chaist releuis agane bargane haist tuskane pepil happinnis sayd ye sal euer sa dullit bowbardis vnwrokin sic iniuris suffir quhat quhow grete ene drede fere thir handis twa yone ilk troiane forhoware asia put deith send doun hell quod lat latyne pepill sitting se myne allane wyth swerde thare presens sall reuenge end alleris offence betid wyn gre lat v vincust til subiect yeild hym crowne enduring terme lyfe lat iois lauinia hys wyfe kyng latyne sad degest mynde ansueris said apoun kynd douchty younkerkyng latynis oracion turnus dis dyng hym fra battell excellent curage fer thy forcy vassalage febil age thou doi excede quod al fer mare diligentlie pertenis ganand counsale prouide examyne euery chance may tide parte ane manere fere lang experience knawand doutis thou weildis dawnus thy faderis realme land feil cieteis conquest wyth thy awne hand thareto thou also ane gentil hert liberale fre maist expert king latyne gold gif eik perfay enewch vtheris fer seik madynnnys bene vnwed latyum wyde laurent feildis besyde blud fryndeschip na thyng myssemand bot wourthy quene ony land thole pray dissait done away thir wourdis quheyn wecht till say samyn prent thir sawis thy wit vnlesum suld wedlok knyt dochteris till wowaris land hir fore askit sic band al spaymen goddis reueling declarit thaym vnlesum thyng netheles vincust clene lufe spousis cousing dere ouer cumming hir wofull teris site maner bandis thou brokin fra son law ful wranguslie spous vnto promyst rest haue forthir mouit ane vikkit sen syne quhat chance stand dangere fers batellis persewis ful wele thou wate seis turnus quod huge trawell thou tholit pane principale mayst douchty capitane lo twyis batal vincust haue skantlie within wallit ciete hope wele italie defendis recent blude notourly kend flude tyber waxis hate agane huge banys quhite semes plane sterit thus purpois sere quhiddir flow thus oft thare quhat mad folie changis thocht gyl reddy doutit nocht troianis frendis ressaue gif war turnus dede war bygraue quhat aucht fer rathir end beand prosperite hale fere quhat wald cousingis rutulianis quhat wald say vthir italianis gif suld thus wise sa wilfully asking dochteris wedlok ally expone offer dede quod fortoun defend chance sa suld behald chance batal variabil persaue fikkil warde vnstabill haue reuth mercy thy fader ald quham ardea cuntre doith withhald diuidit fer disseuerit thy saik wo begone thus sayd king bot violent curage turnus hie mynd bowit neuer ane stage quha wald cure medicine mei incres growis male eis eftir first micht speik agane thus began expreme wordis plane thou maist souerane faderturnus nsur pray sauf honour thou wald away thir curis thochtis sollicitude thou takis schortlie conclude suffir plege dede wage glorius renowne vassyllage fader swak dartis brandis febil stalwart richt handis woundis rede blude ruschis younder proude troiane clepit stout moder tyme sal fer scik quhilk goddis wyth hir subtyl slychtis eik hyr son accustumate ay take flycht wount dek hyde sycht wythin ane wyseler cloud ane trane heild hyr selfe also inschaddois vane p quene persuadys turnus fra stryfe desist bot batel agane resi quene amataquene amatais oration dyssuadyng turnus fra battell al fere vncouth new manere wepyng ful sore al dede lyke ful harmes hyr son law turnus hynt armes feruent ardent desyre turnus sayd scho thou best belouit syre thir ilk woful teris pray wourschip thou awe tyl amata gyf ony honour hyr thy kyn twichis mouis thi breistis wythin beseik ane thyng mine awin knycht decist ceis mache troianis fycht thou onlie comfort febyl eild thow al rest welfare beild haue reuth piete woful bale power michtis rest alhale wourschip empyre kyng latyne hous famyl thou lyke declyne remanis vp bore assure certyfyis tharefore quhat auenture fycht sall happin self chance turuus sal tide samyn wyth gif thou endis stryfe sal depart irk sum lyfe neuer thral sal remane se yone ilk eneas sun law lauinia made wyth sore teris smert hyr moderis wourdis felt depe hir hert rude hir vissage glow ful teris gan hir chekis strow feruent fyre schame risis hie kyndland mare large rede collorit bewtie natural hete blude chase ouer al partis hir quhitlie face quhill vyrgine woful rage sic culloris rendris fresche vissage quhay byspark wald quhite enoure indane wyth scarlot droppis broun sanguane quhare schene lyllies ony stede war pulderit vermel rosis rede hate luf trublis sore knycht thys made fixis al sicht al birnis desyre bargane army hate fyre syne quene amata abade wourdis wyse sayd dere moderturnus thy weping ho beseik persew thus wyth gretand teris quhen pa thir mortal weris marcial bargane contrary fo way present sic takyn wo turnus michtis lyis quod chance deith mak self fre say gif deith way schape may astart yit eschape time instant messengere idmon clepit credence hecht bere yone troiane tirrant rehersyng wourdis quhilkis lykys hym nothing knaw morow al arely bricht aurora orient skye rosy chariot liftis vp hir hede firmament schrouding cullour rede moue aganis rutulians oistis nane army troianis bot athir half fra batall best baith sal troianis rutulians rest lat v twa bargane conclude betuix v dereyne blude younder feild wart strife lat athir seik lauinia wife fra said fast spedis bad anone lat se stedis behaldand thaym reiosis hert se thaym stand sa feirs curage smert quhilk kind hors quhilum thay say orichia lusty fresche may athenis kingis douchter ane maist rial present wounder fare send hyr cuntre king pilumnus ferd grantseir vnto ilk turnus quhilk stedis schapin delite excedit fer snaw cullour quhite speik spede thare swiftnes vntald thay wyndis blastys forryn wald besy knoppis verlotis stabil thaym stude ful yape seruiabil thare luffis gan thaym chere clap straik thare leyndis make stere thare lokkerand manis thare crestis hie dressis trelyeis kami honestly then vnto chalmer went syne schulderis assayis hawbrek fyne burnist male schynand rychely fynest gold quhitly alcomye tharewith also swerd addressis quhat way wald vse mele souir scheild assayis also eik tymbrit helme creistis two quhilk swerde made vnto dawnus hys syre vlcanus mychty god fyre forgit thys blade temperit handis hate glowand dippit stigeane strandis syne wyth grete force enarmyt al gere ful lichtlie vp hynt stalwart spere quhilk tho amyddis hal lemand stude vp ane pillare huge square gude quhilum spulye bereft ane clepit attoure ane capitane armicane schaft schuke brangillis lust ly thareto loude voce thus cry thou spere neuir failyete dede quhen callit desire nede quhilum veildit actoure maist douchty knicht hand withhaldis turnus wicht tyme mayist myster doun bet corp thou grant younder phrigiane skant half ane man wyth stalwart may hawbrek body arrace hakkit rent persit mony place dusty pouder thare subdill fule crispe yallow hare made creis curlis sa wele yplet ilk nycht warme brotht stele dekkit donk wiselie manere fragrant myr vthir enuntmentis sere sikkin furie rage caucht thus carpis ane schaft tre vissage ardent syre sparkis glidis hote fyre verray feruour fereful tene schynis bristis furth baith ene lyke bul bargane begyn wald geuis terrybyl routis lowis mony fald aggreuit bustuous furth borne presys yre assay wyth horne lenand hys spald stok ane tre wyth dynt wynd rentis make debate apoun land wyth hard clufe vpwarpis fast sand self tyme na le curage enee cled hys moderis armour auful se scharpys selfe furour cial rayssand greif ardour bellical ioyus wolx wexe make ane end sic proffer poyntment send syne confortis feris dolorus mesyt drede sayd ascaneus declarand thame fatal ordinance thare destany goddis purueance kyng laurentius latyne twichand forsaid tretye conuyne bad messengeris bare hame delay souir answere thay dasirit alway pece truce thay spak proclame artikles lawis contrak p iuno knauand turnus last delay end stop bargane send sc rslye vpsprang nixt day following scheddand bemes brycht mornyng vpoun toppis mountanis hie phebus stedis fyrst depe see rasit thare hedis noyis thyrllis hycht ouer al feildis blawand clere lycht quhen troianis rutilyanis ground mesuris euynnys dichtis planis vnder wallis cheif ciete thare feyld fechtin place suld amyddis quham harthis vp thay set quharon firis suld made bet common goddis eik bedene altaris couerit wyth scherald grene sum vtheris brocht fontanis wattir tare sum haly ingil wyth thame bare wyth lynning vali lyke apronis lycht thay war arrayt thare hedis dycht wyppys haly herb varuane legiouns tho behaldis plane al routis ausonianis vthir wyse hate italianis furth thringis portis ful attanis wyth lancis lang pikkys nanys thydder al troyanis wardis thirrene oistis ruschis hastely bodin ful wele nobil armour sere nane vtherwyse wyth wappynnis wyth gere arrayit batal al rycht thocht furie mar callit thame fycht amyd thou sandys swiftly throw planys furth sprentis lustely thare capytanys ryche purpour arrayit fyne gold brycht assaritus sonny estheus wycht tothir part strang asilas bald mesapus also wyth hym neptunus son expert hors dantyng efter trumpet blew ane sing euery partyment bownis thare stand gan thare speris stik doune land set thare scheildis behald fyne wom n wedois matrouns syne desirus se bargane stout childer common mony ane rout couth na wappins weild armour wyth vnweildy agit folk fere clam hicht hedis touris wally al housis riggingis flouris sum aboue apoun portis hie ascendit behald melle bot iuno tho doun hecht ywys mountane albane clepyt dayis set hillisdoun nouther name honour renone scho behald amyd feildis plane athir battellis oistis twane baith troianis lawrenteis kyng latinis ciete eik scho seis anon turnus sister apoun hie clepit inturna carpys sche goddis haly nymphe maystres wellis stankis routand stremis expres quhilk honour iouye king heuynnys hie hir gaif bereft virginite sayd thou nymphes wourschip fludis clere saul hald maist le dere thou knawis wele prefar ay til al vthir damysellis perfay latyne cuntre quhat soeuer thay war wranguslie ascendit draw nar bed vnproffi abil iupiter maist glaidli eik haue stakit till ane parte heuyne alsua herk thy sorow thou iuturna wite bot warnit haue turnus thy cheif ciete haue saue sa lang fatis sufferit quhil werde sisteris sa tholit se young men haist fale mache feild wyth fatis inequale lattir terme day approchis ne fatale force strangest destany nowthir bargane younder grene consederatioun may se wyth ene pa thy dere brother germane gif thou dar suffir ony mare dredeful pane thys semys pertenis quod sche gif percase ony better may ocht betyde vnto yone catiuis kend scar iuno thir wourdis brocht end quhen nympheiuturnus answer iuturna bedene plente teris furth yet hir ene hir fare quhite breist thare sche stand thryis foure tymes smate wyth hir owne hand saturnus get iuno sais thay teris na wise thys tyme pertenis efferis haist gif thou way wythdraw thy brothir deith away mak oistis bayth stere provoke batal thaym moue conuyne trety new consaif brek disturbe wyth wynd bewaif sal warrand thy wirkare mak baldly vndertake quod sche wyse iuno nymphe exhort left hir hale dout schort mynde full trift wo begone vnsound full depe smytting wyth sorowfull wound p followis sacryfyce prayere fyrst eneas syne kyng latine fere mene tyme kyngis athir rout thare cieteis strenthis ischis amyd ane four quhelit thare latyne thraw wyth huge pompe stedis foure draw quhais haris templis war wele dicht wyth ryall croun fyne gold byrnist brycht quhareon urettis twelf lyke bemes schene ane riche adornament bene clere phebus grantschire hald nixt came furth rollit prince turnus bald wyth ane wa quhelit art delyte drawin stedis twa mylk quhyte athir hand held fere brade hede brangilland ieuilling spere fader eneas also furth wyth romane lynnagea commendation eneas hys sonne ascaneus originall apoun tothir half come thame agane wyth st scheld bricht sternis schene heuinly armoure lemand lycht besyde rade ascaneus swete knycht semit wele euery mannis doine ane vthir gude beleue hope grete rome furth come preist quham accordit mak sacryfice concord contract vestement clene sic religioun wrocht ane young birssit swyne thame brocht wyth ane rouch twynt schepe samyn fere quhais woll fleis neuir clepit wyth schere beistis furth ilk syrs vnto altare blesand hate fyre princis tho quhylk suld makyng turnus towart bricht sonny vprisyng wyth salt melder thare handis raith forrettis thir beastis toppis baith thay clepe mesure tho gyse coupis ful wyne sacrifyce altaris yettis wyth drawin swerd syne reuthful enee orison furth made thus sayd thou brycht soneneas oracion gud fortoune battell wyth schene bemes glaid witnes behest pray ilk ground mot testifye quhat say quhen sa grete pane aduersite sufferit haue feil syis land se almychty iouy prayere saturnus douchter thou spous sa dere benyng thou swete goddis implore gentil mar thou takis tent heretyl wythaldis writhis thy wyll euery batal stryue werefare debate vnder thy hie power deificate fludis cal fountanis stremis clere al manere goddis reuerent sere abut heuin ydrad starrit sky eik blissit wichtis testifye vnder erth law hel doun bene fomy seyis stremes grene gyf betyde fallis victory turnus ansomane partie conuenient grant fle vincust folk euandrus ciete ascaneus sall al tyte thir feildis wythdraw eneadanis neuir ilk thraw aganis yow sal rebell moue ne wappinnis eftir cuntre dere bot gif sa beis mar god glorius victorie hand grantis v beleif afer rathir sal befall al tyte conferme sal goddis al throw grete mychtis thare deire gif fare fortoune betydis ne command italianis subiect obey troianis yit realme desire bot athir oure pepil mot go fre vnthral vnuincust lawis euinlie conf derate perpetual allye wourschipping goddis sacrifice sal thaym lerne teiche deuise fader law kyng latyne moist reule pepill bayth pece fader inlaw souerane lord syre hys lyfe moist bruke solempnit impire suffir troianis ar boune beild ane strenth wallit toun ciete quhare sal duell hame lat madin lauinia gif name thus first eneas sayd eftir syne apoun thys wise followis kyng latyne behald towart heuyn quhare stand sterne vpheuiskyng latynus oracio richt hand ilk erth seyis sterne hie swere like wyse vnto enee latonys birth twinnis twa bricht appollo chaist diana doubil frontit ianus pissance goddis infernall dirk sanctuarie blak sabyl greuous pluto god reuengeabyll hie fader aboue mothere cry doi thunder sic concord ratifye twiche thir altaris ingill present quod testifyis ilk godly maieste sall neuir tyme sesoun day betyde brek peace italiane syde na confiderance ani part two quhat way euir happin mater go ne na maner violence boist noraw sall ony wyse therfra withdraw bot ferme stabyl sall haldin thougt erth wald myddyll wyth se diluge inundatioun schent couir confound ather element thocht heuin hell resolue wald promis sall inuiolate hald lyke ilk scepture wand se perchance tyme ane scepture hand bare sall neuir burgeoun sprede branschis lite nowthir rank leuis blossum delite sen ani wod thare grew law stock hard rutis hew wantis moder nurissing syouns twistis wount spring grew therfra ye may se perfay wyth edgeit lomis bene sued ful quite away vmquhile ane grouand tre quhare stand thus crafty werkmannis hand inclusit couerit lustely birnist gold finest alcomye geuin forefather latine land scepture riall bere hand wyth wourdis sic ferme relatiouns thir fynale sure confederacions athir princis confirmid sworne amyd thare nobillis standand thame beforne syne eftir thir auld ceremonis gise beistis deuly addressit sacrifyce thay brytnyt haue amang flamis rede rentis thay war fully dede entrellis thare beistis yit lyue syne furth platis ballantis belyue wyth pasit flesche plennyst altaris large thareon bestowand hepis mony ane charge bot tho begouth new ilk bargane seming rutilians euery man ane richt vneuinly interpryse diuers rumour thare breistis ryse wyth mony sundry deinyng consate thinkys thus ane vthir gate ay nerer mare diligently thay mater consider espye wele thay persaue behaldis sans fale thir campiouns war strencht equale vnto opinioun ilk thraw helpit mekil wyth stil pase law turnus mufand towart altaris past laulie adornit face doun cast wyth chekis waxin leyn thare semyng quharon soft berde newlie furth spryng al ying sic ane haue dale thay thocht visage al becummyne pale p iuturna slicht incha tment brekys peace haisty batal sent eftir ilk commonyng thus waxand mare mare mony ane sing iuturna hir sister persaif saw commoun vulgare hartis waif diuers sentencis intentis sere amyd routis drew scho nere forme liknes camertiz bald nobil blude cummin lynuage ald fader brute renownee magnified wourschip wounder thareto selfe maist douchty cheualrye dedis armes fate hardy stout liberal syncere amyd oistis wyse scho thryng vnexpert conuoy sic ane thyng diuers rumouris preis stalis sche syne sic lyke wourdis carpis apoun hye rutulianis eschame ye fere sa grete ane perrell dangere ane silly saule put auenture al sal vnderly sic cure quhidder ar equale entent troyanis nowmer hardiment lo al troianis archadianis v arrayit planis fatall pissance hale stede tuskanis turnus fede sa thay bene ye may behald se gif li mak vnset trai half al menye grete small sal fynd younder ane fa mache yone turnus goddis aboue ful straucht quhais altaris hym vowit betaucht al ye se sayde sche wyth fame eternale sall wpheit eu rmare alife maist name kouth carpit sang euery mannis mouth quhen thrallis leif sall natiue land vnto proude tyrrantis ouerhand sall compellit lordis tyl obey thus sleuthfully sa fant fey huffis still thir feildis war dede self list schape na remede wyth sic lyke wourdis mindis consate younkeris inflammyt hate mare mare feilde murmoure crepis throw euery rout thay quhilkis desyrit peace rest commoun wele thocht best mak end bargane wyse ar alterit halely ane vthir auyse desyre thay batall abade prayand god contract neuer bene made compassioun caucht hart fale turnus chance senyng inequale self tyme eik iuturna wy ane vthir greter wounder ekit thys heich vp heuin thame plane ane takin sche schawin auguriane sic ane sygne nane vthir entent mare effectuous conuenient trubyl italiane myndis mak thame raif wyth fals demonstratioun dissaif iouis oule eirne come forand fleand vp heich touward bricht rede sky cachand ane grete flicht oist foulis ha endlang ceist quhilkis thare wyngis fore dredand wraik skrymmis thare mony spreich craik quhyl suddanly egil wyth anesours towart fludis made cours despituously tyl punsis claucht ane swan excellent bewte italianis apoun athir syde rasit thare myndis se quhat suld betyde sone vthir foulis heich skye corned agane mony skreyme cry chais assale thare aduersare ane wounder thing se vp licht thay dirkin wyth thare penny thik throw skyis wyth mony ane scraik pyk samyn ane sop thik ane clud baide thare fa thay assailye inuade sa lang quhil fors ouerset heuy byrdin sa mait het micht failyeit clukis rude egyl lete pray fall flude vp amang cluddis flew away rutulianis al full glaid gay wyth huge brute clamour loud anone salust signe takin augurione syne sped thare hand made thame fycht fyrst vtheris columnyus wycht ane spaman diuinour sle ya ya quod quhilk oft wesyit desyrit thys gude takin ressaue ratifye knawis goddis fauour supple rutulianis hynt wappinnis follow quham yone wauingeour yone ilk strangere affrayis wyth hys vnwourthy lyke tyl vnweyldy foullis coist marchis fors mekle boist inuadis rubbis spulyeis ye se sal fere gif sone bak fle mak sale anone hald euir away throw depe se attoure fludis gray charfore ye sal al samyn ane assent assembill routis present feild defend men mane king turnus reft slane thus said wyth wourd al fast towart hys fayis forganis hym dyd cast ane werely dart anone al ir souir schaft flew quhissilland wyth ane quhir thare slidis scherand throw oneschewabil baith certane lang square samyn wyth thys vprysis nanys ane huge noyis clamour al attanys wyth sic effray hidduous dyn wardis oistis wax stere rerde deray hait ire hartis kyndil euery bald syre furth flew takill richt ouer forgane face thiddir ilk tyme stude percase myne brethir germane fresche young age nane thare oist mare semely personage quham trew faythful wyfe thirrene ilkane bere tyll hir spous gelip archadene quham dart hit ane thare stand ane gudly springald ane fare young galland richt scharplie maid armoure schynand brycht myddil markit hym ful rycht quhare wouyn girdil orti sche aboue nauyl beltit se smate hym euin samyn place nere quhare bukkil sydis embrace throw gird body wyth ane greuous wound speldit stark dede apoune ground bot hys bald brether ane rout wod wroith wo sum hynt swerdis sum claucht hand darte stele hebe thare blynde furye full fede ruschit thare fais wythane ferfull braid aganis quham resist muaid routis army laurentanis ran recounter thaym attanis agane assemblit ane spate flude troyanis tuskanis wroith wede wyth thaym archade arrayit feildis wyth burnist armour thare payntit scheildis apoun sic wyse al ane assent caucht hale desire fecht apoun bent dereyn feyld wyth bitand brand hale mater sum schot doun wyth thare hand altaris markit sacryfyce beliue ouer al lift vpsemyt rise fell tempest dartis schott flanys thik ony schoure scharp hailstanis incres flycht stelit hedis full greuous grew bargane al stedis sum ran wyne flaccouns grete ire sum hynt vp furnes ful fyre kyng hym self latynus affray fled ciete tursit wyth hym away hys goddis mawmentes dreuin abak wyth ane schamefull rebute mekil lak left concord vndone brocht till end sum bridillis stedis cartis vp dyd bend sum haist ane loupe ane swak thame self vpcastis one horsis bak war reddy stoure hand drawin swerd nakit birnist brand mesapus full desirus preis till confound trety pei ane kyng thirrane anlestys stede wyth kingis ensenyeis crowne hede affrayis sore hym driuand stede tothir drew away fere drede bakwart fallis hys schulderis cronn vnhappely apoun ane altare doun quhilk stude percace behind land mesapus ful feirs wyth spere hand apoun draif thocht besocht hym fare hys schaft also rude square bene ane cabir spar doun stout coursoure na thyng skar smat hym ane greuous wound dedelik bit syne thir wordis said ha art thou hit thou myne auyse grete goddis mare ganand sacrifice italianis hurlis ane flote spulyeit hys corp membris yit alhote charyneus tho ane stout troyane mete ane ebusus come hym agane wald haue smyte hym ane bustuous dynt altare ane birnand schide hynt gan rycht amyd visage stare blesit vp lange berde hare quhilk scaldit thus ane strang fleoure cast forthir choryneus also fast ruschit fa thus fyre fangit vnsaucht left hand hare claucht syne kne possit sit ane plat erde speldit hym al flat wyth hys stife stok swerde sic ane state throw bayth hys sydis first dynt hym smate podalirius drawin swerde list ceis alsus herd persew throw preis quhilk ruschis abak fere lyffe saif vandgarde throw mony poyntit glaue bot quhen saw fa sa nere inuade na wyse mycht eschew cuade vphesit brade ax rude square akwartlye straik aduersare quhilk amyd hys forehede nere croun vnto hys chyn edge caruyn doun fer brede hys armour quhare stude al besprent blandit ful blude tho podalyrius herd reft expres cauld irny slepe deithis stres vp breith yald thare ficht ene closit euirlestand nycht p enee sore woundit feild dyd pa quhais absence turnus mare cruel reuthfull pacient eneas behalding wrang gam pa rycht arme vnarmyt ftynt thare feid furth strekis vncouerit hede cryis clepis pepil tho freyndis dere quhiddir hurle ye ilkane aganis vihir may quhat mouit thys hasty discord quod stanche wraith schame al lorne peace concord twychit sworne artikillis eik lawis ding appoyntit vp promyst euery thyng det richt aucht appoun land allane turnus recounter hand hand snffir performe derene away drede velany sal wyth hand sone mak fedderit flicht swift randoun hys bane licht vncertane fra quhat hand sent quhat kynd schot quhat instrument hie glore sa notabil ane dede hyd nane knew quhat drede wist quha wrocht rutulianis sa vp mustouri wantonlye furth sprentand throw feildis wyl quhare hym list hym wyth hys awne hand renyeis reulis driuand furth thus hys ire laid feil corp dede mony bald syre doun strowand eik vnder fute plane diuers vtheris yit throwand half ane quthir wicht cart rowtis brayf away thay tuke slicht grete e ray cesting speris dartis scharp hynt let thaym thik amang hys fayis fle sic wyfe bludy armypotent god mar besyde frosty flude brum trace ful haistely bowand batel feild makis grete brute clattering hys sch ild quhen list mouing maist cheuelrus furth steris hys stedis feirs furious quhilk fleis furth sa wyth mony ane stend ouer planys large quhare thay wend forryn gois alway zepherus nothus swftest wyndis tway dyn thare fete carte trace gronys vnto forther parte hym walkis godly feris drede wyth pale face deban mortall weris wrayth ire eik frandeful dissait ligging vnder couert ane buschement wa e turnus sic like al chery proude licht amyd batall cachi fycht hys stedis twa glaucus iasus quham imbrasius fosterit baith twa fare cuntre licia thaym instrukkit ful equaly fate armes hant cheuelry owthir till assale yit behynd wyth swift hors till forryn wynd yound ane vthir part amyd feild wmedes feris walkis vnder scheild quhilk son thay tel agit dolon vailyeant battel name bare fore grantschir wicht bot strang handis stout curage ficht awin fader dolon bare quhilk troy vmquhile sege lay thare sa stout curage wyl durst ask chariot achill hys reward quhare sa baldly grekis tentis tuke hand espy bot son tedeus diomede ane vthir fassoun he quyt mede sa stout bot wyth bald hart hym self kest way meit carte renyes richt hand hynt syne writhit aboute euer stynt famy mouthis haisty stedis douchty man sa gude nedis thus hang harlit euery arte lymouris hame brotheris cart thus eneas temanys al flocht sundry motioun ire bot al nocht allace ne knawis quhat dyuers thochtis sere consatis lo hys mynd mony contrare purpois sent thus trublit entent mesapus cais altaris confederance vyolate last ful furius hate mydwart inemyis inuaid wyth prosper chance batal vnglaid terribil fais waxis hale ony difference degre wraik na man lyst spare ane cruel auchter rasit turnus recounterit preis amytus brother diores quham fra thare hors ground doun bet fute feild strangly vmbeset formest ane lang styff spere smate dede ane swerd tothir fere sine baith thare hedis hakkit hy hys cart hyngis thame blude tharfra droppand tursys away theself stede eneas ane alsay ane vnset kelit ianaus talon also stout cethegus syne eftir thame kelit preis sa ay sorowfull onytes renowned thebis blude ofspryng descenbyng doun etheon kyng moder born peridium vther chif captane turnus kelit twa brethir war lithia send appollois cuntre troianis defend eftir thaym ane meneit slane ane young man borne archadane al dayis euir hatit melle bot al forhe moist nedis thus de laik larne fludis gray craft fisching euery day ane pure cote hous held bure law rewardis riche folkis war hym vnknaw fader erit sew ane pece feild hire gang held hys beild like fyre war vp bet sum dry widderit wod vpset baith thare diuers partis sere amyd soundand buskis laurere quhare fomy riueris rede spate hurlis doun mouth ane large gate hidduous brute felloun farde attanis thare thay rin ouer flowand al planis ilkane distroyis waistis driuis away na stawar bayth turnus enee hurllis ruschis feirs throw melle nowthe great hate betuex turnus ene braithful ire felloun thocht within thare myndis boldynnys al flocht thay breistis na wy vincust breistis ful grief cruelte lasch thay bludy swerdis bricht mak woundis wyde al thare mycht tane thaym knaw enee kyng murranus ancestry mayst hie soundand name forefaderis auld ouer al clan latyne kyngis bald obseruit man e man vnto day furth carte smittin qwite away bet doun vnto erd wynd flaucht wyth ane grete rouk quhirland stane ouer raucht murranus renis chetis quherewith stedis yok kit war thretis vnder quhelis weltit doun quhare liggis morrall soun awne ledis aboue rap rap sterand hufis stampand mony clap ouer treddis doun thringis thare maister law thare lordis hi estate misknaw ane turnus recounterit ane hilo ruschand hurllit thro melle tho full feirs mynd austerne curage bot turnus al vassallage gilt halffettis ane grundin dart thraw fixt throw helme schaft flaw peirsand brane quhil bruschit blude thy richt hand creteus sa gude thou forciest greik cummyng fra archade land micht deliuer ilk turnus hand goddis cupentus plane mycht enee come agane bot breist steill poynt met thirlit throw doun bet nowthir scheild obstant plait steil catiuis breist helpit neuir ane dele eoline feildis lawrentane behald ron doun bet slane thy brade bak riche wede ground thou bespred richt fer brede thare lyis thou dede quhom gregioun oistis ficht mnestheus sterne seres u tothir half prince mesapus grete horssis danter clepit eik stalwar asilas thirrene routis semblit attanis kyng euandrus army archadianis euery man hymself best mycht vterance syde cassin ee last behald cite saikles batal fre al sic stryffe pane trauel quiet man wyffe ane greter bargane entent suddanly figure dyd emprent callis mnestheus eik feregestus chif ani hys oist herand euery wicht commandeneas co mand men warre tary delay maid preceptis quhat sal lay se man beswere slaw rin tyl haisty vnset wyl begyn sen iupyter assistis syde herkis quhat purpois tyde thys day sall destroy sone bet doun laurent hale cyete toun quhilk caus al weryng quyte confounde king latinis ing le wil thay relsaue bridil hand obeysance grant comand yone hie turettis thay p hie reikand chynais younder se sal mak plane equale ground quhat suld tary delay ane stound abiding sic place quod quhyl turnus list fecht wyth v melle quhil ane vther time agane ouer cum vincust batal plane may haue refuge thys toun beleif syne efter feild v recounter gre cytezanis hede ciete welefare cheif iniquite twrs thidder hy hate byrnand fyre brandis aud wyth blesand flammis handis renewis pussance thay thryst ledderis wallis thay wyst haistelythe town stormy fire blesys dyd appere sum vtheris troyanis ruschit fere vnto portis first thaym met kelit entre doun bet sum vtheris schutis dartis takillis flanys thayin quhilk berinkin hede remanys wyth flicht schaftis thare thay dirknit skyis enee hym self wyth formest stand vnder wallis puttand hand assalt loude voce hye kyng latinis fast cusis drawand goddis wytnes agane constrenyt hors moue bargane italianis thus twyis sundry tymes schew hys inemyis falsly day thay brokin secund confederatioun sworne mad amang cietezanis grete affray vprais distord monysundry way sum bad vnclois ciete al fast warp vp portis wide wallis cast troyanis thare grete prince enee ressaue thare kyng ciete vtheris stert thare wappinnis thare gere defend thare toun fere may gyf ane similitude wele like quhen herd fund byis bike closit vnder ane derne cauerne stanis fyllit full sone littile wanys wyth smoik soure better rekis stew beis wythin affrayit new ouerthowrt thare hiuis waxy ten ti rynnis mekil dyn beming innis scharpand thare stangis ire thay wald ficht swa laithly odoure rais hicht fyre blesis dirk ony roik thar ruvis toppis went smoik stanis warpit fast rebound within wallis grete brute sound vp reik wod went quhar na tenementis stude hossis ware betide also thir wery latinis quhilk irkit myscheif pynys ane chance mysfortoun toun wyth womenting straik boddum doun quene amata saw sic wise ciete vnbeset inemyis wallis kyndillitquene mata seig towne stormy hi gi hi self flammis hete fyre blesis aboue ruffis glete na turnus army cumand thame aganis na yit oistis rutulianis sche fell vnhappy batell stede wenyt young turnus fechtand bene dede tho verray sorow suddanlye hir mynd trublit cane rame cry sche caus wite al thys greif bayth crop rute hede sic mycheif hir dolceus fury thus myndeles al enragit dule tho dyd expres ful mony ane thing reddy de wythal rent handis hir purpoure wede rial ane hie balk teyt vp sche ane loupe knot ane stark cord ane lace quharewith hir self sche spilt schameful dede fra latine matrouns wil rede persauit vile mycheuous wraik thay rent thare hare harro allake hir dochter first beside dede corp standis riuand hir giltin tressis hir handis hir rosy chekis tore startis sche laif piete se ladyis dede corp stude rentis ruggis thaym self thay war wod thare goling greting deray large hale resouudis ane fer way quhill kyngis palice inuiroun divulgate went sprede ouer al toun fey vnhappy fame sic ane dede euery wicht tynt hart wo drede wyth habit rent king latine gate waxis wo begone astonist fate dere spous ciete syne semyt brocht vnto fynale rewyne cannois hare sare mouit entent vnclene pouder besprent mony tymis hym selft accusit sa lang lachit refu ressaue glaidlie troiane enee repenting sare wele ciete requirit draw maich son law p quenes deceis fra turnus wyst went sege eneas resyst mene time weriour vnder scheild turnus youd fer part feild ane menye persewand ouer plane quhilk stragil fled al thare mane sum dele walxis dol syre seing hors begyn sope tyre euer le le ioyus thare renkis gate throw melle thare wynd southing fereful clamour brocht rycht thare myxt wyth vncertane terrour effere confusioun sound smate hys ere come ciete ane felloun murmuring rycht vnglade brute care womenting ha wa sayd quhat may bene wally trublyt ciete wyth sa grete dule sorow thus ruschis sa felloun noyis bere clamour fra toun euery part thus sayd gan stynt cart al enragit tyt renyeis abak quham syster iuturna spak scho turnyt sayd semblant metestus cartare hors renyeis fyde renyeis cart sche reul direct amydwart melle wyth sic wourdis scho ansueris fute hate turnus lat v persew troianis thus gate quhare victory v schewis reddy way thare bene enew vtheris fay defend wele mantene toun yone eneas makis brute soun inuaid italianis ye mydlit batall sic feare tharfore lat v wyth cruel hand stede lay al fele corp troyanis dede wyth na le nowmer slane vnder scheild le honour sal thou wend feild turnus ansueris thou sister dere knew ful wele thou lang gere craft quent wilis sa fle consideratioun trublit trety enterit thys batal quhilk thou wrocht goddes thy wilis ar nocht bot quha send heuin schene huge sturt trauell sustene qubiddirgif thou come entent se cruell deith thy brother sayd quhat sall lat se quhare sal quhat succour promittis fortoun sal self myne ene lang gere grete murranus quham nane mare leif dere vnto leuand day swete ground loude voce perfay call quhare lay vnsound ei th discumfist wyth ane grislie wound lo doun bet slane defence also stout capitane vsence suld lak schame behald hys corp armour doi troianis bayith wythhald sal al suffir thaym doun ciete ding myscheif thare restis bot ane thyng sall wyth thys rycht hand hy confound schir drantes lynnage vnworthy sal euer ground behald se sic lak sall fle turnus gyf bak al sa wrechit thing de thay steruin men suld rather fle ye mane clepit goddis infernall beis dome saw neuir fane wald wit quhen quhat wise quhare aganis trespassit ocht haue wele quod tothi wald thou mercy cry mak amendis sall remit falt bot vthir wayis set sall full salt knawis thou mapheus wegious poete vnto virgillis lusty werk swete xiii buke ekit eneadane nathyng fane tothir thuelf thy toung translait new thay may red soung ouer albioun ile vulgare lede bot buke yit list ye tak na hede maister said wele quhat ye say thys case perdoun pray haue ony thing offendit bot rather haue tyme mispendit lang virgillis volume stare laid syde full mony graue mater wald wryte trety quhat abhominabyl thare studying thing vnproffitabyl thus sare dredis sall thole ane hete graue study haue lang forlete ya son quod wald thow eschape sa fayth sall thus part ga think assonyeis astart thame subdew troiane enee beseik pece amite rest quyet euermore thame thare landis moblis vthir gere eneas tho wyth plesand voce ful brade stand aboueexhortacion ecircumspects tymes cummyng mouing better aspectis happy begynning moue tak hand debait blyssit sterne brychteneas humanitye gentilnes swere neuer na oistis yit armour gla dly aganis batal mouyt bot cunstrenit furie kend wyth al force thaime call thare rerde bemyng quhare thay fare deray full hich dynnys p eneas glaid victory louit goddis sacrify thocht enee besy thochtfull curis constrenit twiching sepulturis folkis slane bering furth haue thay rent thare entraillys ful vnrude gan denude striping thare hydis syne hakkyng thame tailyeis sydis hayt flambis brycht thame laid furth thay yet wyne coupis glaid god bachus gyftis workar thare harmes syne hale remanent thare cumpany goddis thay name furth wyth hie vocis wyth loud cryis louit borne vp hie amang skyis thame al maist gratius eneas handis two custum towart heum gan vplyft arrace syne chyld ascaneus enbrace sayand ane wourdis al mycht thou son onlie chylde moist dere quham onlie restis thy faderis beleif quham throw sa mony laubouris myscheif caryit haueeneas co forteth son efter gret laubouris cachit ful mony gatis hard fortoun thrawart fatis lo rest quyet found ay lo rest maist desirit day mak end harmes distres paneful laubour passit expres lo acceptabil day euermore quhilk ful oft schawin quhen vntil hard bargane callit cum betid disposicioun goddis abufe derest chyld thy behufe morne sone aurora waxis rede ciete laurent rial stede sal send victor ouir hand maister mantene land eftir turnyd agane vnto folkis pepyl troiane boddum breist wele law wyth soft speche furth thir wourdis draw ye feris freyndis bald throw mony hard perrellis thik fald throw sa feil stormis baith land se hidder caryit thys coist wyth throw sa grete feruour batall stour doubil furie werefare armour sa feil wynterys blastis tempestis al wayis noyfum vnrestis horribil yit heuy woful hidduous wykkit vnhappy yit cruel myscheuus stade bettir hope returne myndis beis glade end al ennoy wo terme cuming sal thay stynt ho lyke desyrit best wyth latyne pepill ferme peace rest fal conione life vnite lauinia ilk blude quod quham defendit haue strang bargane troiane kyn wyth blude italiane samyn mydlyt spous hy sal yeild lynnage reyng perpetually ane thing fallowis freyndis dere besekyng requere bere myndis equale al anys commoun freyndis italianis fader law kyng latyne obeyis al wyth reuerence inclyne ane mychty scepture ryal weris mynd wyl perde bot batal douchty dedis armes wreik reuenge harmes lerne follow meik ye conterfete reuch piete eik quhat glore betid ful wele knaw bot heich heuin sterne law wytnessyng samyn wycht quhilk thou deliuerit fycht sa huge harmes mischeuys sere sal seis induce fer largeare rewardis mychtely rendir desiret wyth sic wourdis gan thame confortyng hys mynd ful mony sundry thyng chancis bypast rollyng fro thinkand brocht rest also na litil laubouris sturt panis wyth excedand luf troianis ful ardently flowis al ioye glade last dangeare ennoy huge heuy perrellis mony fald thay war eschapit brocht souir hald lyke quhen gredy glede hycht skummand vp turnus flycht wyth felloun fard watchand chykinnis lyte thare deith mannassand reddy smyt ereiseit foule thare moder tho ful smart hir pullettis wyth harmes hir hart affray gretely wofull chance gan rax hir self hir curage auance resist hir fa scharpand hir bill hale force mycht egar apoun hir aduersare baldlie fettis sche quhill last gif bak fle mekill pane verray violence scho constranis pik hence hir birdis syne clokand scho sekis raw affrayit doi thame samyn draw ennoyit greitlie hir childer dere quhen thay bene assemblit fere glaid scho wourdis thare mete scrap thay haif sa grete perrell eschaip nane vthir wise son anchises freyndlie wourdis thus amyd preis troyane myndis mese assuage man fulfillit wit vassalage driuand furth thare hartis flocht hald drede birnand heuy thocht wele thame likis thare ioy eis last fundin eftir sa grete diseis lait fore tedious suffir sustene ennoyus remember samin rehersing doi thame solace confort lykyng bot maist al grete enee quhilk excellent vertewe bounte excedit remanent ane fer way sa seil dangeris mony affray goddis power mychty maieste giftis grete offerandis wourschippis eik iupiter fader goddis king gan extoll maist souerane louing turnus folkis made sare regrete king latyne contempnis wrechit estate menetyme rutulianis yche one grete dede corp reuthfull wo begone thare duke turnus slane said within ciete laurentum bare mekill murnyng thare myndis emprent thare ene ane large schoure furth sent ofteris grete thocht heuin rane fer one brede dyd fyl eris twane kyng latyne cry womenting al irkyt nobill king breist self tyme ballance rolling mony selcouth diuers chance bot quhen hard thare loude womenting incressyng mare mare turnus ying wyth sa grisly ane wound throw gird sene mycht youling dyd complene mene bot thare lord rasis hys hand bedene byddis ceis thay hald thare mouthis still thare quhyngeing thare questing hys wyll refrenis clois gan thame withhald thir wyse thir rutulianis wald gan command debait thare voce ceice kingis mynd hald thare peace thus weping hart rute wele law king latyne begouth thir wourdis schaw grete motioun quhat altering vnstabill oft syis interchangeitking latynis piteful oration deploring inconstance toune rehersinge great alamitys incommodytyis kingdomes commoun w lthys variabill bene actis dedis men quod wyth grete trubil thou blynde desire insatiabil may tary mortal myndis quhiddir thou cary glory renowne lois vane conquest feil perrellis huge pane quhat condicioun quhat estate thou steris furth thir proude myndis infltate mony slichtis dissatis quent thou tursis mony wayis schent feill tormentis grete harme wikkitnes quhat labour curis falsched craftynes mony dartis feyll swerdis kene gif thou beheld thou afore thy ene allace thou swete venom schawis yit warldly wourschip dedelye bit allace sorowful reward al thing realme thame couatis ryng quhilk coistis oft na litil thyng allace heuy birding warldly gere neuir houre may suffir promyt thare possessoure rest pece sit allace miserabil chance hard estate kinglye honour sa infortunate chance kingis standis vnder lout mekil drede ay subiect dout thare estate decay suddanlie quiet eis tham deny turnus quhat aualit stere huge bargane fere al italie sic deray attanis perturbe strang eneadanis constrenyng tham hard batall tyl assay quhat aualis pray say til haue brokin violate schent haly promyssis bandis gent peace concord oblist sworne quhat thy mynd rent al torne sa mekyl impacience wyse thay list moue myne auise thy pepill bald strang sage bene discendit goddis lynnage command ioue god thunder ar hiddir carryit mak sic blunder wylfully motiue beliue enforcit thame ouer coist dryue forth brek band promyst douchter til gud son enee thy hand hard bargane ray stere quhen planely denyit moue sa grete folie dotage inuoluit thy mynde furie rage oft quhen thou auful batall wend amyd routis thy stede assend schynand armour arrayit al rycht assayit wythdraw fycht feil tymes defendit forbad go way thou begunnyng al efferit quhen thou wald depart amyd yet stoppit wicht sare hart bot al nathing mycht slyntin quhat haue sufferit syne standis wyth ciete wallis wytnessing fute hate wyth tenementis bigginnis half doun bet aud large feildis strowit quhite banis hale pissance italyanis al wastit distroyit thus alake huge slauchter mischeuus wraik al feyldis waxin rede browne mennis quelling grete occisioun lang abasit ferful quaking drede hard laubour quhilk extreme nede age sa oft vndertane sa feil dangeris quhare remede nane bot turnus thou lyggis dede quhare nobil renoune thy youth hede quhare thyne excellent hie curage quhydder went thy strenth vassillage quhare statly bewtie thy face quhare schinand fygure alace thy fare vysage quhidder gone thy pleasand forret schaiplie ene clere ha feil teris woful dolour smart sal thou turnus rendir dawnus hart large wepyng dule wa ouerfleyit sal al ciete ardea bot thay sal behald wyth siclake throw gyrd wyth schamful wound caucht bak na note na cowardice thy mynd thou degenerit kynd woful fader wil rede last sal solace thy dede al thocht thy harmes doth sore smert grete eneas swerd persit thy hart sayand thus teris piete chekis baith face ouer chargit syne turnand towart mekil rout reuthful corp ilk turnus stout bad turs away cary furth anone vntil faderis ciete wo begone commandit body cald al funeral pomp efter vsage ald p turnus corp tyll ardea quhilk suddand fyre vrynt doun schent rutilianis anone al ane rout dede corp slane lay stert gentil body stout youngkere thay haue addressit layd ane riche bere eik feil takynnis way reft troianis bargane bare thay baith helmis hors scheildis vthir gere swerdis githernis mony stalwart spere syne eftir wery cart furth went troiane slauchter hate blude al besprent furth haldis wepand metestus cartare craft lere ledand stede bedouin al swete thekis wet flotterand teris grete quhilk stede caryit turnus oft tofore victore hame grete triumph glore ful pompusite apoun ane vthir wyse efter feruent slauchter inemyis younder vtheris enuyroun beris thare armour scheildis turnit doun remanent syne hale barnage followis wepand knycht swane page haboundance mony trigland tere kyng latyne wyth al thame towart palace returne anone wyth mynd trublit trist wo begone sa excellent dede corp slane teris al samyn furth yettis euery ane bayth agit men matronus chylder lite ciete fillis wyth womenting site daunus fader wyse wyttand suld remane se sic dule wo son stalwart sprete yald maid end lattir bargane bald thus brocht toun dede feris wyth sic plente bitter wepand teris samyn tyme vthir diseis socht mekil said dolour hauy thocht latyne pepill war set battall troyanis doun bet turnus het recent dede wyth hys blude littyt ground al rede suddane fyre within wallis hie vmbeset halelye ardea ciete byggyngis hys fader wo begone brynt doun bet reky flambis schone returnis assis rede fyrie sparkis eueyry sted twynkland vpspringis sterne hye hope help may fundyn quhydder vnto goddis lyking fatis list schaw sum signe turnus deith horybyl battal slane quhen pepill saw remedy nane belife woful trublit citezanys thare drery breistis batand attanis gan fast bewale pietuous wepand face vnhappy chance wrechyt cais lang rabill woman matron al thare fors fled reuchfully attanis bald flambis bry blesis stout like emotis blak rout ythandlie labouris besy beildit vnder rute ane hye tre tyll ane clift thare bike duelling stede hyde thare lang sum werk wyuter brede gif betid thay fel ax smyte apoun treis schank theron byte crop weltis ground felloun rusche grisly sound thare smale cauernis brok rent spedely litill rout furth sprentis wyll rede fleand thay wat quhare tursing thare bi dingis affroi lye thare like house syde snale schakand hyr toppit schell hir tale fleand birnand hett schodois fele ane lang tyme gan wersil wrele thristand fast thare feit vnto wale yit hede force strenthis frawart feruent flambis fast drawis scho skaldis mony wrikis thrawis preissis eschew ferefull hete nane vthir wise sa feil perrellis grete thir wofull cietezanis gan thame self slyng ruschand trublit mynd tylane lyng bayth thare wist quhare away bot maist allace wellaway wyth reuthful vocis cryand heuin git kyng dawnus woful steuin tho amyd flambis furth wyth ardea foule quham heroun clepe betand hyr wyngis thay behald fle furth fyre heich vp bayth name takin ouer al quhare beris ciete ardea auld quhilom wyth wally towrys hye vntauld stude werelye wrocht strenth grete defence chaunget ful quyte gone hence wyth wyngys wyde fleand bayth vp doun bot ane foule ane ryal toun astonyst thys nyce new cace oft wounderus meruellis place quhilk semyt nothing lytyl thocht thay send war goddis hie pepil al coufusyt styl dyd stand thare burding thare schulderys cariand mouit nouther fute toung mouth kyng daunus thys affray vncouth ardent lufe smytyn desire thys cheif cyite destroyt brynt fyre hard dolour sorow smert haldys ful clois depe grauyng hys hart fra dawnus son turnus saw dede huge lamentatioun made stede amyd al thys deray grete effere fame dyseis forryder messingere come hurland huge murmure fast toun wyth large clamour fillis enuiroun thare myndis al howane dede corp new cumand hand mony wofull man turnus lifeles laid wyth mortall wound feild discomfist slane brocht ground euery wycht trublit wo begone blak blesand fyre brandis mony one gyse hynt thare handis schinand flambis glitteris landis thus thay recounterit thame cumand samin ionit cumpanyis fere quham al fast materis espye thay smate thare handis rasit vp ane cry sterne went thare wofull bere bot fra dawnus corp son dere beheld gan stynt arreist pase syne half dele enragit ane rase wyth huge sorow smyte ruschis amyd rout reuth se apoun turnus corp strekis doun enbrasing groufe ane swoun al fast speke micht furth brade wyth wourdis lamentabil thus wyse said son deseis thy fader thus drest febyl eilddawnus pitefull complaint sone turnus deith reuthfull rest bireft quhy thou allace sa grete perrillis insye case cachid thus driue quhidder quod vnder cruell bargane may se finale thus vincust ouercum quhare thy wourthy valour becum quhare thy douchty constance thy sprete caryit thus rest quyet notabyl honour louyng thy manhede glory thy ring grete wourschip thine empyre dere son quhilom thou bald syre bryngis thou v hame sikkin triumphe thys rest eis thou promis thy fader trist wo begone oft ouerset wyth inemyis mony one meith finale terme end al laubouris desirit wend wa wretchit wofull wycht haistely doun fallyng hicht thir slyddry warldly chancis drawis fast grete farde ouer rollit doun cast sa haistely bene thare fatis behald laitlie sa stout hie bald renownit grete honour quhilum al italie nane sa fare nane mare gracious til eloquence nane byg armes defence son quhare thy schinand lusty hede thy fresch figure visage quhite rede thy plesand bewtie thine ene tweyne thare fortoun ouertane thou promist thare labouris distres help support efter diseis solace nouthir thy promyssis fader sentence dissauit lo reuerence faderis italye se discrepance fully thir yeris thre blyssit peace son enioyis land certis fader vnderstand vnto e rnit heuinly hald hie thou promyst raise thy maist douchty enee merite aboue schynand skye place heuin deifye quhat thochtis doi rolling thy mynd sen elli doi verteuis theuis kynde thys reuthful eneas require aboue polis bricht rais syre fader tho men goddis gan ky venus child thare ther profound wourdis breist urth braid dere douchter citheriaiupiters answere venus said thou knawis stranglie mychty enee eneadanis menye ithandly vnirkit lufit haue sey landis catchit perrillis sere oft time eik hauand piete douchter meke luf thare diseis wo haue lo finalie also al thare harmes ennoy brocht til end made iuno ful wele kend becum freindly fauorabil likis forsoith al ferme stabil sentence promist complete quod quhen riall troiane duke enee amang heuinnis institute sall nowmer goddis cale thus grant gude willis perfay tharefore se thou change away gif thare ony mortal thing sine aboue al sterne thou bring sal also heich ony kin quhilk thare propir vertew list wyn perpetual louingisgod promotis euer verte u mene ded honorabil doth contemne wrechit warld vnstabil thame inlikewise aboue heuynnys hie sal place deify quod hoddis aboue alhale gaif thare consa riall iuno tyme present list contrary gan persuade ful euin bring grete enee vp til heuin freindle wourdis carpis thare venus slaid discendand throw theare socht vnto feildis laurentane nere quhare numetius throw fres riuere flewis se dikit redis growand hie quhare body hir son dere scho maid wesche vnder stremis cler al mortal corruptibill thyng gart awayeneas saul resa ed heuyn sine hir lyking recent happy saul hir hint sche bare vp aboue full hie vnto heuin quhare reuthful eneas amyd stremes chosin place quham famile kinred iuliane doith clepe cal amangis thame euery ane indigites quhilk al mekil say god induellare thare sudiornis aye remembrance ilk torne thay templis wourschip adorne finis conclusion werk al finist complete quhom iouis yre firis birnand hete trensche swerd sal defays doun thring lang proces age consumis al thing quhen vnknawin day sal addres quhilk one body power endis date mine vncertane eild bettir part sal vpbeild aboue sternis perpetually ring name remane emparing throw yle clepit albione red sal soung mony one thus vp pen instumentis ful yore virgillis post fix euermore neuir then sic materis discriue muse sal clene contemplatiue solitary doith bird cage sen fer worne childis age aud dayis nere passit half date nature suld granting wele wate thus sen feile doun sweyand ballance resigne vp younkeris obseruance wyl derek laubouris euer moir vnto commoun welth goddis gloir adew gud readeris god gif al gud nycht eftir deth grant v heueinly lycht space tyme date translatione buk compilet werk virgiliane apoun feist marye magdalane fra cristis birth date quha list ane thousand fyue hundreth threttene yere quhilk vthir grete occupacioun lay wusterit clois beside mony ane day neuirtheles quhidder serf thank wyte fra tyme tharto set pen wryte thocht god wate gif thare boundis werful wyde sic ines besyde apon wyse god list len grace compilyt auchtent monethes space set feil syith sic twa monethis fere wrate neuir ane wourd micht volume stere graue matteris grete sollicitude al sic laubour fer beside stude thus grete skant time besye cure made werk mare ubtil obscure plesand aucht quharof ye curtes reders perdoun ye writaris althe author forbid euerye man change ryme wourdis gentil redaris eik offendis volume beseik bot rede ele tak gud tent tyme ye nowthir mail mismeter ryme alter wourdis pray lo bew schirris haue gude day finis p ane exclamacion aganis detractouris uncurtase redaris bene ouer studious occasioun note spye faltis offensis volume vthir thrifty werkis throw depe fast porte merk endit lang disparit werk virgil volume lent souir raid ankerit werke dout na storme cabillis ar sa sterk haue eschapit ful mony perrellis went god belouit sic grace till v sent sen virgil beis wyde quhare latine soung thus laboure red vulgare toung bot quhat dangere ocht compile allace herand thir detractouris till euery place euer thay rede werk biddis birn buke sum bene sa frawart malice wangrace quhat wele sayd thay loif worth ane ace bot castis thame euir spy falt cruke al thay fynd hiddillis hirne nuke thay blaw sayand euery mannis face lo failyeis lo lei luke bot gif le lat virgill iudge werk patent may haue na refuge thareby go faltis one one wounder volume sa huge quhay mycht perfectly al hie termes luge barbare langage thame deulie expone bot wele wate sentence wantis none quha bettir lat se quhare foruayit begyn new al thing gude vnassayit f r ethar quha list syt doun mote ane vthir sayaris faltis spye note offence falt thame self wyte bot chyde sum bene birnand hote bald thay thare pece word wald skald thare throte sic custom iangil bakbite bot thay schent sum thay suld birst site say quhen al thare rerd roung wicht mon speik hald toung go vulgare virgil euery churliche wycht say auow thou art translatit richt beseik al nobillis correct amend beis effrait cum prisaris sicht nedis eschame thy licht haif brocht thy purpois gude end sal thou euery gentil ot kend vnletteryt folk red hicht erst bot clerkis comprehend finis knaw name translator gaw vnbrokin mydlit wine dow ioned glas richt ane lyne quha knawis translatouris name seik forther lo wyth lytil pyne spye leile vers men clepis sa hame finis
